In the Summer Departure calendar, at the end of the first year of the imperial reign, snow fell in the imperial capital of humankind. But winter always came late to Seven Blood Eyes, and besides, the climate was temperate, so the most that happened was that it rained. That was true even at the end of the year.

The rain that fell covered the Port District. From a distance, everything looked hazy. The crowds on the street and the ships coming in and out of the harbors created a beautiful scene. The pitter-patter of the rain on oilskin umbrellas was as gentle as the sounds of nature, tugging on the heartstrings of the people. It was like an affectionate confession of the sky to the earth, or the clouds expressing deep attachment to all the living things below.

Xu Qing walked through the rhythmic rain until he found Harbor 176. There, squatting in the eaves of a big warehouse was Zhang San, wearing the same style of clothing he had always worn. And just like always, he was smoking a pipe.

There was a familiar face squatting next to him. It was Erniu, who was wringing out his soaking fur all while talking nonstop.

Upon spotting Xu Qing, Erniu waved and shouted a greeting. Meanwhile, Zhang San’s eyes lit up. Shooting to his feet, he put his pipe away and rubbed his hands together in anticipation, all while flashing a silly smile. That smile came instinctively to Zhang San, either when he was around old friends or important people.

Nowadays, Xu Qing counted as a familiar face to Zhang San, but at the same time, was something of a stranger. He was a familiar face because of their times together in the past. But he was a stranger because, nowadays, his cultivation base and status had reached an astonishing level.

“Xu...” he began hesitantly, unsure of exactly how to address Xu Qing.

“Elder Brother Zhang San,” Xu Qing interrupted with a smile before Zhang San could decide which form of address to settle on. And with that, he squatted down beneath the eaves. It was just like the time years ago when Erniu introduced Xu Qing to Zhang San.[1]

Zhang San grinned.

Erniu, meanwhile, looked off into the distance for something before snorting coldly and grumbling, “So, that damned old bird Huang Yan isn’t with you? Let me tell you, little Ah Qing, that crappy bird is one foul fowl!” freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing thought for a moment. “Eldest Brother,” he said quietly, “given Huang Yan’s cultivation, even though he’s not right here, he can probably still hear everything you say.”

Erniu’s eyes widened into a glare, and he loudly said, “This is Seven Blood Eyes! My Junior Sister is here! My Master is here! I’m the Grand Highness of Seventh Peak! You think I’m scared of some dumb bird?”

It was hard to say if it was a coincidence or not, but the moment the words left Erniu’s mouth, thunder crashed deafeningly in the sky.

Erniu’s face became a mask of abject terror.

Zhang San could feel a headache coming on already. Erniu had returned earlier that morning, and from the moment he had squatted down until now, he had been complaining about Huang Yan nonstop.... Zhang San obviously didn’t want to offend either Erniu or Huang Yan, so the moment Xu Qing arrived, he quickly changed the conversation topic.

“Xu Qing,” he said, “I heard you and the Captain went to the outer sea!”

Xu Qing nodded. Waving his hand, he produced the crumbled remains of his dreadnaught, which dropped down with a thump into the courtyard outside the warehouse. It took up about ninety percent of the entire courtyard. Though the dreadnaught had been mostly destroyed, it still pulsed with the aura of a godly entity, and was also full of outer sea mutagen. Combined, it created a vicious and evil black mist that spread out rapidly. As the rain fell, the black mist devoured it and expanded. Wherever it went, everything became as dark as night.

Zhang San was shaken to the core.

Xu Qing waved his hand, which dispelled the black mist and cleared it from the area as thoroughly as if it had been erased.

“Elder Brother Zhang San, my dreadnaught broke down. Do you think you could come up with a plan for how to fix it?”

Xu Qing was a big admirer of Zhang San’s work. From his first dharmaboat until now, he had always relied on Zhang San. Although Zhang San’s cultivation base was now far too low to be of much help, his deep understanding of dharmaboats would be enough to come up with a good plan.

Zhang San looked at the dreadnaught and its broken-down state, and he nearly gasped. “It looks almost like something opened its mouth and took a big bite out of it....”

Xu Qing nodded.

Erniu cleared his throat. “You’re absolutely right about that, Sansan. It did get bitten by a huge creature. And then, little Ah Qing and I were swallowed up along with the dreadnaught. Yep. It was all because I summoned the thing.”

Erniu looked very proud of himself when he offered the explanation.

When Xu Qing saw how pleased Erniu looked, he was struck somewhat speechless. That said, he had to admit that what Erniu said was fairly close to the truth.

Zhang San’s eyes went wide, and a moment later, he shook his head. Now that he thought about it, he actually didn’t want to know too much about what Xu Qing and Erniu had been up to. There were some things that, the more you knew about them, the more danger you were in.

My weak little body is not made for things like that.

Zhang San was very pleased with his high standing in Seven Blood Eyes. He had his own harbor, he had more spirit stones than he could spend, and he had a lot of daoist partners. There were very few people who would dare to offend him. Things had been very good lately. The last thing he wanted to do was start courting death.

Not responding to what Erniu had just said, Zhang San walked over to the dreadnaught and started inspecting it. Shortly after, he was back under the eaves. Taking out his pipe, he looked at Xu Qing and sighed.

“It’s ruined. You might as well just get rid of it. The materials are too damaged. Sorry, Xu Qing. I can’t really help you.”

Xu Qing looked at the broken-down dreadnaught for a moment. “Elder Brother Zhang San, can’t you just make a new one?”

Zhang San shook his head. “Given your cultivation base, an ordinary dreadnaught wouldn’t be of much use. And a special dreadnaught requires extremely high-quality material. But if the materials are too high-level, then I wouldn’t be able to do anything with them... that is, unless you could arrange for help. And you would need to chip in some help as well. Although, that’s really secondary to the main issue.

“Ultimately, the materials are key. An ordinary godly entity isn’t going to cut it at this point. You would need the flesh of a high-level god. Now, maybe you have that already, but in addition, you would need some extremely powerful item to serve as the foundation. Unfortunately, I can’t think of anything that would be able to bear the weight of the flesh of a god.”

Zhang San seemed to be at a loss.

Off to the side, Erniu’s eyes lit up. “Hey, what about that mountain that used to be a holy land? Little Ah Qing, what do you say we write a letter to the empress demanding it back? We can sign it in the name of our Master!”

Zhang San immediately nodded. Though he hadn’t actually seen that mountain, based on his understanding, using a holy land for materials would definitely suffice.

After a bit of thought, Xu Qing put away the dreadnaught, then flicked his sleeve to produce a chunk of flesh. It was from Floating Fiend. Xu Qing reached out and squeezed the flesh with his hand, crushing it so that a stream of gray light flew out, which turned into a dilapidated pagoda right in the middle of the courtyard. It was the very same mysterious pagoda that Xu Qing had discovered on the seafloor and used as a hiding place. Floating Fiend discovered it and absorbed it into his own flesh. Later, when Xu Qing was freed by Yu Liuchen, he had assimilated Floating Fiend’s flesh, and thus acquired the pagoda. Given Xu Qing’s current level of strength, he couldn’t absorb the pagoda, so it made sense to leave it with Floating Fiend’s flesh.

After taking it out, Xu Qing looked at Zhang San. “What about this thing?”

Before Zhang San could answer, Erniu’s eyes locked onto the pagoda as if in excitement. He could sense a terrifying aura in the pagoda, and he could also see the aura of the sageheaven god vine.

“That thing is incredible!” he blurted, and all of a sudden, his sageheaven god vine shot out and wrapped around the pagoda, all while emitting excited fluctuations.

Xu Qing’s god vine did the same. It quickly formed a resonance with Erniu’s vine, and an instant later, starlight glittered out from the two of them. That, in turn, affected the pagoda, which also started to shine with starlight.

Zhang San had a very serious expression on his face as he observed what was happening. The more he observed, the more shocked he was. And then, with the approval of Xu Qing and the help of the vines, he passed through the bubble and entered the pagoda.

When he came back out a short time later, he looked shaken, but his eyes were shining.

“I can’t identify the material it’s constructed from, but it doesn’t look like a postheaven item. In all likelihood, it’s a naturally-occurring material! The aura is chaotic and primeval, and also incredibly ancient. It seems to have the same origin as those two vines of yours.... This is definitely an incredible item. Something unique and one-of-a-kind. I’m going to need to study it more to determine further details.”

Zhang San inhaled deeply and looked at Xu Qing. “Xu Qing, my intuition is telling me that if we had a way to refine that thing and turn it into a dreadnaught... it would be absolutely stupefying. But even if we can’t refine it, using it as a reference point will be very beneficial. As for your vine... well I need to put some thought into the whole matter. Incidentally, we’re going to need help from the exalted Flame Phoenix.”

Xu Qing quickly took out a transmission jade slip and sent a message to Huang Yan.

Shortly after, as Erniu grumbled inwardly, Huang Yan arrived. When the two of them saw each other, they exchanged nothing but sharp glares.

Xu Qing quickly hurried in between them, all while Zhang San started explaining the situation with Xu Qing’s dreadnaught.

After Huang Yan heard the explanation, he looked at the pagoda for a moment and then nodded. “You need some flame? No problem.”

Zhang San was about to say ‘yes’ when Erniu cleared his throat.

“San,” Erniu said, “if you’re planning to build a new dreadnaught for little Ah Qing, wouldn’t it help to have the power of frigid coldness?”

Seeing the look in Erniu’s eyes caused Zhang San to hesitate. In the end, he could only agree.

Erniu and Huang Yan continued to glare at each other for a while until Zhang San and Xu Qing managed to smooth things out between them. Then they started refining the pagoda.

Making a new dreadnaught for Xu Qing was one of the most important things for Seven Blood Eyes at the moment. Since Zhang San couldn’t do it alone, Second Elder Sister ordered all of the equipment forgers in the sect to hurry over and help.

Eventually, they decided to use an open area in a forbidden ground as the construction yard. In that spot, hundreds of thousands of cultivators started working on Xu Qing’s dreadnaught.

As the work progressed, Xu Qing himself didn’t need to do much personally. In most cases, he could just leave his god vine behind.

As a result, Xu Qing ended up having a lot of free time. He spent time helping the Mute with his cultivation base. He also gave some dao sermons in Seven Blood Eyes, in which he explained matters of personal cultivation enlightenment. Not only did he provide general instructions to the disciples but he also gave individualized help, enabling specific disciples to deal with questions and obstacles.

A month passed.

On one particular morning, Xu Qing was seated cross-legged in his mansion grotto when he received a voice message from Zhang San.

“Xu Qing, your dreadnaught is just about done. Everything went smoothly. You... should just come see it for yourself.”

Xu Qing rose and walked out of his mansion grotto. As he was about to leave to meet Zhang San, he suddenly sensed something. Looking up into the canopy of heaven, he smiled.

Up above, he saw a prismatic beam of light shooting toward the Seventh Peak.

There were two people within the beam of light. One was middle-aged, the other was a young woman. The middle-aged man was Grandpa Ninth, while the young woman... was Ling’er.

“Big Bro Xu Qing,” Ling’er said in a cheerful and lighthearted voice that sounded like the chime of silver bells.

1. Erniu took Xu Qing to meet Zhang San in chapter 55. ☜

At Seven Blood Eyes, dawn was the purest and most tranquil part of the day. The first stream of light that came from the east brought golden color with it, and it shone around the approaching female figure.

She wore a long white gown that was the perfect complement to her beauty. The rising sun behind her made her skin seem extraordinarily fair, like exquisite porcelain. She seemed clean, pure, and free of all worldly defilements. She was slender and elegant, like a supple willow tree. Her long, straight nose, rosy lips, and beautiful smile were as warm and gorgeous as the sunrise. As she approached, her long hair swayed behind her in a mysterious, intoxicating rhythm. Especially noteworthy were her eyes, which glittered like gemstones, and brimmed with pure, joyous light. She was like a butterfly slowly stretching its wings, with charm and loveliness that was almost palpable.

Ling’er missed Xu Qing so much that she had finally come to see him at the Seventh Peak. When she threw herself into his arms and breathed in his scent, her eyes overflowed with tears.

“Big Bro Xu Qing....”

Endless longing and worry had filled her, as well as an ineffable indecision, and all of that came out in the words she spoke.

A host of memories filled Xu Qing’s heart and mind when he heard her speak. He gently lifted his hand and stroked her hair.

“Why are you crying?” he asked softly.

“I don’t know.... I just feel like I’ve lost you, Big Bro Xu Qing.” She looked up at him.

He was quiet for a moment, and then he laughed softly. “Impossible.”

“Really?”

“Really,” he said with a nod.

Ling’er laughed through her tears.

Xu Qing looked up at Grandpa Ninth, who had not descended from the dome of heaven. Grandpa Ninth closed his eyes, settled down cross-legged in midair, and started meditating.

After some thought, Xu Qing decided not to go to the forbidden ground to check on his dreadnaught. Instead, he sat down outside of his mansion grotto and told Ling’er the story of everything that happened after he left the Moonrite Region.

Ling’er listened intently to all the twists and turns, and her emotions rose and fell as he went through the different parts of the story. When she heard the parts where Xu Qing was in danger, she got nervous. When she heard the parts when he won great victories, she got happy. Gradually, her worries faded away, and she became immersed in Xu Qing’s world.

As he recounted his tale, that feeling of indecision within her gradually faded away. It was replaced by a smile, and then, with a love of life and a hope for what was to come in the future. It was something unique to young women. It was the liveliness and excitement of youth, the pure manifestation of a girl’s dreams. She suddenly seemed like a flower blooming in spring, or the sunlight in summer, or the leaves falling in autumn, or the snowflakes in winter.

When Xu Qing told the parts of his story that touched on Erniu, she laughed and laughed, sounding like a gentle stream flowing through a mountain.

Time passed.

As Xu Qing spoke, the sky turned blue, and white clouds drifted overhead. Just like Grandpa Ninth had, they looked down calmly at what was happening on the Seventh Peak. Combined with the shining sun, it looked like a simple but elegant painting.

Eventually, Ling’er yawned. Then her eyes fluttered closed, and she fell asleep.

Xu Qing gently stroked her head to make sure she was in a deep slumber. Then, he looked up at Grandpa Ninth with a very serious expression. Clasping hands, he bowed.

“Grandpa Ninth, what’s going on with Ling’er?”

Grandpa Ninth opened his eyes and looked down. “Last month, when she reached the great circle of Nascent Soul, her bloodline curse started flaring up again. The imperial energy you left for her ran out.”

Xu Qing looked down at the sleeping Ling’er. Earlier, he had sensed the fluctuations indicating her cultivation base was unstable.

Face expressionless, Grandpa Ninth continued, “I brought her here to see you because I want you to come with me to see Emperor Ancient Spirit. My plan is to force him to give up the rest of his imperial energy. All of it. That said, there’s no need to rush. Ling’er isn’t in any immediate danger.”

Xu Qing nodded. Going to see Emperor Ancient Spirit would involve traveling to the Wood Spirits in Sea-Sealing County.

Although he once had a command medallion that would take him directly to Emperor Ancient Spirit, after he was resurrected in South Phoenix, that medallion stopped working. Xu Qing had tried using it when he was being chased by Floating Fiend, only for it to fail.

“Very well, Senior. Please wait just a moment.”

Xu Qing waved his hand, sending out a gentle force that helped suppress the instability in Ling’er’s cultivation base. Then he floated up into the air before vanishing. When he reappeared, he was in the forbidden ground where his dreadnaught was being made.

A huge open space had been prepared there. As soon as Xu Qing appeared, he saw the hundreds of thousands of cultivators under the command of Zhang San, making the final inspection of the dreadnaught.

Huang Yan and Erniu were meditating at opposite ends of the open area.

Astonishingly, the object that Zhang San and the hundreds of thousands of Seven Blood Eyes disciples were inspecting was a massive nine-floor pagoda that rose high into the sky. It rotated slowly, glowing with majestic light, and pulsing with an ancient aura. All it took was a single glance to realize that it was extraordinary. The sageheaven god vine coiled around it, casting its own starlight into the glow of the pagoda.

Close examination would reveal that the nine-floor pagoda wasn’t actually a unified structure. It had been pieced together. The bottom level was made from the earliest version of the dilapidated pagoda. The eight floors above it had apparently been added on to provide a higher level of control.

When Zhang San spotted Xu Qing, he looked at him and grinned. “What do you think, Xu Qing? Happy? That dilapidated pagoda of yours was very, very difficult to refine. Thankfully, the exalted Huang Yan’s flame was extraordinary, and made it possible to refine it. When you add in the Captain’s marvelous abilities, we were able to add eight floors to the pagoda.

“Now, you should be able to directly control it! This dreadnaught won’t just work in the Forbidden Sea. You should be able to use it... in the starry sky! This is a dreadnaught designed to traverse the stars!

“It doesn’t just have materials from godly entities. The Captain and the exalted Huang Yan also added in the flesh of gods. It’s completely astonishing, and at the same time, can be released and collected back at will.

“What’s more, given how much I’m familiar with your practice of blowing up your ships, I didn’t bother building in divine abilities and magical techniques. Instead, I focused everything on durability. This dreadnaught... can also be used as a weapon to bash enemies over the head! And of course, in terms of speed and strength, it surpasses your previous dreadnaught by a longshot!”

Zhang San kept talking louder and louder in his excitement. Over the last month, he had been the one orchestrating the plan to build the dreadnaught. He had poured blood, sweat, and tears into the project, and had pushed his skill and imagination to the limit. As far as he was concerned, this was the best work he had done in his entire life.

“Now you just need to awaken your god vine! The vine is the spirit automaton of the dreadnaught. During the process of refining the pagoda, it became inextricably linked to it. Right now, it’s asleep. With it as the spirit automaton, you can control the pagoda perfectly! By the way, I kept the defensive bubble that surrounded the pagoda.”

Zhang San hurried to Xu Qing’s side looking very excited, and all the while trying to hide his exhaustion. However, his bloodshot eyes made it obvious how tired he was.

Xu Qing was moved. Taking a deep breath, he clasped hands and bowed to Zhang San. Then he bowed to the hundreds of thousands of cultivators in the area. Finally, he waved his hand in the direction of the pagoda.

As his divine will streamed out, the sageheaven god vine coiled around the pagoda twitched. Then it slowly woke up and started moving around the pagoda. Starlight glittered resplendently as the sageheaven god vine carried the pagoda right toward Xu Qing. Along the way, both the vine and the pagoda shrank down until they landed on Xu Qing’s palm, hardly more than an inch tall.

Xu Qing checked it with divine will, then retracted his divine will. Around that time, Erniu and Huang Yan emerged from meditation. Both of them looked very pleased. But then they noticed each other. Glaring at each other, they seemed just on the verge of bickering when Xu Qing cleared his throat.

“Huang Yan, I have a matter to attend to. I need to leave South Phoenix.”

Huang Yan opened his mouth to say something, but before he could, Erniu jumped up, rushed over to Xu Qing, and laughed heartily.

“We’re finally leaving? Alright, let’s hurry up and get out of here! Having to deal with this birdman on a daily basis is really getting old. It’s high time I un-bird-en myself, I can tell you that!”

Xu Qing clasped hands to Huang Yan. There wasn’t a need for any parting words. With another bow to everyone else present, he threw the pagoda into the air. In accordance with his thoughts, it grew to a height of 300 meters tall, and also emanated a seven-colored glow. A magnificent will spread out in all directions as Xu Qing stepped onto the pagoda. Erniu followed, and as his sageheaven god vine glittered with starlight, he was admitted. Next, rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth as the pagoda pierced through the void and disappeared.

When it reappeared, it was above the Seventh Peak in Seven Blood Eyes. There, the pagoda’s main doors opened, and the sleeping Ling’er floated up and into the pagoda. Grandpa Ninth also stepped inside. He looked around, and his eyes flashed with amazement.

“This thing is incredible!”

Hearing that, Erniu laughed proudly. “I refined it!”

Grandpa Ninth ignored him.

Xu Qing bolstered Ling’er again, slowing down the changes to her cultivation base. Then he sent more divine will into the pagoda. As all the Seven Blood Eyes disciples watched, the pagoda flared with seven-colored light. Dazzling brightness spread for 5,000 kilometers, and then the pagoda vanished.

It moved with shocking speed out over the Forbidden Sea. Immense waves swept out over the water as the pagoda shot toward Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. Wherever it passed, countless sea beasts sensed the pressure of the pagoda’s aura, and they trembled.

***

In Emperor-Receiving Prefecture, the Swordsage Court grand elder in charge of the prefecture was flying over the Supreme Arbiter Salvation Mountains. After passing the Everlasting Immortal Profundity River, he appeared outside the Spiritsound forbidden ground.[1]

Looking into the forbidden ground, he said, “Three days ago, a swordsage from my Swordsage Court was out on a mission when she encountered the wanted cultivator Li Zimei from the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. After chasing her into the forbidden region, they both disappeared.[2]

“Lord Spiritsound, things are different in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture, Sea-Sealing County, and the Holytide Region in general, compared to the last time you awoke! Therefore, I’m here on orders from the Swordsage Palace in Sea-Sealing County, demanding that you release these people from your forbidden ground!”

Natural sounds erupted from the Spiritsound forbidden ground, turning into sounds of death that swept out in all directions. The shocking power of the sound caused the entire forbidden ground to tremble. Waves broke out on the surface of the Everlasting Immortal Profundity River, all while a sinister voice spoke from inside the forbidden ground.

“Screw off!”

The Swordsage Court grand elder was shaken deeply as he fell back 300 meters. Face pale and eyes sharp, he looked at the forbidden ground. “That swordsage was named Qing Qiu, and she was a close childhood friend of Region Lord Xu Qing. If you insist on being stubborn, you’ll bring catastrophe down on your own head. And now, you can’t claim that I didn’t warn you!”[3]

1. The Spiritsound forbidden ground was first mentioned in chapter 269. More details about it were explained in chapter 347. ☜

2. Li Zimei was introduced by name in chapter 49. She was last mentioned in chapter 660, and last appeared onscreen in chapter 287. ☜

3. Qing Qiu was first introduced by name in chapter 355, although she had appeared onscreen before that. She first showed up as an adult in chapter 335, but her first actual appearance onscreen was in chapter 6. She appeared in far too many chapters to include references. The last chapter in which she appeared onscreen was chapter 543, though she was mentioned in a few chapters after that. ☜

Deathblade's Thoughts

By this point in the novel, the author has seemingly forgotten his original designations for the Swordsage Court, Palace, and Division. Because of that, this chapter is a bit confusing when you read it in Chinese. I’ve edited the text here (as well as in subsequent chapters) so that the continuity is maintained.

A classified report was sent from the Swordsage Court in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture all the way to the Swordsage Palace in Sea-Sealing County! The Swordsage Palace received the report and immediately assigned a powerful expert to Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. The report was also sent to Xu Qing.

“Twenty days ago, a sect by the name of the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture issued an arrest warrant for a disciple named Li Zimei. The entire prefecture was notified that she had been bedeviled and was no longer human. She had killed fellow disciples in the most brutal manner. She fled, and the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society pursued her for ten days. Of the dozens of teams the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society sent after her, more than half were wiped out.

“During the process, she encountered Swordsage Qing Qiu from the Swordsage Court in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. For some unknown reason, the two of them started fighting, and then ended up disappearing into the Spiritsound forbidden ground.”

***

The Sageheaven Pagoda that Seven Blood Eyes had mobilized to create was able to cross the Forbidden Sea in only a day. Upon arriving in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture, Xu Qing was seated cross-legged in the pagoda when he received the classified report from the Swordsage Palace.

“Qing Qiu...” he murmured.

As he pulled his divine will out of the jade slip, he thought back to the scavenger basecamp, and the little girl that had later come to be a fellow swordsage. He would never be able to forget her strong determination.

The other name also struck a chord in him. She was someone he had come to know in Seven Blood Eyes, and she was similar to Qing Qiu in some ways. Though she had a timid personality, her sense of pride was sky-high. Later, she ended up being taken into the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. The last time Xu Qing remembered seeing her was on the Everlasting Immortal Profundity River. Back then, Li Zimei had left him a letter explaining that she was going to accept a legacy. Xu Qing eventually moved on to Sea-Sealing County, and the two of them lost touch.

Never could he have imagined that the next time he heard about either of them, it would be in a situation like this.

“Spiritsound forbidden ground....” Xu Qing looked down at Ling’er sleeping and mulled the matter over.

“Have something to take care of?” asked Grandpa Ninth, who was standing off to the side.

Xu Qing turned to look at him. “I received a classified report from the Swordsage Palace. Two old friends of mine went missing in the Spiritsound forbidden ground.”

Grandpa Ninth looked at Ling’er. Before he could say anything, Erniu interjected, “Spiritsound? That craphole of a forbidden ground? Raze it to the ground, I say! Who went missing there?”

“Qing Qiu,” Xu Qing replied calmly.

Erniu thought about it for a moment, and then smiled enigmatically. “Qing Qiu? The same one who tried to steal our loot on the Nethersprite heist, and then later became a swordsage? The same chick who went to the Holytide Region with us? Right, I remember. She loved that scythe of hers. It had a spirit automaton, right? And I remember she had some kind of blood will domain. That girl was a real freak of nature! Who’s the other one?”

“Li Zimei,” Xu Qing replied.

“Li Zimei? Who? That’s not ringing a bell.” Erniu scoured his memories but couldn’t recall who Li Zimei was. After all, whether it was her time in Seven Blood Eyes or the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society, he had never had any dealings with her.

Meanwhile, Grandpa Ninth looked away from the sleeping Ling’er. “Dealing with one forbidden ground shouldn’t waste too much time. Go if you want.”

Xu Qing nodded, then sent the Sageheaven Pagoda flying over the Eight Sect Coalition and toward the mountain range beyond it. The mountain range was made of undulating black mountains, some of which were very tall, some of which weren’t. They seemed to stretch on endlessly into the depths of Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. Altogether, they resembled the corpse of some massive beast, dark and hazy as if filled with sinister evil. The place overflowed with vile trees and grues.

These were the Emperor-Receiving Prefecture’s Supreme Arbiter Salvation Mountains! In the spot where the mountains approached the sea, the Eight Sect Coalition had made their headquarters. At the other end of the mountains in the Emperor-Receiving Prefecture was the notorious Three-Spirits Dao-Suppressing Mountain.

After Xu Qing’s pagoda sped into the airspace over the Supreme Arbiter Salvation Mountains, it slowed to a halt.

In the direction of the Three-Spirits Dao-Suppressing Mountain, two figures appeared, one short and one tall. Both were looking in the direction of the pagoda.

The tall one was incredibly skinny, almost to the point of looking skeletal. The only thing about him that wasn’t incredibly bony was his back, which was hunched and looked almost like a small mountain. That ‘mountain’ was actually some sort of cancerous growth, covered with horrid, greenish-red veins. It almost looked like that growth had absorbed all of the other flesh and blood on his body.

The person next to him was actually a dwarf.

The dwarf wore a black robe and had tiny, beady eyes along with a bulging forehead. He had two very long eyebrows that drooped down to his cheeks. He had a recessed chin, and a mustache shaped roughly like the character 八, with the ends curled up so they resembled tusks. He was surrounded by a black cloud that looked like it was formed from countless shrieking centipedes.

Obviously, the arrival of the Sageheaven Pagoda, and the pressure it emanated, had shaken these two individuals to the core.

Xu Qing emerged from the pagoda and looked at them. The two enormous figures breathed sighs of relief. Eyes shining, they ducked their heads down and bowed at the waist to Xu Qing.

They were none other than the heavenly soul Sporelight and the earthly soul Sunslaughter! Years ago, Xu Qing had relied on their help to deal with Forbidden by the Zombie, in exchange for a promise to help them break free from the shackles of the Ghost Emperor, and thus earn freedom.[1]

“I don’t break my promises,” Xu Qing said in a low voice. “Once I reach Smoldering God, I’ll live up to my word.”

When Sporelight and Sunslaughter heard that, it was very thought-provoking to them. Although they hadn’t personally witnessed Xu Qing’s rise to prominence, they had been there for two important events along the way.

The first was when the two thieves Xu Qing and Erniu broke in and stole Nethersprite’s clothes. Back then, any one of the three souls had a cultivation base so powerful they could have killed the two with the wave of a hand.

The second was when Xu Qing and Erniu came with Qingqin and asked the heavenly soul and earthly soul for help. At that time, Xu Qing was already showing he had the potential to rise to prominence. Therefore, Sporelight decided to casually place a game piece into play. As far as Sporelight was concerned, that random game piece wasn’t really very important. And he wasn’t very certain that anything would come from making that move.

Neither of them could have guessed that Xu Qing would perform so dramatically, that he would go to Sea-Sealing, and Moonrite, and Holytide, and even the imperial capital.... In fact, he was now a region lord of two regions, plus the tutor to the crown prince, the Grand Darkheaven of the Firemoons, and a person whose name had shaken the entire east of Revered Ancient. And he had single-handedly brought down an entire holy land.

Combined, that surpassed anything they could have imagined. Xu Qing had reached the point where they had to struggle just to lift their heads high enough to see him. Today... was their third encounter.

Keeping their heads down, they bowed respectfully. That casually placed game piece had really turned into good fortune.

Xu Qing looked at the two souls but said nothing further. He went back into the pagoda, which shone with bright light that drove away the darkness of the Supreme Arbiter Salvation Mountains. Surrounded by brightness, the pagoda shot off into the distance.

Sometime later, Sporelight and Sunslaughter looked up, their hearts pounding.

“In all the history of Revered Ancient,” Sporelight murmured, “how many chosen have there been who could surpass him?”

***

Heaven and earth grew dim as evening fell. As the afterglow of sunset began to fade, Xu Qing spotted a great river ahead of the Sageheaven Pagoda.

Emperor-Receiving Prefecture had a famous mountain range and a famous river. The mountain range was the Supreme Arbiter Salvation Mountains. The river was the Everlasting Immortal Profundity River.

The majestic, ancient river was as wide as a sea, and its waters rushed turbulently, creating a constant crashing sound as the waves frothed. The immortal energy was strong.

It entered the prefecture from the outside, passing through the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society in the east of Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. It passed through the Supreme Arbiter Salvation Mountains, ultimately entering the Spiritsound forbidden ground, before eventually reaching the sea in the distant west. At the spot where the river and the mountains intersected, the Sageheaven Pagoda shot through the air, following the river... to the Spiritsound forbidden ground.

Spiritsound split the Everlasting Immortal Profundity River into two parts.

Before reaching the forbidden ground, the water rushed along filled with life and immortal energy, which helped countless living beings to cleanse themselves of mutagen. But after it entered the forbidden ground, the life in the water vanished, and it turned black and murky. The mutagen of the forbidden ground invaded it. Infected it.

However, there is karma in all things, and counterparts in everything. For years on end, water full of immortal energy had poured into the forbidden ground. Though that water ended up polluted, the reason was that it was taking mutagen out of the forbidden ground. And the result was that, despite how much time had passed, the Spiritsound forbidden ground hadn’t expanded its borders.

Though it was officially a forbidden ground, it wasn’t close to being on the same level as Forbidden by the Zombie. Nor could it compare to the forbidden ground in South Phoenix.

The lord of this forbidden ground, who was sometimes referred to as Emperor Spiritsound, and sometimes as Lord Spiritsound, occasionally awoke. But when that happened, the combined forces of Emperor-Receiving Prefecture would work together to create a sealing mark to contain him. After all, if the emperor of a forbidden ground ended up dying, as long as the forbidden ground itself remained, a new emperor would eventually arise. And as far as Emperor-Receiving Prefecture was concerned, it made a lot more sense to just keep dealing with an entity they knew, rather than have to handle an unfamiliar entity. Thus, the two parties had existed for a long time without very much friction.

But today, catastrophe loomed over the Spiritsound forbidden ground. As the haze of evening spread out in heaven and earth, a nine-floor pagoda shining with seven-colored light appeared. It pulsed with a chaotic, primeval aura, and emanated terrifying pressure as it came to hover above the forbidden ground.

As soon as it arrived, Xu Qing stepped out of the pagoda and hovered in the air.

The afterglow of sunset would make it hard to see most things, but it didn’t obscure Xu Qing at all. He stood tall and straight, his eyes glittering profoundly.

“The lord of this forbidden ground will come out immediately to see me.”

In response to his words, countless sounds erupted from the forbidden ground.... They included the sound of the wind, the sound of rustling leaves, the sound of water dripping, and the sound of swamp lands stirring.... Countless sounds, including those of innumerable living beings and everything else that existed in the forbidden ground, erupted uncontrollably. Every single one of those sounds existed within Xu Qing’s authority of sound. Every movement was within his god perception.

As of this moment, all of those sounds didn’t belong to the forbidden ground. They belonged to Xu Qing! As they converged, they became part of the words he had spoken, causing heaven to shake and the earth to quake.

When facing the authority of sound, this forbidden ground had no choice but to acknowledge allegiance.

Countless images and perceptions appeared to Xu Qing. He saw everything, including... Li Zimei in the depths of the forbidden ground. She was trapped inside of a gruish tree. Her long hair was draped around her, and her eyes were closed, but her expression was fierce, and she pulsed with a baleful aura. Her aura was very gruish, and seemed to be on the verge of fusing with the forbidden ground around her.

It was at that exact same moment that the entire forbidden ground came to be under Xu Qing’s control....

The only part of Li Zimei that was visible was her head. Suddenly, her eyes opened, and they shone with a fiendish, bloody glow. In the past, her face had been delicate and pretty. But now it was ferocious, covered with black veins that formed the image of a ghost face.

The sight of it caused Xu Qing to sigh inwardly. He suddenly thought back to the letter Li Zimei had left for him when they parted ways last.

The past was now vividly in mind.

***

“Elder Brother Xu Qing, I’ve been doing well in the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society....

“I’m going to participate in one of the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society’s ceremonies of enlightenment.... If I succeed, it’s possible that my personality will change.... I’ve never liked my personality anyway. Sometimes I’m too weak....

“I don’t know if I’ll succeed, and if I do, I have no idea how I’ll transform....

“Finally, Elder Brother, I want to offer you my sincere well wishes. I hope you do really well in life. Forever. Always.

“Li Zimei.”

1. The part in which Sporelight and Sunslaughter helped Xu Qing with Forbidden by the Zombie started in the second part of chapter 500. ☜

Thoughts of former days filled Xu Qing’s mind, until the images blurred together like spilled ink.

The ink covered everything, eventually turning into the tree with Li Zimei’s distorted face on it. It was very clear. Thus, the fiendish will was incredibly prominent.

The scene in front of him, plus that letter from Li Zimei, caused a cold light to appear in Xu Qing’s eyes as he turned to look in the direction of the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. He could see what was going on. Because Li Zimei had begun cultivating a special technique, her soul had developed problems.

Some sort of baleful energy had invaded it, inflicting severe damage. That invasion hadn’t happened overnight. In all likelihood, it began with that ceremony of enlightenment she had mentioned.

Because of the pain inflicted during that invasion, Li Zimei’s personality had become distorted, and her mind had changed. She had once been weak, but the pain she had gone through turned her into an increasingly insane killer. Eventually, Li Zimei’s soul was completely fractured to the point where it didn’t even exist. Perhaps that meant that the ceremony had succeeded. When she returned, she wasn’t Li Zimei anymore. Instead, she was a freakish and monstrous killer.

Yet, clearly, something unexpected happened that caused Li Zimei to flee, leading her into a state of conflict with the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society.

Presumably that’s why the classified report mentioned the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society saying she was bedeviled.

The coldness in Xu Qing’s eyes deepened. He could see now that the supposed fiendish will was actually a soul! And it was a very ancient and cruel soul.

The supposed ‘invasion’ was actually a remolding. A possession. Li Zimei had been changed into an embryonic form to be taken over by that ancient soul. And that was why Li Zimei was stuck in a huge tree in the very middle of the Spiritsound forbidden ground.... It was because her transformed, embryonic state was perfectly suitable to be used by the lord of this forbidden ground.

Parasitizing this body would be the perfect way to get out of the forbidden ground... Xu Qing thought.

As for whether or not this was a coincidence... Xu Qing didn’t bother trying to figure it out. The Swordsage Court in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture would have plenty of time to run an investigation later.

Qing Qiu was also stuck in the same tree. She was completely surrounded by the tree, and the blood-red light she emitted had become nutrients that Lord Spiritsound was using as part of the parasitization process.

All of this was actually a natural rule that governed the cultivation of all living things. The weak were the prey of the strong.

Floating Fiend had followed that rule, as did the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. And it was the same with Lord Spiritsound.

Regardless of what fate had in store for the weak, they would experience similar things.

Given Xu Qing’s current level of strength, he couldn’t do anything to change the natural rules that governed the cultivation of all living things. But what he could do was prevent things like that from happening to the people close to him.

Therefore, he started walking into the depths of the Spiritsound forbidden ground. Every step he took caused the forbidden ground to tremble. The mutagen here could invade countless creatures, but it couldn’t affect Xu Qing at all. That was because Xu Qing also emanated the aura of a god, which meant he had his own personal mutagen. And it spread around him in all directions.

The two types of mutagen clashed invisibly, causing the forbidden ground to lurch about. Trees swayed and mountains rumbled. The sound quickly grew louder.

As the sound spread out, Xu Qing took control of it. It became part of his god perception. It became a tool that he sent speeding from all parts of the forbidden ground toward the tree in the middle. It was a deadly sound, like a shocking tempest. Previously intangible sound waves suddenly took shape, bearing down on the huge tree with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force.

Li Zimei’s head suddenly tilted up, and with a twisted facial expression, she opened her mouth and unleashed the most piercing scream imaginable. It was a sharp sound that could flay metal and shatter rock. Heaven and earth trembled, and everything in the area shook.

The sound in the forbidden ground that Xu Qing had taken control of immediately showed signs of breaking away from him.

This was the Spiritsound forbidden ground, and to some extent, that very name, Spiritsound, represented the power of the lord of this place. Although it wasn’t on the level of a god, as the lord of a forbidden ground, he had an amazing status, and obviously had the strength to fight back violently. As the piercing cry spread out, it shook Xu Qing’s control, and also bore down on him with deadly force.

Xu Qing’s expression remained the same as before as he lifted his right hand and slowly closed his fingers into a fist. It was as if he were crushing the void, and taking away everything there. In an instant, his shaken sound authority became as majestic as a mountain. Not even winds from heaven could shake it.

There was more than that. The scream from Li Zimei’s mouth, which had become raw killing intent, was also crushed by Xu Qing.

It was sound seizing! Heaven and earth went quiet!

Next, Xu Qing extended his hand and waved it at the forbidden ground. In an instant, the power of sound authority was fully unleashed.

Countless sounds shattered the silence. It was like the sunrise breaking the dark of night. The entire Spiritsound forbidden ground exploded with sound.

The sound of rushing water from shattered rivers. The sound of leaves falling from exploded evil trees. The sound of howling animals throughout the forbidden ground. Everything became a deadly attack. Rumbling rose high into the heavens. Innumerable trees shattered. Countless mutant beasts screamed as they died.

From high above, it was possible to see the power of the destruction, starting from the borders of the forbidden ground. It spread ferociously, like a huge hand covering everything. As it shot toward the huge tree in the center, nothing could block it. Everything in its path was crushed.

Then it slammed into the tree itself! The tree vibrated. And then, unable to stand up to the force, it collapsed into pieces!

Wood shavings and dust billowed out as Li Zimei and Qing Qiu were revealed. However, they did not fall down as the tree collapsed. Instead, they floated there in midair in a very gruish manner. It was almost as if some mysterious power were controlling them.

Behind the two women, amidst the haze of dust, emerged a three-inch-tall wooden marionette. The marionette was in bad shape, and hanging from his neck was a broken flute. One of his eyes was missing, while the other eye was wide with confusion. From the look of it, his mind was in a state of complete chaos. And yet, he pulsed with clear fluctuations of godliness.

The moment the marionette appeared, the devastated forbidden ground once again surged with life force. The mangled mutant beasts and grues all involuntarily prostrated to the marionette.

And yet, the marionette wasn’t paying attention to the forbidden ground. He was completely focused on Xu Qing. Then, the chaos in his eye rippled, as if he was struggling to force himself into a state of lucidity.

“Leave!” he shouted.

Xu Qing ignored him and kept walking forward.

Upon seeing that, the marionette’s eye became more chaotic and insane. Taking control of Li Zimei, he sent her flying toward Xu Qing.

Powerful killing intent surged out of Li Zimei as she closed in. A freezing wind sprang up in the area, altering perceptions and distorting any line of sight. It was a will domain of killing.

Qing Qiu’s eyes opened, and they were blank with confusion, as if she had just woken from a deep sleep. A blood-colored light suddenly erupted from her, turning everything around her into a hell of blood. Gruish laughter erupted from her mouth.

“Heh heh heh.” That laughter contained a horrifying will. As it echoed out, Qing Qiu’s blank eyes turned to look at Xu Qing. “You... seem really familiar....”

Even as she spoke, the blood from the mutant beasts that had died in the area swirled toward her.

Xu Qing looked closely at Qing Qiu. He was well aware that the strange phenomenon manifesting with Li Zimei and Qing Qiu was called a will domain.

Li Zimei’s will domain focused on slaughter.

And Qing Qiu used the Supreme Arbiter Blood Will Domain! Years ago, his Eldest Brother had explained that the latter was a taboo secret magic from the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. Even achieving minor success with it was very difficult. Supposedly, someone who succeeded in gaining enlightenment of the Blood Will Domain would develop two or more personalities! Each personality would result in one’s view of the world losing some of its color. After reaching ten personalities, the only thing left would be the color of blood, which was considered the level of ultimate success! However, throughout the history of the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society, no one had ever reached the level of ten personalities. All of them died violently before reaching that point. [1]

Back in the era of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity, the Sword Division studied will domains, all in the hopes of identifying ways of subjugating gods.... But in the end, such efforts failed.

Xu Qing also thought back to the cultivation advice the Heir Apparent had given him years ago in the Moonrite Region.[2]

As Li Zimei and Qing Qiu attacked him, Xu Qing didn’t pause for a moment. He kept walking forward, all while gathering essence power in his right eye, causing a dao lineament to appear! The arrival of that lineament caused the cosmos to shiver. It was the authority of erasure!

Using the authority in that eye, Xu Qing looked again at Li Zimei and Qing Qiu. Immediately, the countless threads connecting them to the marionette were visible to him. And if he could see them, he could erase them.

Xu Qing closed his right eye, and that motion was like an act of cutting. Instantly, Li Zimei and Qing Qiu lurched to a halt and stood in place, trembling.

There were no more invisible threads connected to them. Xu Qing’s act of closing his eye had severed all of them. The two women opened their eyes, only to close them again and fall to the ground, where they lay unmoving. The will domains they had summoned quickly dissipated.

At the same time, a miserable shriek rang out from the mouth of the marionette whose strings had been severed. The marionette shivered, and then shot toward Xu Qing, bursting with madness and hatred. He shrieked, and it turned into a semi-transparent spear of sound waves that sped viciously toward Xu Qing’s heart!

Xu Qing didn’t do anything to evade the spear. When it touched him, it was as if it had slammed into an immovable mountain. The spear shattered. It was destroyed in an instant.

The backlash affected the marionette. And thus, Lord Spiritsound was sent tumbling backward, cracks spreading out over him. Then the instinctive fear of death that all living things took over. Despite the chaos in his mind, the marionette turned and fled at top speed.

He was too slow.

Xu Qing took a step forward, and a great sun took shape in his sea of consciousness. Outside of him, brilliant light and endless heat erupted as he became a magnificent sun. And he rose over the Spiritsound forbidden ground!

At the moment, evening was giving way to the darkness of night. But all of a sudden... night reversed, and the dome of heaven grew bright! The pitch black forbidden ground was inundated with beams of light, causing the mutagen-filled river to suddenly seem clear and distinct.

All living things were being purified!

The sun rose into the sky, lighting up the night, illuminating the Spiritsound forbidden ground, filling everything with brightness and heat. Though it was not the same as a real sun, and could not nourish all living beings in Revered Ancient, as far as this forbidden ground was concerned, the rising sun that was Xu Qing was more than enough to suppress everything that was within his gaze.

Within that gaze was the forbidden ground, which was currently rumbling loudly. And the river water within it was seething violently. Overhead, the dome of heaven rippled and distorted, all while the ground underfoot blurred dramatically.

The moment the sun rose, Xu Qing was the lord of this place. The mutagen native to the Spiritsound forbidden ground tried to struggle. Fluctuations rolled out, and endless howls filled the air, including those from the marionette with the broken flute.

The marionette tumbled backward, eyes full of madness, shrieking and howling in defiance. He wanted to fight back, but the light from the immense sun made that completely impossible. At that critical moment, he put the broken flute to his mouth and blew, causing an ear-piercing sound to pierce through the air. That was his attempt to fight Xu Qing.

It was somewhat effective in dimming the light of the sun. However, it only lasted for an instant before everything went back to normal. And all that was left behind was despair. The marionette’s mind was muddled, but right now, he gained a moment of clarity, and his face became a mask of bitterness. He knew that his success came from this forbidden ground, but he also knew that this forbidden ground had limited his growth.

As the marionette wallowed in bitterness, the flute music shattered. The flute trembled, and several horrifying cracks spread out through it. Loud cracking sounds rang out from the marionette as a network of cracks spread out over him as well.

Immortal light flowed out, shining on everything from the sun that was Xu Qing. Then, most of the marionette crumbled into fragments, while the portion that remained was smashed out of the air by the pressure. A boom rang out as he landed right on the spot where the enormous tree had stood. He struggled mightily, but it was to no avail, as if a gigantic invisible mountain was on top of it. He couldn’t even rise to his feet.

The mutagen in the forbidden ground was suppressed along with the marionette. The river went still and all living things prostrated.

Only Xu Qing was still in motion, striding over the horizon until he was right above the marionette. He looked down at him.

The marionette could barely look up. When he opened his mouth, nothing came out except the rough swoosh of wood shavings scraping against each other. Then the clarity in his eyes faded away, replaced again with chaos and madness as he glared at Xu Qing.

Voice calm, Xu Qing explained the truths he had come to realize. “When you realized that you couldn’t rely on the forbidden ground to grow stronger, and that you would be forced to wait for the gaze of the broken face, you got impatient. You decided that you might as well take a risk and try to free yourself from the restrictions of the forbidden ground.

“Thus, you possessed Li Zimei. At the same time, you paid a steep price. The process caused your mind to flee, resulting in your devolution into chaos.”

The marionette responded by struggling to free himself.

Xu Qing shook his head and looked over to the unconscious Li Zimei and Qing Qiu.

Qing Qiu seemed to be doing well. Xu Qing had arrived with time to spare to help her. Though she had lost some life force, her foundation had not collapsed, and she could be saved.

But Li Zimei... was struggling to breathe. Her soul had suffered immense damage, and looked like it was about to rot away completely. Plus, Lord Spiritsound had halfway succeeded in possessing her.... That possession was a tribulation, but at the same time, had kept her alive. If Lord Spiritsound died, then the half that had been possessed would disappear, and Li Zimei’s spiritual souls would leave, and her physical souls would dissipate.

If this situation had occurred before Xu Qing faced Floating Fiend, then he wouldn’t have been able to reverse things. Without help from Empress Summer Departure or his Master, he would have been forced to just watch Li Zimei die, unable to change her fate.

But right now, he did have a way to change things.

The dao lineament of the authority of erasure in Xu Qing’s right eye glittered. At the same time, he waved his right hand and pulled a needle out of nowhere. It glittered with frigid light. That needle looked completely ordinary in nature. But the moment it appeared, a host of projections appeared around it.

That needle came from Floating Fiend’s son. In the Vivifiend holy land, it had been a legacy treasure handed down by a peak Grand Emperor. And it had the power to stitch karma. It could be used on its own, although the results would be crude. However, when it was combined with the authority of erasure, the results could be considered perfect.

Because of the authority of erasure, Xu Qing’s view of the world was completely different from that of an ordinary person. He could see the numerous threads of karma. Earlier, he had severed the threads connecting Li Zimei to the marionette. However, that was a temporary thing. Those threads hadn’t ceased to exist. And now, they were already forming anew. If they were permanently and completely severed, then given Li Zimei’s weakened state, she would die immediately.

Therefore, before preparing to sever Li Zimei’s karma, he needed to connect her karma to something else that would keep her alive. And the best karma available was right in front of him. Xu Qing’s gaze took in the forbidden ground around him.

After some thought, he waved his hand, and the needle glittered as it shot toward Li Zimei, then began whizzing about her as the stitching began. It was taking the karma between Li Zimei and the forbidden ground and stitching it tight.

At the same time, Xu Qing called out a pair of rusty shears, which appeared above the marionette’s head. Then, Xu Qing used his authority of erasure to control it, causing it to snap closed loudly.

A loud snipping sound rang out. The karma between the forbidden ground and the marionette was thus severed. The marionette spasmed and released a howl of anguish.

However, given the level of Xu Qing’s cultivation base, that severing couldn’t be absolute. It was only temporary. The severed threads immediately tried to start connecting again. Thankfully, the needle was already stitching the karma threads together between Li Zimei and the forbidden ground. As the needle sped around, it caused a host of afterimages to build up.

The process repeated several times over. He continued to sever karma threads with the shears, while simultaneously stitching Li Zimei and the forbidden ground together with karma threads. Eventually, they were inextricably linked, at which point, the marionette’s karma had been permanently and completely severed!

The marionette shivered from head to toe as more cracks spread out over him. Black blood sprayed out of his mouth, and he fell unconscious. The broken flute hanging from his neck faded into nothing.

Meanwhile, Li Zimei’s aura skyrocketed as she became one with the forbidden ground. The extreme damage to her soul also began to heal.

Branches snaked out, spreading in all directions, and surrounding Li Zimei, converging to form an enormous tree. Li Zimei was sucked into the tree until only her face was visible. However, this time, her face wasn’t twisted and distorted. It was tranquil.

In the spot where her chest was, there appeared a broken flute. That was the symbol of rulership over the Spiritsound forbidden ground.

At a glance, Xu Qing could tell that though Li Zimei was currently asleep, once she woke up, she would become... the new ruler of Spiritsound. She would be Lady Spiritsound.

“Li Zimei, I hope you do really well in life. Forever. Always.”

He was returning the same well wishes to Li Zimei that she had given to him years ago.

When the words reached Li Zimei’s ears, she shivered slightly despite being asleep. Then her eyelashes fluttered, and though she couldn’t open her eyes, tears leaked down her cheeks and onto the ground. Perhaps when she woke up, the spot where the tears had landed would be full of little flowers that would preserve the memories of this moment forever.

Xu Qing left. He took the sleeping marionette with him to give as a gift to Emperor Ancient Spirit.

With the wave of his hand, Xu Qing pulled Qing Qiu floating up into the air. Along with her, he flew up to the Sageheaven Pagoda floating above.

Once inside, he turned and looked off into the distance. Dozens of figures were approaching from over the horizon.

They included the grand elder from Emperor-Receiving Prefecture’s Swordsage Court, representatives from Sea-Sealing County, as well as top experts from the Church of Departure and the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. Even just seeing the Sageheaven Pagoda from a distance provoked reactions of shock from them. Then they spotted Xu Qing. The Swordsage Palace grand elder immediately bowed formally.

“Well met, Your Excellency!”

The people sent from Sea-Sealing County to help out didn’t include anyone Xu Qing recognized. They were nonhuman cultivators who had been recruited recently. Though none of them had ever seen Xu Qing in person, all of them had seen images of him. The moment they laid eyes on him, they reeled in astonishment, and immediately bowed.

The experts from the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society and Church of Departure also offered greetings. The representatives from the former were visibly nervous, while the latter seemed concerned.

Among the people from the Church of Departure was someone Xu Qing had seen before. He was Qing Qiu’s older brother. Because he was in the Junior generation, he was located in the back of the group. The mere sight of Xu Qing left him shaken to the core. After all, he had heard a lot about Xu Qing from his little sister, and how she had once called him Big Bro Kid. Of course, he knew all about who Xu Qing was, and how important he was. He had heard the stories, which were already becoming legends. But to see him in person now was a totally different matter. He just couldn’t stop thinking about that dirty kid he’d seen so many years ago in the scavenger basecamp. It was impossible to predict what would happen with the passage of time. Back then, he’d hardly spared a passing glance for Xu Qing. But now, didn’t hesitate to incline his head and bow at the waist.[1]

***

Shortly after, Xu Qing went back into the pagoda.

The people from the Church of Departure took Qing Qiu with them, saying that they had a secret magic that would speed up her recovery. They also respectfully told Xu Qing that though the teachings of their Church of Departure had previously been closely related to the holy lands, a new way of thinking had taken hold, and thus, going forward they would steadfastly side with Revered Ancient. As for Qing Qiu, she would become a holy daughter of the Church of Departure in the east of Revered Ancient, and would receive the legacy of their Arbiter of Destiny.

Xu Qing decided to let the Swordsage Palace deal with the problems with the Supreme Arbiter Immortal Society. They would be put on trial, and if it turned out that they had colluded with Lord Spiritsound to set him free, then they would be severely punished.

In formal and respectful fashion, everyone waited as the pagoda glittered with seven-colored light and disappeared over the horizon. Then they went their separate ways, all of them thinking different things.

Night returned to the dome of heaven.

The Spiritsound forbidden ground filled with mutagen once more, and barely discernible flute music drifted out from the huge tree in the middle of it.

Two days later, the clouds parted as the Sageheaven Pagoda appeared in the sky above an area filled with massive trees. It was the ancestral land of the Wood Spirits in Sea-Sealing County.

The moment the pagoda appeared, terrifying pressure radiated down. The Wood Spirits’ chief, grand elder, and other powerful experts rose up into the air suspiciously. Then Xu Qing emerged from the pagoda. After him came Grandpa Ninth and Erniu.

When the Wood Spirits’ chief and grand elder saw it was Xu Qing, they breathed sighs of relief and bowed in greeting. After a brief reunion, Xu Qing explained his reason for coming.

When Xu Qing requested access to the subterranean tunnel leading to Emperor Ancient Spirit, the Wood Spirits immediately parted to make a path for him. Soon, Xu Qing and the others were walking down the dark passageway.

Once inside the cool, damp cave, Grandpa Ninth expressionlessly stepped forward. Xu Qing followed him. Erniu kept pace curiously. It was his first time here. Together, the three of them jumped over the edge and shot down. freewebnovel.com

An aura of death rose from below, cold and sinister. It was accompanied by mysterious cries that one would expect to hear in the Yellow Springs. They were constantly hit with a force of expulsion.

To the three of them, though, none of those things were worth mentioning. All of them exuded pressure that destroyed the aura of death, suppressed the howls, and shattered the force of expulsion.

The bottom grew nearer and nearer.

"What a lovely place, little Ah Qing!” Erniu said, his eyes shining as they sped along. He licked his lips. “However, in terms of karma, this place exists outside of the influence of the heavenly daos. It’s not part of reincarnation. The only thing here is death.... This place has nothing going for it except that it’s the perfect hiding spot! Also... I can smell the aroma of treasure!”

Erniu was going to keep talking, but then they reached the bottom. Upon piercing through it, they entered a world of illusions. There was mist everywhere, making it difficult to see very far.

Of course, Xu Qing was a very different person compared to the last time he was in this place. When he sent his god perception out, he was easily able to identify the path he had walked in the past, as well as the enormous snake.[2]

Erniu just kept smacking his lips in excitement.

Grandpa Ninth looked cold and apathetic, and didn’t say a word.

After an incense stick’s worth of time passed, Xu Qing’s god perception picked up something unusual.

“Hmm?” He stopped moving and turned to look in that direction. He had just noticed a very faint trace of something that glittered briefly. It was something ancient, hidden, and full of malevolence.

“Nothing worth worrying about,” Grandpa Ninth said coolly.

Erniu also looked in that direction, then licked his lips dramatically.

Xu Qing looked away and kept going forward.

Shortly after, they reached their goal. It was a gargantuan, decomposing snake that pulsed with a strong aura of death. Resting atop the head of that dead snake was a major world, blurry and filled with anguished howls that filled Xu Qing’s god perception. His eyes flashed as he vanished. When he reappeared, he, Erniu, and Grandpa Ninth were above the world that existed atop the snake’s head.

“This is the place!” he said, leading the way inside.

Eventually, a heaven-rending, earth-crushing rumbling sound echoed out as they broke through the world barrier.

The aura was familiar. The sky had no sun or moon, only ghostly stars that cast dim light. The ground was made of decomposing flesh. There were no mountains or trees, only endless death.

This was the Ancient Spirit world!

The moment the three of them arrived, a huge eye opened above an imperial palace made of flesh.

“Dammit! What are you doing here again??”

“The Ancient Spirits,” Grandpa Ninth said calmly, looking around at the world of death with its dusky dome of heaven. “Before the time of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity, this species conquered Revered Ancient! As a people, they were known for being skilled at warfare. They are born as snakes, but can take human form later, whereupon they live life accompanied by dragons and snakes. Ultimately, they can master the Ancient Spirit Battle Body. Back when they ruled Revered Ancient, they dominated all other species, forcing them to bow their heads. At that time, humans were weak and fragmented.”

As Grandpa Ninth strode forward, his footfalls caused the dome of heaven to tremble, and sent rumbling sounds through the lands. Countless deceased souls fled, and the zombies in the mire trembled. And it seemed to be calling out to something from the outside world.

Xu Qing and Erniu followed him.

Erniu glanced around curiously, and would occasionally squat down and scoop up some soil, or reach out to grab a deceased soul. His eyes shone more and more brightly with every moment that passed. He was obviously very interested in this place.

But considering that his right eye contained the authority of erasure, he was now able to see karma. Because of that, he could tell that this aura coming off Grandpa Ninth was karma from beyond the heavens.

Eldest Brother once said that Senior Li Zihua was on the way back here.... Considering that, I bet Grandpa Ninth’s aura is guiding him here.

There was a gleam of admiration in Grandpa Ninth’s eyes, although it wasn’t because he looked up to Emperor Ancient Spirit personally, but rather, because he appreciated the ambitions and choices of a powerful expert.

“Someone like that—” Grandpa Ninth suddenly stopped in place and looked out into the void, his eyes flashing with the desire to do battle. Lifting his right hand, he clenched his hand into a fist in the direction of the canopy of heaven.

The arrival of that sword caused wild colors to flash in heaven and earth. A powerful aura and terrifying fluctuations erupted from Grandpa Ninth. And then... he slashed the sword toward the sky.

Because of it, an enemy hē looked at would have light injuries turn into serious ones. And serious injuries would become fatal and deadly. What was more, within the Ancient Spirit world, there were eyes above ninety-eight other imperial palaces. All of them opened, looked at Grandpa Ninth, and unleashed their power.

Having placated Grandpa Ninth, Xu Qing turned to Emperor Ancient Spirit and bowed. “Well met, Your Majesty!”

Emperor Ancient Spirit’s heart was pounding, and countless curses were building up within hīm. Hē wanted to let loose an enraged roar. But after looking at Xu Qing, that rage turned into pure astonishment.

His fleshly body....

All of Emperor Ancient Spirit’s pupils constricted. Previously, hīs attention had been focused on Ninth Sib. But after looking at Xu Qing, hē noticed his terrifying fleshly body.

“Senior,” Xu Qing continued, “I happened upon a destined opportunity a while back, and transformed my fleshly body. I can explain all the details to Your Majesty later. Today, I came for those streams of imperial energy.”

Xu Qing was already eyeing the thirteen dragons made from the destiny aura of the Ancient Spirits.

Xu Qing’s expression didn’t change. Actually, he wasn’t surprised at all that Emperor Ancient Spirit had reacted in this way. After all, he had negotiated with hīm on occasions before, and on the way here, he had come up with a plan along with Erniu and Grandpa Ninth.

When she succeeds, she’ll come to find you.”[1]

Xu Qing looked at the palace. He couldn’t send his god perception very far inside, but he could sense that the fluctuations were stable. Retracting his god perception, he sat down, closed his eyes, and began to meditate.

The night passed.

Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior solemnly stood watch the entire night. Little Shadow was also completely on guard. Little Shadow seemed antagonistic, while Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior was smiling.

There had been developments since the arrival of the celestial-level holy lands.... Large-scale war had broken out in the south, west, and north of Revered Ancient. There had been great victories and defeats on both sides, and casualties were high. At any given moment, lives were being lost, and new fighting was breaking out. Revered Ancient was in a state of major upheaval.

In the east, the alliance of species led by the Firemoon Darkheavens and humankind created a consummate spell formation that separated heaven and earth. What lay outside of the formation was the dome of heaven, where four celestial-level holy lands were. Inside of the spell formation were the living beings native to Revered Ancient.

Though the four holy lands in question all had Grand Emperors, after the initial clash with the empress and the three Firemoon gods, they didn’t show their faces again. That said, the three gods also stayed out of the public eye. No one knew exactly how that peak battle had played out.

There was only one certainty: Empress Summer Departure was fine, and was the one leading the war effort.

Fighting continued in the east, with both Firemoons and humans willing to fight fiercely. There were no major battles, as both the eastern forces and the holy lands both tried to keep things under control. That said, there were small battles that occurred on a daily basis.

At the moment, one of those small battles was playing out atop the consummate spell formation. A lot of people were involved in the fighting, and they looked like a host of black spots buzzing around atop the spell formation.

It was around that time that Xu Qing and Erniu arrived in the imperial capital, having taken several teleportation portals from Sea-Sealing County. Things had gone smoothly on their journey. The moment they appeared on the teleportation portal, they heard the sounds of booms and screams from above. The countless sounds mixed together into a rumble like that of thunder. The colorful light of magical techniques flared everywhere, creating dazzling glows interspersed with periods of darkness.

When looking up, it was possible to see the ranks of eastern cultivators, some of them on the front lines fighting, others in the back resting. Those who came back into the spell formation were all in bad condition.

However, the situation was the same with the holy lands. Corpses dropped down constantly, to be destroyed by the spell formation.

“War...” Xu Qing murmured, his expression grave.

Because the teleportation portal was located in the middle of an army encampment, it was under constant watch of the divine sense of numerous cultivators. The moment he and Erniu arrived, streams of deadly energy locked onto them. Upon realizing who Xu Qing was, though, the divine sense and streams of energy vanished.
