Xu Qing had seen this person before. He was a human heavenly marquis surnamed Chen.

“Greetings, Imperial Tutor!” Heavenly Marquis Chen said. “Some of the heavenly kings are trapped on the battlefield outside the formation. As a result, your humble servant is currently in charge here. What’s more, Her Majesty issued orders for you to go to the grand hall as soon as you returned.”

Xu Qing nodded. Looking up at the fighting and scanning the field of battle with god perception, he could see that the forces from this encampment were made of a variety of species, and there were many of them who were wounded. In the other parts of the east that he had traveled through, the fighting wasn’t nearly as severe as this. It seemed most of the action was taking place here. This was the core of the east, and it could also be considered the front line of fighting.

“How goes the battle?” Xu Qing asked.

“We’re holding strong for now,” Heavenly Marquis Chen replied with a grin. However, his aura wasn’t very stable, and he had obviously sustained some injuries. He was about to continue speaking when, all of a sudden, a huge boom echoed out beyond the spell formation.

In the swarm of black dots above that made up the forces of both sides, a dazzling eruption of light could be seen. It was a burly, middle-aged man from the holy lands who had a pair of wings on his back. He pulsed with a fiendish, bloody aura, and had a cultivation base in the five-world Smoldering God level. It was a cultivation base that surpassed many of the human heavenly kings.

In a small-scale battle like this, some of the species had fielded Smoldering Gods, but most of those were pinned down and couldn’t disengage to move to other parts of the battlefield. Therefore, this newcomer was able to unleash slaughter as soon as he arrived.

From the look of it, he was carving out a path through the battlefield. Flanking him was a group of over a thousand Devilbird cultivators, who were acting like bodyguards. Together, they crushed everything in their path. And their target was the spell formation.

When Heavenly Marquis Chen saw what was happening, his pupils constricted. However, he didn’t panic. Obviously, there were measures in place to deal with situations like this. Light flowed across the spell formation as it reacted to stop the assault.

However, that was when Xu Qing vanished. Astonishingly, when he reappeared, he was outside of the spell formation.

A sound far more intense than anything from before rang out clearly for both sides to hear. As that deafening sound erupted, Xu Qing appeared right in front of the path of the charging Devilbird. The burly man saw him, snorted coldly, and continued forward. All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint.

Inside the spell formation, Heavenly Marquis Chen was shocked. He knew that Xu Qing was a very important person, but had the impression that his battle prowess was just barely able to meet the standard for heavenly kings. And this was a five-world Smoldering God.... He immediately got nervous.

Next to him was Erniu, who cleared his throat. “What are you getting worried about? Calm down.”

Of course, it didn’t matter what Erniu said, there was no way Heavenly Marquis Chen couldn’t be nervous.

And he wasn’t the only one. There were heavenly kings from numerous species on the battlefield who saw what was happening and recognized Xu Qing. All of them were stunned, and some of them even started cursing and swearing. Clearly, none of them believed that Xu Qing could stand up to this five-world Devilbird cultivator. Some were inclined to interfere, but none were able to break free from the fighting to do so. All they could do was watch as the burly Devilbird closed in on Xu Qing.

“Foolishness! Why’d Xu Qing show up here of all places?”

“Activate the spell formation! Send it out to protect Xu Qing!”

“Hurry!”

The spell formation emitted rumbling sounds and bright light as it prepared to extend protection to Xu Qing.

But that only served to emphasize to the Devilbird that Xu Qing was important. Upon seeing what was happening, his eyes lit up. He had recognized Xu Qing!

It was only natural that the Devilbird holy land would have information about all the important humans. And that was especially true of Xu Qing. After all, he had brought an entire holy land to ruin. After all, he was why all the terrestrial-level holy lands had been driven out of the east. That said, their information was limited to the fact that Xu Qing had been captured by Floating Fiend and then subsequently freed. They didn’t know all the details. For example, they didn’t know that Floating Fiend ultimately died at Xu Qing’s hands, nor did they have any clue what Xu Qing’s battle prowess was.

Therefore, this burly Devilbird’s eyes lit up. Cackling, he accelerated in Xu Qing’s direction. But then... just as he was about to reach Xu Qing....

Xu Qing’s facial expression didn’t change a bit as he lifted his hand. Reaching toward the burly Devilbird, he clenched his hand into a fist. That gesture caused all of the sound surrounding Xu Qing on the massive battlefield to cease! Sound had been seized!

The silence only lasted for a moment. Then, all of that sound converged on the burly Devilbird. It was like an unrivaled wave that turned into a massive sphere surrounding the Devilbird and his thousand bodyguards. freewebnovel.com

The sound waves assailed them endlessly with deadly force. Screams began to ring out from the mouths of the burly Devilbird and his guards. But that only added to the deadly sound authority. Thirty percent of the bodyguards exploded, whereupon the burly Devilbird’s face fell. He had just heard chanting.

The chanting grew clear and intense, repeating endlessly. It was an ancient power, something mad and voracious that penetrated his heart and mind, overtaking his perceptions. And it took away the very concept of sound from them. Their bodies, souls, and even their sense of self was being taken. And then... the burly Devilbird and all the remaining guards shattered into a blood mist!

The sphere collapsed, turning back into countless sounds. Xu Qing remained in the middle of it all as the sounds spread in all directions. Wherever they passed, and wherever sound existed on the battlefield, deadly attacks were unleashed.

Although this incident only took place on one small corner of the battlefield, its effects spread instantly. In fact, the heavenly kings from the various species as well as the Smoldering Gods from the holy lands were all visibly taken aback!

There was no doubt... that Xu Qing’s attack was simply too fast and deadly. The eastern cultivators were stunned. The holy lands cultivators were astonished.

“Godly authority!”

“Something’s off about this human!”

Though the forces from the holy lands were shaken, the reality was that... the actions of one person couldn’t affect an entire war. At least, not unless that person was strong enough to crush anything and everything.

Next, a terrifying stream of divine will shot out from one of the holy lands hovering above. It indicated the arrival of an Imperial Sovereign!

At the same time, the aura of a god shot out from the human region below. It was the zombie emperor Dark War!

Because of pressure from those two forces, Xu Qing vanished, returning back into the spell formation. Upon leaving, he released the power of sound authority onto the battlefield, mixing misfortune and curse power with it. The rumbling outside of the spell formation turned into a tempest of sound.

The cultivators of the east who were participating in the fighting were all enlivened. The heavenly kings issued decisive orders, and thus took advantage of the moment to launch a deadly counter attack. The small-scale battle was now becoming somewhat one-sided. Given that, it wasn’t long before the sound of bells rang out from the holy lands, calling for a retreat....

About two hours later, this particular battle was over, and the forces from the various species fell back, all of them discussing Xu Qing’s arrival.

***

Xu Qing and Erniu had already entered the imperial capital, and were now waiting outside of the grand hall.

Xu Qing had changed into his imperial tutor’s robe, while Erniu was wearing his special Grand Zodiacist Armor, which was an imitation of the Grand Darkheaven Armor. The suit of battle armor had been made according to his specifications, and he had personally overseen the process. He didn’t get many chances to wear it, but loved how it looked. As he stood proudly in front of the grand hall, his armor sparkled like the sun and made him look like he was made from pure light. From a distance, he really did look mighty and impressive.

They didn’t have to wait long before a voice called out from inside the hall.

“The imperial tutor and the Grand Zodiacist are hereby summoned for an audience with the empress!”[2]

Xu Qing and Erniu strode into the hall. Upon entering, they saw the assembled officials, as well as the empress seated above everyone else. Next to the empress was Ningyan, who looked very excited.

“My respects, Your Majesty!” Xu Qing said, bowing at the waist.

Erniu also bowed and said the same words.

The empress nodded slightly, then spoke in a cool voice. “It’s good you’re back. Have a seat.”

Xu Qing strode over to his spot among the thirty-three heavenly kings. Specifically, he was able to sit in the second-ranking spot. From that position, he could look down on all the other officials. There was only one person who could sit higher than him among the officials, and it was King Firecrusher, who wasn’t present. The other officials all had to incline their heads when Xu Qing looked at them.

As for Ningyan, he bowed to Xu Qing. Whether it was because of how Ningyan had previously relied so much on Xu Qing, or the fact that Xu Qing was now the imperial tutor, it was from deep in his heart that Ningyan offered him devotion. In fact, Ningyan was actually closer to Xu Qing than he was to his own mother.

When Erniu saw all of that happening, he felt a bit jealous. However, his attention was soon drawn to an old friend. At first he looked surprised, and then thoughtful. He even took out his sageheaven god vine and started fiddling with it.

As for Xu Qing, after he looked over at the officials, his gaze was also drawn to that same figure....

The Devilbird cultivator they had both noticed was filled with mixed emotions as he took a deep breath and bowed. “I, Feng Lintao, offer greetings to the imperial tutor!”

1. The living teleportation portal was introduced in chapter 743, and Erniu took the hairs in chapter 744. Back in roughly 904-907, when Xu Qing and Erniu went out to the broken face, they used these hairs as part of the plan. Unfortunately, the author got mixed up and started calling them feathers. Back then, I was confused about where the ‘teleportation feathers’ came from, but assumed I had just forgotten something. As it turns out, it was an author mistake. He also calls them feathers here in 1016. It was in the course of going back to search for the references that I realized what happened. Some of you (mostly Champions) read the 904-907 part with the ‘feather’ translation. I’ve since edited that mistake away, so for those who became Champions later, or who read them after their public release, you might have read them as ‘hairs.’ In any case, everything is now edited to maintain continuity. ☜

2. Erniu is being called the Grand Zodiacist because of his Grand Zodiacist Armor that he was given in chapter 929. I originally translated that suit of armor in a different way, and some Champions might have read that version. I later decided to change the translation when I realized that it was supposed to be connected to a title. That wasn’t clear early on, but here in 1016 it’s much more obvious. ☜

Feng Lintao was sighing in his heart. Sometimes it was impossible to predict how things would turn out with certain people. Things could change dramatically. That said, Feng Lintao was an extraordinary individual in his own right. After all, it was Lan Yao herself who had described him as selfish, cold, apathetic, brutal, and someone who could patiently endure all sorts of situations.

Therefore, after defecting to humankind, he had done just that: endure. And now, even though the sight of Xu Qing provoked some mixed emotions, he quickly set them aside. As he did, he didn’t attempt to hide what he was feeling. In fact, he intentionally let those emotions flicker across his face. This was something he had become quite skilled at doing.

Even as a half-blooded Devilbird, he had made the difficult journey to Smoldering God. Given that, it was only natural that he was a survivor. He knew how to use every asset at his disposal, even his emotions, to his advantage. He had learned how to do that from a young age. And how, he was using that tactic in order to prove his sincerity.

After all... in the months since he had defected, he had mostly been ignored. The empress hadn’t made any special arrangements for him. As a result, he was feeling a bit unsettled. He was well aware that it was all because the empress hadn’t fully accepted his request for asylum. Shē was still watching him. Therefore, he needed to find the right opportunity to prove his loyalty.

It was with such thoughts in mind that he clasped hands and bowed to Xu Qing. He made sure that it came across as sincere.

Xu Qing looked at Feng Lintao calmly and without speaking. He looked neither happy nor angry, and in fact, there didn’t seem to be any emotion at all within him.

Though Xu Qing didn’t speak, Erniu did. Beaming, he toyed with his sageheaven god vine and said, “Hey, Little Fengy! Long time no see!” [1]

Feng Lintao turned to Erniu. Looking somewhat sorrowful, he clasped hands and bowed. “Greetings, Grand Zodiacist. I apologize for how I acted when we first met. I hope you and the imperial tutor can let bygones be bygones. I can’t pretend that I had another choice other than surrendering to you humans, but at the same time, I hope you know that I’m being completely sincere.”

Feng Lintao chose to bow his head as a show of both respect and weakness. At the same time, it was a way of proving that he really was acquainted with Xu Qing and Erniu.

Of course, all it took was a glance for Xu Qing to see what was going on. And considering how sharp Erniu’s eyes were, how could he not realize as well?

Hefting the god vine, Erniu smiled happily. “Why wouldn’t we let bygones be bygones? After all, you gave little Ah Qing and I some really nice stuff! In fact, I haven’t had a chance to thank you for your generosity!”

Feng Lintao smiled wryly and forced himself to suppress his inner rage. In the final analysis, he didn’t hate Xu Qing very much. But he definitely hated Erniu. Erniu was the one who had scammed him. Erniu was the one who had pretended to be gasping on the verge of death, and had caused Feng Lintao to slip up in rare fashion. What was more, it was Erniu who, at a most critical moment, had devoured the god vine and taken away his trump card. That was what had led to the prolonged pursuit by Lan Yao and Yue Dong. Were it not for Erniu, he could have turned defeat into victory. The source of all his problems was right in front of him.

That said, he couldn’t openly show his hatred. Taking a deep breath, Feng Lintao suppressed the rage inside of him.

Unfortunately, that was when Erniu said something unusually shameful. “Come now, you cute little vine. Say hi to our benefactor!”

Looking very pleased with himself, Erniu lifted the vine up. The vine turned, and its leaves rustled....

Feng Lintao had to struggle to keep himself under control.

Standing not too far away was the chief minister. When he saw that Erniu was planning to keep talking, he quickly interrupted by speaking to Xu Qing.

“Imperial Tutor, the reason Her Majesty summoned you, beyond mundane military matters, is because we need to confirm something.”

Xu Qing looked over at the chief minister. “I supposed it has to do with Feng Lintao’s identity?”

The chief minister nodded. “Not just that, though. Imperial Tutor, would you please take a look at the contents of this jade slip?”

The chief minister took out the slip and sent it flying over to Xu Qing. Inside of it were the testimonies and entreaties of Feng Lintao.

Xu Qing took the jade slip and studied it for a few breaths of time. Then he said, “I first encountered this person on the way back to humankind from Firemoon Darkheaven territory. All the relevant details are within the jade slip I previously submitted.

“As for the conflict between this person and the women named Yue Dong and Lan Yao, based on what I saw, they really did want to kill each other. In fact, were it not for the assistance provided by my Eldest Brother and I, this person would have had a hard time escaping death that day.

“As for how my Eldest Brother and I got wrapped up in that whole affair, it seems to me it was just random chance. If the Devilbird holy land had sent this Feng Lintao here in advance as a spy, it seems unlikely to me that he would choose to surrender. In the end, Her Majesty will need to make the final decision about what to do.”

Xu Qing said nothing further after that. The chief minister nodded. Xu Qing had essentially corroborated Feng Lintao’s story about his surrender. As a result, Feng Lintao breathed a slight sigh of relief inwardly.

With that, the session of court went on. As various ministers brought their reports about the war effort, Xu Qing was able to get a general understanding of how things were going, and what losses had been sustained.

Overall, things weren’t looking good. The atmosphere in the grand hall slowly grew more and more oppressive.

As Feng Lintao listened, he didn’t dare to do anything to attract attention to himself. In fact, had he been given a choice, he would rather not listen to this information.

About two hours later, the session of court ended, and Feng Lintao respectfully left.

Xu Qing didn’t move. The grand hall emptied until the only people left behind were Xu Qing, Erniu, Empress Summer Departure, and Ningyan.

Standing, Xu Qing bowed to the empress. “Your Majesty, is it correct to assume you asked me to stay behind because you have some orders?”

The empress glanced at Erniu. Erniu pretended to not notice.

A moment later, the empress said, “Xu Qing, I need you to help me do something.”

Xu Qing didn’t react to the words. He just waited to hear what would come next. freewebnovel.com

“I need you to think of a way to capture Lan Yao. And if you can’t capture her, I want you to bring her corpse back here.”

A look of curiosity appeared in Xu Qing’s eyes. “Lan Yao?”

Based on the words exchanged between Lan Yao and Feng Lintao in the Fardark Cistern incident, he was under the impression that Lan Yao was backed by powerful people in the Devilbird holy land. But even still, that didn’t seem enough to make the empress herself take an interest in the woman.

Ningyan looked surprised, and clearly had no idea what his mother was up to.

“There is more to Lan Yao than meets the eye,” the empress said. When both Xu Qing and Ningyan looked confused, shē expressionlessly continued, “The Devilbird holy land apparently has two Grand Emperors. One of them is suspected to have perished, and Lan Yao is a descendant of that perished Grand Emperor. Based on the intelligence reports I’ve received, she has the most pure bloodline in her clan. If you can bring her back, I can use her blood to ascertain whether or not the Grand Emperor is actually dead. And I can use her blood for other purposes as well.”

The empress took out a white jade slip. It was made from a special material that made it seem real, but at the same time, illusory. It almost looked like a construction of pure light.

“If you encounter any obstacle you can’t overcome, Xu Qing, just crush that light-jade, and I will go in person to help.” With the wave of a hand, the empress sent the light-jade flying over to Xu Qing.

He accepted it, and could immediately sense the immense pressure coming from it. Xu Qing established a mental connection to it, then put it away. “Your Majesty, capturing Lan Yao will require the use of Feng Lintao. Putting him out there as bait will definitely draw her out. That said, he’s crafty, and can’t be relied upon in life-or-death situations. He definitely has backup plans in place. If we conceal the truth from him, only for him to find out we’re using him as bait, it’s hard to say what will happen.”

“What suggestions do you have?” the empress asked.

Before Xu Qing could respond, Erniu’s eyes lit up and he interrupted, “I have an idea!”

With that, his lips moved slightly as he transmitted a message to Xu Qing and the empress. An odd expression appeared on Xu Qing’s face, all while Erniu looked incomparably pleased.

The empress’ eyes glittered. “Permission granted.”

Xu Qing got to his feet, took his leave from the empress, and left the grand hall with the eager Erniu.

Inside the hall, Ningyan watched them go and wished he could go with them. He also wondered what the three of them had just talked about secretly. Of course, he didn’t dare to take any action without his mother’s permission. Even as he thought about the outside world, the empress spoke to him in a calm voice.

“Ning’er, I need you to pen an imperial edict for me.”

“Yes, ma’am,” Ningyan said solemnly.

***

Five days went by.

Xu Qing and Erniu tracked down Wu Jianwu, who had been living in the imperial capital for all this time. Wu Jianwu handed over to them two baby rats, golden in color, that had hatched from the eggs they gave him....

Around then, an imperial edict was circulated in the east of Revered Ancient.

Feng Lintao was appointed as Heavenly Marquis Birdslayer, and his accomplishments were publicly announced.

“He renounced the darkness and sought the light, providing top-secret information about the holy lands to humankind, thus preventing major losses in the war! He is brave and ferocious, and has irreconcilable animosity with the holy lands. He hates all Devilbirds to the core of his being, and has killed over a hundred infiltrators from the Devilbird holy land!”

The imperial edict was a shock to everyone in the east.

Feng Lintao immediately became the focus of a lot of attention, and many species began running investigations into his background. Sadly, none of that was what Feng Lintao wanted.... Being the center of so much attention made him nervous and uneasy. But what made him even more uneasy was the shocking development that occurred a month later.

Humankind began achieving many victories in the small-scale battles with the Devilbird holy land. In fact, it almost seemed like the humans were privy to all of the Devilbirds’ war plans.

And every single time, the empress would reward Feng Lintao. In fact, a special guard contingent was assigned to him, which made it clear how important he was. There was no way that the Devilbird holy land would be unaware of the developments.

And yet, Feng Lintao was fully aware that whatever intelligence reports the humans were using to figure out the Devilbird battle plans had nothing to do with him.... More time passed, and then something truly shocking happened to Feng Lintao. He was appointed as a heavenly king!

The ceremony was to be carried out under the glow of the grand spell formation, right where the holy lands could see what was happening....

***

In the wilderness outside of the imperial capital were all of the prisoners of war the humans had captured from the holy lands. There were no less than 10,000 of them. Feng Lintao stood in front of the prisoners, clad in the garment of a heavenly marquis.

The empress’ voice rang out into heaven and earth. “My dear official Feng, you might not be human, but you are completely and utterly loyal to humankind. You have a steadfast heart and have earned awe-inspiring battle credit. Therefore, it is on this day that I appoint you as a heavenly king. You are now Heavenly King Birdslayer!

“I am aware, my dear official, that you hate the Devilbirds to the core of your being. Therefore, I shall celebrate your appointment to the rank of heavenly king with the blood of these Devilbirds. You may slaughter them now!”

Everyone looked on intently.

The holy lands. The humans. Xu Qing. All the other species. Everyone was watching.

As for Erniu, his eyes glittered with anticipation and excitement.

Feng Lintao’s heart was racing, but he didn’t let any negative emotions show on his face. Instead, he seemed very excited as he clasped hands in the direction of the imperial palace. “Thank you for making my wish come true, Your Majesty!”

1. There’s some funny wordplay in the nickname Erniu uses for Feng Lintao. Basically, the nickname is based on Feng Lintao’s surname (Feng), which means wind. If directly translated, it could be rendered as something like ‘Little Wind.’ But the pronunciation of the nickname, including the tones, are the exact same as the word for ‘crazy person, madman.’ Something similar in English that I thought of would be if someone was a psychologist, so you called them by the nickname “Little Psycho.” ☜

Feng Lintao had been appointed as one of humankind’s heavenly kings!

The matter caused quite a stir. The reality was that there had been quite a few battles between humans and the Devilbirds, and when it came to the total victory count, humans had the edge. What was more, humans had won some victories that could only have been possible if they had access to leaked information. In fact, humans seemed to be intimately familiar with all the details about the Devilbirds’ top experts, and even the complexities of their relationship networks.

The result was that the Devilbirds were starting to feel a lot of pressure. When it came to war strategy, the humans had the initiative. What was causing the biggest headaches for the Devilbird holy land were the spies!

Ever since the war broke out, the Devilbirds had been focused on trying to take down the humans’ unique spell formation. In order to make that happen, they sent out a lot of spies. Some spies went to remote locations, some immediately took action. Some of them went into hiding.

Regardless, all of them were focused on the goal of destroying the formation. It was a very important matter, and thus, they had a very detailed plan to follow in that regard. Unfortunately, over the time that had passed, their spies just kept being exposed one after another. And all of it started getting really bad... after Feng Lintao received his appointment to heavenly marquis. And after he became a heavenly king, it got even worse.

If that were all there were to it, it wouldn’t have been possible to prove Feng Lintao’s usefulness and value. After all, there were some things that Feng Lintao couldn’t possibly have known about given his status and identity, and the Devilbird holy land knew that.

However... when Feng Lintao was appointed as a heavenly king, he was offered the chance to slaughter 10,000 prisoners of war in a blood sacrifice. That was a monumental matter as far as the Devilbird holy land was concerned. After all, those prisoners of war had relatives, daoist partners, fellow disciples, and friends in the holy lands. As a result, the extended ramifications were dozens of times if not a hundred times more dramatic than the deaths alone. If those people had died on the battlefield, the people of the Devilbird holy land would have mourned, but wouldn’t have been infuriated. But for those people to be sacrificed... would instantly provoked intense hatred by everyone in the Devilbird holy land!

Thanks to the spell formation, the Devilbirds didn’t have very many human prisoners of war, and thus, trying to retaliate in kind was as effective as punching a cotton pillow. The public nature of the blood sacrifice was just another thing that made the Devilbirds so incredibly angry.

Feng Lintao was the one carrying out the execution, and he was also receiving an amazing reward for his action. Thus, he became the focus of every ounce of hatred for everyone in the Devilbird holy land.

As soon as the empress’ words rang out, and Feng Lintao offered excited thanks, the holy lands outside of the spell formation rumbled as numerous streams of divine will locked onto that specific area. The rage and killing intent in them was unprecedented. Whether or not it was a smart move to do something like this didn’t matter. What had happened... couldn’t be accepted! Their reaction was required as the response to an open plot that everyone could see! It was like a raging inferno that could ignite all heaven and earth.

Meanwhile, Feng Lintao was left reeling mentally. He was a crafty person, and was no fool. He had long since started to get nervous with how things were playing out. And now... although he seemed excited on the outside, the reality was that his heart was in complete chaos. It was not some sort of secret conspiracy. It was very obvious to him what was going on.

They’re forcing me down a path of no retreat! They’re ensuring that I’m utterly and thoroughly tied to humankind.... But that’s just the first part of their plan. The empress has a second goal.... Shē wants to make me so valuable that I’m priceless. The more shē packs it on thick, the better for hēr. Shē wants the vast majority of people in the Devilbird holy land to hate my guts.

When that happens, even the top leaders in the Devilbird holy land will realize that I’m being set up. There’s no way it’ll be lost on them that I couldn’t possibly be privy to so many intelligence reports!!

However... if everyone there hates me down to the core of their being, then it won’t really matter if I’m being set up or not. They’re painting a big target on my back.... The holy lands will be able to shift the blame for any losses onto me. At the same time, they can whip up their forces’ battle spirit into a frenzy. That will be beneficial to the holy lands’ interests.

The same goes for humankind. If the holy lands hate me that much, then I’ll become the perfect bargaining chip for the humans. If humankind starts to lose the war, they can offer to turn me over in exchange for some big advantage. After all, humans have been setting things up perfectly so that the holy lands hate me more than they hate the humans.

The leaders in the Devilbird holy land must surely realize this. And maybe they’re not happy about it. But in the end, they’ll go along with it because it serves their own interests. How ruthless! Whether it’s the humans or the holy lands, they’re full of rigorous schemes and deep foresight from bottom to top!

Despite such thoughts running through his head, Feng Lintao kept an excited expression on his face. He looked at the holy lands beyond the spell formation, and then looked at the imperial palace. Finally, he turned to the Devilbird prisoners of war. Stretching his hand out... he unleashed the full power of his cultivation base! freewebnovel.com

Heaven and earth filled with rumbling sounds as one-tenth of the group of Devilbird cultivators exploded. They were killed in body and soul!

Outside of the spell formation, the Devilbirds observed, and their rage burned.

Feng Lintao’s eyes were bright red, making him look completely and utterly bloodthirsty. As all the humans watched, he walked forward... and continued the slaughter. As the prisoners of war died, and as the reek of gore grew more intense, Feng Lintao seemed to be enjoying himself. And the holy lands cultivators on the other side of the spell formation were overwhelmed with grief and terror. ŘΆΝȯbЕš

All they could do was watch their fellow people die. There were members of the older generation, fellow disciples, offspring... and none of them died decent deaths. They died in the most brutal fashion.

But this was war, in which there was no such thing as right and wrong. From the moment the holy lands had come and launched their invasion, it was a given that things like this would happen.

Either you die, or I die.

The humans looked on coldly. It was the same with the other species present. Xu Qing did nothing to stop the events from unfolding. Erniu licked his lips.

Feng Lintao seemed to devolve into madness as he unleashed slaughter. At the moment, all he was thinking about was his own interests. All he cared about was what this massacre would lead to, not the process itself. It was after an incense stick’s worth of time that Feng Lintao killed the last of the prisoners. After that palm strike was complete, he stood there soaked in blood, his facial expression ferocious as he looked up at the holy land and laughed coldly.

After that, he turned to the imperial palace of humankind and bowed at the waist. “Thank you, Your Majesty!”

Both his ruthless actions and the words he spoke made clear his attitude. From the human perspective, there was nothing to find fault with. He had cooperated fully, and had turned himself into a target for the Devilbirds to hate.

When Xu Qing saw it all play out, his eyes glittered.

As for Erniu, he grinned. “The little lunatic really is ambitious and ruthless. We didn’t even have to force him. I have the feeling that he had everything planned out even before he defected. It was all to make sure that his fishing expedition works out the way he wants. In the coming days, little Ah Qing, I need to figure out a way to get five chunks of his flesh. That way I’ll be able to use my Grand Five Ox Essence-Tracing Grand Merciless Dao on him!”

Xu Qing nodded in agreement.

With that, the two of them melted into the crowd and disappeared.

***

Time slipped by slowly but surely. Half a month.

During that time, the clashes between humans and Devilbirds grew more frequent. And the holy land was sending in more and more spies. However, the spies now had a new mission in addition to dealing with the spell formation. They were also assigned to kill Feng Lintao!

As it turned out, there was another mass slaughter of prisoners in the half month that passed. What was more, many of the successes that humans achieved in battle were attributed to Feng Lintao.

As a result, Feng Lintao was now extremely famous in the east of Revered Ancient. What was more, he was considered public enemy number one in the Devilbird holy land. Innumerable Devilbirds hated him so much they wanted to eat him alive.

Given that, it was only natural that there were assassination attempts. In order to protect this most important government official, the humans assigned a personal bodyguard contingent to Feng Lintao.

As for Feng Lintao, he seemed to be on the side of humankind in body and soul. On multiple occasions, he even submitted requests to personally go out and kill enemies. It was as if he hated the Devilbird holy land even more than the humans did. However, the empress, in hēr benevolence and magnanimity, did not approve his requests to go out of the spell formation. Instead, he was asked to stay in the Imperial Region and hunt down spies. Feng Lintao seemed disappointed, but he fully complied with the empress’ imperial decrees. And thus, he hunted down spies and killed them in the most brutal and ruthless fashion. In the process, he ended up with some injuries, but nothing very serious.

And thus... another seven days went by.

At that point, the Devilbird Grand Emperor finally made an appearance, and the conflict went beyond small-scale battles and into full-scale war. Several Imperial Sovereigns took to the field, and numerous Smoldering Gods joined them. On the human side, Empress Summer Departure showed up on the battlefield, joined by the zombie emperors. Heavenly kings from various species unleashed their mightiness to bolster the war effort.

As a critical moment in the war arrived, and the Imperial Region was almost completely emptied of its most powerful forces, an assassination attempt was being carried out in the suburbs of the imperial capital!

There were two assassins, and they were both seven-world Smoldering Gods from the Devilbird holy land! They had been in deep cover for a long time, waiting for the right moment to strike. And when they struck, their attack was like a bolt of lightning.

Their target was none other than Feng Lintao, who was with his personal guard, on his way back from arresting some spies!

The assassination was perfectly timed and ruthlessly carried out.

Feng Lintao’s bodyguards all died. Feng Lintao himself was unable to flee. His fleshly body exploded, and his soul was shredded to pieces. His head was taken away as a trophy.

King Firecrusher desperately rushed over to help, but he arrived too late. Though he managed to take one of the Devilbird assassins captive, he wasn’t able to stop the other one from getting away with Feng Lintao’s head. In the end, all he could do was take away the corpses of the bodyguards who had pledged to protect Feng Lintao with their own lives.

When word got out, the forces of the Devilbird holy land rejoiced. The empress looked grim, but clearly wasn’t going to take the time to sit around thinking about the matter. The war... had to go on.

What no one noticed was what happened to the corpses that King Firecrusher took away. After they were locked up in a certain mansion in the imperial capital, the corpses suddenly turned illusory. Then they became scintillating motes of light that converged onto each other and became Emperor Eastglory. Those ‘bodyguards’ weren’t really bodyguards after all.

King Firecrusher wasn’t surprised by this. After bowing, he turned to look off into the distance, a meaningful smile on his face.

***

Beyond the Imperial Region and on the border of the Gray Sea Region, there was a remote mountain with a cave underneath it. The cave was overgrown and almost impossible to spot when passing by.[1]

A figure was seated cross-legged in the cave, cloaked in so much shadow it was hard to make out any distinct features.

A short time passed, whereupon the figure’s eyes opened, and they glittered with aggressive light. The figure then began to glow, causing light to seep out into the surrounding cave. Thanks to the light, it was possible to tell that this figure was a young man. He looked very similar to a human, except that he had a red mark on his forehead, made of a host of minute magical symbols. It was the mark of the Fardark people, although it quickly disappeared.

Neither the human empress nor the Devilbird holy land can possibly hold a candle to me! I never planned to stay among the humans for long. Although the empress’ scheme put me in a passive position, the reality is... that everything went according to plan! I finally managed to fake my own death! Now that everyone thinks I’m dead, I can use my Fardark body to finally break free of all this karma!

This person was none other than Feng Lintao!

Deathblade's Thoughts

Many thanks to Jimbo, Appledapple, and KazuyaAkihito for the reviews!

The Gray Sea Region was located right next to the Imperial Region of humankind. In the cave underneath the remote mountain there, Feng Lintao opened his eyes and cast his senses out in all directions. After confirming that everything in the cave was as expected, he breathed a sigh of relief. Then his eyes narrowed, all the while gleaming with a sinister light.

From the moment he had chosen to start working with the humans to stay safe from Lan Yao and Yue Dong, he had been working toward a specific goal. He wanted to make a big splash while with the humans. The point was to attract the attention of Lan Yao and Yue Dong, and then to ‘die’ a very flashy death. At that point, everyone would think he had perished.

It would be a case of slipping out of a predicament like a cicada sloughing its skin. He could get rid of the Devilbird half of his bloodline, and use his Fardark doppelgänger as his new true body. He would truly be able to make a clean escape, and turn his whole situation around completely. To reach this goal, he had made full use of both humankind and the holy lands.

Although there were some unexpected twists and turns, and I ended up being used by the humans to a certain degree, I was able to mostly stick to my plan....

Feng Lintao chuckled coldly.

Abandoning my Devilbird bloodline caused my cultivation base to fall some. I’m only in Nascent Soul at this point.... But that’s fine. It won’t take long for me to catch back up. It’s a price I’m more than willing to pay to earn freedom and my own life! That said, the people I’m dealing with are not fools.... My ultimate success is going to depend largely on how things develop in the world at large.

With such thoughts in mind, Feng Lintao maintained full vigilance as he flew out of the cave and sped along a pre-planned route to his next hiding spot.

Shortly after, two blurry figures appeared overhead. They were none other than Xu Qing and Erniu, who had used Erniu’s special essence-tracing ability to find the spot where Feng Lintao had reappeared in clone form.

No one could possibly see them as they hovered there. In fact, even gods would have a hard time noticing them. The reason was they were relying on the invisibility powers of the Wordless words. That same concealment technique had allowed them to remain unnoticed by the three gods of the Firemoons. Given that, there was no possible way that Feng Lintao would ever notice them.

“You have to give it to Little Fengy. We didn’t need to push him at all. He just went and turned into the best fish bait possible.” Erniu looked so pleased with himself he was licking his lips in anticipation. “Little Ah Qing, it wasn’t long ago that we were Yu Liuchen’s bait when he went fishing. I have to admit, I was a bit jealous of him! Hahaha! Now we can satisfy our own craving for a fishing expedition! Come on, let’s follow him.”

Xu Qing nodded. Together, he and Erniu zipped through the sky as they tailed Feng Lintao.

***

Seven days had passed.

During that time Xu Qing and Erniu didn’t interfere with Feng Lintao in any way. They just followed. They knew how paranoid Feng Lintao was, and didn’t want to do anything that could result in him noticing them.

Things went well for Feng Lintao. He did encounter a few dangers, including wild beasts, grues, and malicious cultivators. Sometimes he fled, sometimes he killed his enemies, and sometimes he hid. Regardless, he made it through all the dangerous situations.

Xu Qing and the Captain were right about Feng Lintao. He was naturally suspicious and paranoid. The fact that everything was going smoothly didn’t cause him to reduce his level of vigilance. Quite the opposite.

On the seventh day, when Feng Lintao was just about to leave the wilderness, he stopped to hide in a crevice in a cliff. Various expressions flashed across his face.

Things are going too smoothly. Something’s off! It’s true that everything is playing out according to plan. And I even considered the possibility of everything going smoothly. After all, I put a lot of thought into this. And the war is still going on. And yet.... I need to think things through very carefully and figure out if there’s something I missed.

After a lot of thought, Feng Lintao identified three concerning possibilities.

First, he wondered if it was possible that the humans had seen through his plan, and were now trying to catch him. Second, he wondered if the humans had let him go on purpose to use him as bait for a fishing expedition. Third, he wondered if Lan Yao and Yue Dong could possibly have figured out what he was up to.

If the humans realized that I came up with the plan to slip out of a predicament like a cicada sloughing its skin, then if they catch me, the worst that will happen is that I’ll lose my freedom. They won’t kill me, at least not for a while....

His eyes narrowed.

If they realized early on what I was doing, and let me go on purpose.... then they probably have some other goal besides just a fishing expedition. Could it be that they want to use me as bait to lure out all the spies? If so, then they wouldn’t make a public announcement about me being dead. They would spread rumors that I had fled. That would probably tempt the spies to come out of hiding to track me down....

I guess that means I’ll just have to pay attention to what happens going forward. That’s the only way I’ll be able to figure out if the third possibility is a reality.

Having reached this point in his train of thought, Feng Lintao took a deep breath, left the crevice, and headed into the heart of the Gray Sea Region. For the time being, he wouldn’t be traveling in the wilderness. Instead, he would start looking for cultivator cities in the region. The first order of business was to gather information. ℞aNƟВΕŝ

***

Another seven days had passed.

Feng Lintao was in a simple tavern in a bustling cultivator city, listening thoughtfully to the chatter of the crowd. He had learned some things in the past week. In addition to some general updates about the Devilbird war, he also heard some news about himself.

The humans had announced his death!

The fact that the humans have spread news about my death indicates that there’s not much of a chance they’re using me as bait.

He took a drink from his cup of alcohol.

However, it doesn’t completely eliminate that possibility.... There’s one more step I need to take to determine whether or not I’m being used as bait. Furthermore, I need to determine whether or not the humans actually think I’m dead, and whether or not they’ve sent people to track me down. Furthermore... I need to figure out whether or not I’ve fooled Lan Yao and Yue Dong. I need conclusive proof.

Feng Lintao’s eyes narrowed, this manner of thinking might be exhausting to some people, but it had become second nature to him. After drinking the rest of the alcohol, he crushed the cup, erased all traces of his presence, and then left the city.

From that point on, he stuck mostly to the wilderness. At no point did he experience anything that would indicate he was being followed by either the humans or the holy lands. It was really starting to seem like he had made a clean getaway.

However, Feng Lintao’s paranoid nature ensured that he wanted repeated proof. Therefore, he went out of the way to put himself in some extremely dangerous situations. In some cases, it seemed like he was just about to die, before somehow surviving by the skin of his teeth. That was how far he went to try to figure out if he was being followed....

Only after doing that several times, to the point where he was gasping on death’s door, did he finally believe that he was alone.

Finally, he breathed a sigh of relief and started moving a bit faster than before. It was hard to say whether it was bad luck or something else, but three days later, before he had fully recovered from the previous incidents... he ran into a wild beast with a cultivation base equivalent to Spirit Trove.

The beast viciously pursued him, putting him into a desperate situation that forced him to pull out all the tricks he could think of. Yet even then, he couldn’t shake it. In the end, the beast caught him and ripped him apart bite by bite before eating him. Then the beast went on its way....

A few days later, as that beast raced through some mountainous jungle, its eyes glittered.

It seems that I’m really not being followed secretly....

The beast flew on.

High above in the sky, Xu Qing and Erniu looked at the beast that had been parasitized by Feng Lintao. Both were dumbfounded.

“Little Fengy really is paranoid!” Erniu said with a sigh of admiration. “Just what did he go through in the holy lands that made him like this? I’ve already learned a thing or two from him!”

Xu Qing looked thoughtful as he watched the ‘beast’ disappearing over the horizon. “Given how paranoid Feng Lintao is, I have the feeling that what’s happened up to this point isn’t going to be enough to convince him he’s in the clear.”

“Seriously?” Erniu said, looking stunned. “Even after all that, you think he’s still worried about being followed?”

Erniu’s question was answered only five days later.

When the beast Feng Lintao had parasitized was passing by a forbidden ground, a host of tentacles from a godly entity shot out from inside. Blood sprayed everywhere as the tentacles burrowed into him and dragged him back into the forbidden ground. Unexpectedly, he perished!

Outside the forbidden ground, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered, all while Erniu looked on feeling a bit exhausted.

“I’m honestly not sure if the fellow died on purpose this time or not....”

Xu Qing looked at Erniu. “Eldest Brother, go ahead and use your essence-tracing ability again. According to my godly authority of sound, Feng Lintao’s life force fluctuations really were extinguished just now.

“But if he has another clone somewhere, then it’ll prove that he died on purpose just now. Since he can’t prove definitively whether or not he’s being followed, he might have chosen to die again just to play it safe.”

Erniu sighed. “Little Ah Qing, I’m suddenly starting to feel a bit bad for what Yu Liuchen went through back then....”

With that, Erniu yet again unleashed his Grand Five Ox Essence-Tracing Grand Merciless Dao. A moment later, he suddenly looked up and gritted his teeth. “That little punk! He really does have another clone! He just never activated it before, so it was essentially as dead as a corpse. That’s why it evaded my notice. But now I’ve locked onto it. It’s actually quite a distance away from here....”

***

In another part of the Gray Sea Region, a fleshly body was suspended in the depths of a swamp, surrounded by countless venomous insects. The power of life force surged within the fleshly body, all while a red mark appeared on its forehead. Its eyes... snapped open.

Rumbling sounds echoed out as a Void Returning aura rose up within the fleshly body. After that aura locked down the surroundings, the body shot out of the swamp and up into midair.

Now I’m completely and utterly safe! Even if Lan Yao and Yue Dong saw through my plan, and even if the humans figured out what was going on and either sent someone to follow me or use me as bait... it doesn’t matter! Either way, they’re powerless to do anything to me now!

Feng Lintao’s eyes glittered with cold light as he flew off. This time, he tapped into the full limits of his speed.

I’m leaving the east of Revered Ancient and going to the north! In the frigid north, in the 300,000 meter ice plains, I’ll start my cultivation again. And I’ll conform to the legacy requirements of Grand Emperor Fardark! When I come out of seclusion in the end....

Feng Lintao’s eyes narrowed and his expression became very sinister as he shot along at top speed.

***

Outside of the Imperial Region of humankind, in what had once been the Fardark ancestral land, there was another hidden cave. It wasn’t very far from where the golden rat had been holed up.

In that cave, two people sat cross-legged. One of them had a very withered fleshly body that lacked even a scrap of life force. In fact, it looked no different from a corpse. There was also a red Fardark mark on its forehead, which glowed with a faint red light that seemed to be getting darker and darker with each moment that passed. It would soon go out completely.

This was yet another clone that Feng Lintao had secretly prepared for use in his plan. Only he could possibly know how many such clones he had prepared. Of course, there were drawbacks to this method. There was a time limit involved. If the mark of the forehead went out, then the clone couldn’t be used. At the moment, that light was just about to go out.

In front of the corpse was another person, a middle-aged man, who was staring at the corpse with boundless sorrow. “You’re so heartless, Feng Lintao! You actually assimilated Miss Yue Dong’s little sister to fully activate your Devilbird half! Thankfully, the guilty can never escape justice from heaven! As the exalted Yue Dong has ordered, all of the Fardark criminals in the holy lands were sacrificed, and their blood led me to this Fardark clone of yours.... And now, the moment you activate this clone, you’ll be trapped with no way of escaping!”

The man gnashed his teeth in hatred of the clone in front of him. However, there was something about his emotions... that seemed off. He was acting similar to the way Lan Yao was acting. His thoughts had been altered, and his emotions tampered with. His karma had been confused. He had been turned into an emotional puppet that was in control of its own faculties!

If Xu Qing were around, he could use his authority of erasure and the power of those shears to see what was going on.... This middle-aged cultivator’s karma threads were in complete chaos. They were clumped together in a strange way that made the outline of a face.

And that face belonged to... Yue Dong! This was Yue Dong’s way of fishing!

Xu Qing and Erniu were using Feng Lintao as bait to try to hook Lan Yao. Meanwhile, Yue Dong was using Feng Lintao’s clone as bait to try to hook Feng Lintao’s true soul!

Feng Lintao was a very clever person. He had manipulated humankind, manipulated the holy lands, had faked his own death, and had then made a clean escape. He was also very cautious. After faking his own death, he faked his death again in order to erase all tracks leading to him.

And yet... he was still quite a tragic figure. Xu Qing and Erniu were using him as bait, all while Yue Dong was trying to reel him in like a fish. There was no other way to explain it than by saying that Feng Lintao was fated to be both bait and fish at the same time.

With that dual identity, he sped across the Gray Sea Region toward the north of Revered Ancient. He wanted to take advantage of the war between Revered Ancient and the holy lands to slip unnoticed into the frozen north. There, in the frigid ice, he would cultivate the legacy of Grand Emperor Fardark. He was confident that, given his talent and the preparations he had made, he would have a high chance of success.

The only sad thing is that I didn’t get much of that holy fardark nectar. With some more of it, my chances of success would have surpassed seventy percent!

Taking a deep breath, he accelerated, shooting off into the distance.

A few days later he passed over the border of the Gray Sea Region. Skirting the Imperial Region, he went through Firemoon territory as he left the east. Things were chaotic, and Feng Lintao was a bit jittery. He ran into various mutant beasts and grues. But being as careful as he was, he got through all of the situations safely. He was being very protective of his fleshly body. Add in the fact that he believed himself to be in a safe situation, he didn’t do anything risky like before.

High above, Xu Qing and Erniu noticed the change, and were happy that things seemed to be going a lot more smoothly.

After the most recent instance of Feng Lintao faking his death, they had to lock onto his new position again and race to find him. Seeing that Feng Lintao was now taking good care of himself caused Erniu to flash a pleased smile.

“Little Fengy is finally putting our hearts at ease. Is it that bad to just be a nice little piece of bait? What's the point of all the silly rigamarole? Did he ever take the time to consider the feelings of the person we’re fishing for? That’s why I have no choice but to say that this Feng Lintao is a far cry from us! I mean, look at how obedient we were when we were acting as bait!”

Xu Qing glanced at Erniu and thought back to everything that happened in the outer sea. Considering what had played out when Erniu opened his mouth back then, Feng Lintao wasn’t too bad at all. At the very least... he wasn’t causing terrifying gods to pop up or getting them devoured by a gigantic beast.

That said, Xu Qing always took his Eldest Brother’s feelings into consideration. Therefore, he didn’t quibble. And thus, the two of them remained concealed in invisibility as they followed the bait and waited for the fish to get hooked.

***

Another five days passed.

That was when things changed for Feng Lintao.

Previously, the Devilbird holy land had canceled the death warrant they put out on Feng Lintao. After all, he had been assassinated. But now, they issued the death warrant again! Along with the issuance of the death warrant came a dharmic decree. It was a public announcement that King Birdslayer of humankind, a traitor to the holy lands, wasn’t actually dead. He had faked his own death and escaped to parts unknown!

The news caused an immediate stir in the east. After all, thanks to all of the work the humans had done to put Feng Lintao’s name on the forefront of the war effort, he was extremely famous. And his death had enraged the humans. But now... the holy lands were saying that Feng Lintao had faked his own death!

The entire thing seemed absolutely bizarre. Outsiders had no way of knowing what was true and what wasn’t.

The death warrant came with a huge bounty that piqued the interest of countless cultivators. Anyone who earned the reward would get a chance to become an Imperial Sovereign! Species from both Revered Ancient and the holy lands could get the reward, as long as they killed Feng Lintao. All of the holy lands spies that were under cover in Revered Ancient were now on the move, looking for Feng Lintao.

Different forces throughout Revered Ancient reacted differently. That said, most seemed angry and dispatched people to stop an actual assassination from happening. As for what their true goals were, only they knew. The humans seemed very angry, and they immediately started investigating the matter. As the war outside of the spell formation continued, forces within the spell formation scattered to look for Feng Lintao.

The ones who were suffering the most were the people involved.

The jumpy Feng Lintao didn’t feel safe at all now, and had to be increasingly careful.

When Xu Qing and Erniu heard the news, they exchanged a glance.

“Come on, fish,” Xu Qing said, “bite!”

Erniu licked his lips, and his eyes glowed with blue light. “Interesting. This announcement from the Devilbird holy land could mean different things.... Was it the doing of Lan Yao? Or did the holy land leaders make the decision? Do they really want to kill Feng Lintao? Or... is this a case of beating the grass to startle the snake?” RaNǒ฿ЁS̩

Xu Qing looked down into the mountainous region where Feng Lintao was fleeing. Eyes narrowing, he coolly said, “When I was a kid, I would catch snakes by beating the grass. When the snakes are hidden, they’re hard to snatch. But when you beat the grass and startle the snake, they’ll crawl out into the open. Then you can just pick them up.”

Erniu frowned thoughtfully. “This whole thing still seems suspicious, though. The Devilbird holy land could have sent this news to its agents secretly. Why are they making such a big deal out of it...? We need to think long and hard about this situation, little Ah Qing. Something definitely seems off.”

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment. “We need to put ourselves in his shoes, Eldest Brother. If I was Feng Lintao, and I was in this situation, what would I do...? For one thing, I would worry that something was going on behind the scenes. And if I was being hunted like this, I would find a good opportunity to fake my death again in front of everyone. I’d do it as many times as necessary, and I would give them time to be convinced of the results. And what that means is that my biggest need would be time.”

Erniu’s eyes lit up with understanding. “That makes sense. In that case, it would make sense that the Devilbirds actually want Feng Lintao to do that. Given Feng Lintao’s paranoid personality, he would definitely act like the startled snake, and would react in kind. Therefore, the real question is what purpose the holy land has for pushing Feng Lintao into faking his own death again....”

As the words left Erniu’s mouth, he looked at Xu Qing. Xu Qing looked back at him. Both of them came to the same answer at the same time.

“Feng Lintao has a third clone out there!” Xu Qing said. “And most likely, Yue Dong and Lan Yao know where it is. Either that, or the holy land itself knows.”

“Exactly,” Erniu said. “And whether it's the holy land or Lan Yao and Yue Dong, the goal is for Feng Lintao to die and then be resurrected in his third clone. When that happens, he’ll fall into their hands! They’re manipulating Feng Lintao with his own paranoid nature! The more paranoid he gets, the harder it will be for him to see how they’re setting him up! freewebnovel.com

“He’ll come up with all sorts of suspicions and theories that he’ll think are beyond his control. And in the end, he’ll want to gain the initiative again. To be in control. Given that, I bet he's going to show his face soon. He's definitely not going to stay in hiding.”

As everything clicked into place for them, they started making plans for what to do next.

***

Feng Lintao really was paranoid to the core of his being. A few days later, he was still moving in concealment, and he was moving a lot more slowly.

His paranoid nature was really starting to show. When he encountered anything even slightly suspicious, he would blow it out of proportion and create a whole series of contingencies to deal with it. And the more contingency plans he created, the more suspicious things he noticed. The interconnections only continued to grow more and more complex....

On the sixth day, Xu Qing and Erniu realized that it would be easy for Feng Lintao to stay out of sight. But even as the search for him widened, he decided to show himself!

He did it in a clever way that made it seem like he had been successfully plotted against.

The moment he revealed himself, he started fleeing like mad. Then he used a number of different methods to cover his tracks behind him. But clearly, that wasn’t enough. People almost immediately locked onto his position, and thus, a big chase began in Firemoon Darkheaven territory.

The chase lasted for eleven days.... At that point, just as Feng Lintao was about to make it across the border between Firemoon Darkheaven territory and the south of Revered Ancient, he was stopped. He seemed exhausted and overwhelmed with despair, to the point where he looked crazy. He fought bitterly, but the outcome was predetermined. Though he killed many of his enemies, in the very end, one of the holy land’s spies cut him down.

Feng Lintao had died again!

***

In the cave in Fardark County, the red mark on Feng Lintao’s third clone was just about to go completely dark. But then, it flared brightly. The clone’s eyes opened.

An instant later, his face fell, and he lunged backward. At the same time, a cold snort echoed out as the middle-aged cultivator who had been waiting there reached out with his hand. Rumbling filled the cave as spell formations and other measures activated to prevent Feng Lintao from escaping. In an instant, he was bound in place.

There was also a gravitational force that latched onto Feng Lintao’s fleshly body and dragged him toward the middle-aged cultivator.

The middle-aged cultivator grabbed him by the neck and glared at him, his eyes burning with abhorrence.

“You finally showed up, Fellow Daoist Feng.”

Feng Lintao’s face drained of blood as he stared at the unfamiliar cultivator. He had never seen this person before, but he could sense something familiar about him. The abhorrence in his eyes matched the look and tone of voice that Yue Dong had used in the past.

Feng Lintao wanted to speak, but the man’s hands were clamped onto his neck like iron pincers, to the point where he couldn’t make a sound. His cultivation base was fully sealed, and the only thing he could do was wait to die. He suddenly realized what was happening. He knew why the Devilbird holy land had made that announcement about him, and he also realized where he had slipped up!

“Your paranoid nature is a strength,” the middle-aged cultivator said coldly. “But it’s also a weakness.”

Keeping Feng Lintao in his grip, he turned and left the cave. Once outside, he sped off into the distance.

***

It was currently sunset, and the light of evening filled Fardark County with peace and calm. The only movement came from the middle-aged cultivator as he sped across the landscape. There was something that cultivator hadn’t noticed. Specifically, there were a host of invisible threads coming off of Feng Lintao. They represented karma, essence, and fate. They led off into the distance until they reached Xu Qing and Erniu, who were following them at high speed.

Erniu was using his essence-tracing ability, and his eyes were shining. “The fish is finally hooked!”

The dao lineament in Xu Qing’s right eye glittered as he looked at the thread and coolly said, “This fellow is also very cautious. And he’s only a small fish.”

“Yeah,” Erniu said with a grin, “but follow the little fish, and you’ll find its owner soon enough. Little Ah Qing, why do you think Lan Yao and Yue Dong have worked so hard to target Feng Lintao this way? Do you think he has some sort of treasure we don’t know about?”

Erniu’s eyes narrowed, and he licked his lips.

As the dao lineament in Xu Qing’s right eye glittered, he looked off into the distance and coolly said, “If we want to know what treasures or other secrets Feng Lintao has, we can just ask him. And if he doesn’t provide the answer, we can ask Lan Yao and Yue Dong.”

Erniu chuckled darkly, and his eyes gleamed with anticipation. He and Xu Qing accelerated, maintaining the concealment of invisibility as they raced through the canopy of heaven.

***

A few more days went by.

During that time, the middle-aged cultivator who had captured Feng Lintao proceeded with utmost caution. He constantly shifted directions as he traveled, and he kept a close eye on his surroundings. Eventually, in a small random city somewhere, he handed Feng Lintao over to an unremarkable-looking old man. Then he flew away, and the fate threads that had formed the face of Yue Dong disappeared. His fate went back to normal, and he permanently forgot everything that had just happened.

As for the old man, he left the small city and continued the journey that had been started by the other cultivator. The same thing happened about five times over the following two weeks.

Every time Feng Lintao was handed over, a different person would take over and continue on the journey. There were different species involved. Sometimes it was a human, sometimes it was a Firemoon Darkheaven.

In that manner, all traces of passage were wiped out, and the karma with any pursuers was severed.

However, Erniu’s Grand Five Ox Essence-Tracing Grand Merciless Dao had been created by a god during one of Erniu’s past lives. It could even lock down onto the personhood of an Imperial Sovereign. Therefore, it didn’t matter how many times Yue Dong switched agents, in the end, Erniu was always able to keep track of Feng Lintao. Yue Dong never interfered, and they were able to track the target the entire time.

Eventually, Xu Qing and Erniu caught up with Feng Lintao and personally witnessed the strange handover procedure. At that point, Erniu’s pupils constricted, and Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed.

“Little Ah Qing, these people... are very unusual. There’s no way they’re Devilbird spies, right?”

Erniu had no authority to tap into. Although his essence-tracing ability was able to lock onto Feng Lintao’s fate threads, he wasn’t able to see how Yue Dong meddled with the emotions of the agents she was using, and he had no way to see their fate. freewebnovel.com

But Xu Qing could see such things clearly. The dao lineament in his right eye flickered as he looked at what was happening. After a moment, he came to a realization.

“Eldest Brother, the fate threads attached to those people are actually clumped together to form the face of Yue Dong....”

Upon hearing that, Erniu’s eyes shone. “Fate threads that form a face.... We’re obviously dealing with some sort of puppetry magic. Wait, could it be that Yue Dong is actually controlling Lan Yao?”

Xu Qing thought back to everything that happened with Yue Dong and Lan Yao when dealing with that golden rat. Although that alone wasn’t enough to prove anything, he definitely remembered how much Yue Dong had hated Feng Lintao.

“Let’s wait until the fish is fully hooked,” Xu Qing said. “Then we can see if Lan Yao has a similar face in her fate threads. Then we’ll know what's really going on.”

And thus, the two of them continued to follow the various cultivators that were traveling with Feng Lintao.

Eventually, snowflakes appeared in the sky. Looking down from above, it was possible to see the dark soil slowly being covered with white. The further one went north, the more ice and snow there was.

The person currently transporting Feng Lintao was a beautiful, middle-aged woman. She was obviously an important person in the area, as she was able to travel freely and without any obstructions.

Although this area was technically controlled by the Firemoon Darkheavens, it was very close to the border with the north of Revered Ancient. The territory controlled by the Firemoons was like a long, thin strip, with the top part bordering the north, and the bottom part connecting to Fardark County. Therefore, from the current position, it wasn’t necessary to rely on teleportation to reach the north of Revered Ancient.

As the beautiful woman moved onward, she eventually accelerated a bit. Apparently, she was very close to her destination. And that meant that the fishing expedition would soon conclude.

Three days later, the beautiful woman landed on top of a snow-covered mountain. There, she dropped to her knees and touched her head to the ground. She didn’t speak a word.

Feng Lintao’s eyes were shut tight, making him look like a corpse. In fact, the woman had set him down to the side, and he wasn’t moving at all. Silence prevailed for a time, with the only sound being the wind. Snowflakes drifted along.

Eventually... a person appeared within the snow and the wind. It was a woman.

She was graceful, with a skirt decorated with the image of a starry sky. Her facial features were as lovely as a hibiscus flower, and she had long, black hair that flowed down her back like a waterfall, drifting back and forth as she walked, and slowly interweaving with the falling snow. Her slender waist was particularly eye-catching. It was as lithe as a willow branchlet. Her long legs were barely visible through the flowing skirt, but that only made her more tempting to look at.

She was none other than Lan Yao! She had both the daintiness of a youth and the charm of a mature woman. Those elements mixed together to make her alluring in a way that could shake the soul. She also had a pair of snow-white wings behind her that added something holy to her.

Emerging from the snow and wind, she alighted on the mountain in front of the middle-aged woman.

“Well met, Fellow Daoist Lan,” the woman said respectfully. “I have accomplished the task you and Miss Yue Dong assigned to me, and have brought the heaven-damned Feng Lintao here with me.”

Lan Yao nodded. She looked at the unconscious Feng Lintao, and her beautiful eyes gleamed with hatred. She waved a jade-like finger.

Feng Lintao shivered and opened his eyes. He looked confused. It almost seemed as if he couldn’t believe what he was seeing. However, the reality was that his mind was already spinning as he analyzed the situation and tried to come up with plans to escape. The blank look in his eyes was a facade.

Unfortunately for him, Lan Yao knew him all too well. Before he could say a word, she waved her hand, and Feng Lintao’s face distorted. A scream escaped his lips. Blue veins bulged out on his face and neck. He even started trembling, as if... his soul were being ripped out of him!

“Lan Yao, wake up!” Feng Lintao howled. “Haven’t you noticed that your personality has changed since you and I first met? During this time in which the two of you were chasing me, I thought long and hard about the past, and I came to realize... that something is off about Yue Dong! Lan Yao... you....”

Lan Yao wasn’t moved by his words. She just kept her right hand extended as she extracted his soul. Feng Lintao’s eyes shone with despair as afterimages of himself popped up around him. It seemed that his soul really was about to be pulled out of him.

Right in that moment of crisis, just when Feng Lintao was about to run out of strength, he shouted into the sky in a bitter voice.

“Help, Your Majesty! Your Majesty, I know that you approved of the assassination attempt in human territory. You probably wanted to use me as bait.... Your Majesty, Lan Yao and Yue Dong hate my guts! Please, help!”

Lan Yao looked around. Everything remained the same. The wind blew and the snow fell. Nothing changed.

The despair in Feng Lintao’s heart grew stronger. In reality, he had no idea if the human empress was around. However, during his travels... his ruminations had left him with the increasingly strong suspicion that the humans were using him as bait.

Feng Lintao felt like his soul was about to be ripped to shreds. As the anxiety within him increased to a fever pitch, he decided to throw caution to the wind.

Feng Lintao in soul form trembled as Lan Yao’s hand clenched down onto him. In his despair, he shrieked, “Wake up, Lan Yao! You’re being controlled by Yue Dong! Lan Yao!!!”

However, there was more to the shriek than met the eye. Ignoring the risk of damaging his soul, he used that shriek to unleash a secret magic that formed a soul spike. The spike shot with incredible speed into Lan Yao’s forehead.

That soul spike attack had a name. It was the Fardark Soulstirring Technique! When used, the person who was struck would find their soul devolving into chaos, to the point where they couldn’t control it. All of a sudden, Lan Yao shivered from head to toe. Her eyes became blank, and the hand with which she held Feng Lintao loosened.

In the blink of an eye, Feng Lintao’s soul shot backward. The reality was that Feng Lintao would have loved for the humans to show up and interfere. But even if they didn’t, calling out to them was a tactic to escape from this deadly situation. Yet even as Feng Lintao’s soul began to speed away, Lan Yao’s eyes turned bloodshot. Looking up, she glared at him and spoke for the first time since she showed up on the mountain.

“Looking to die!?”

The moment the words left her mouth, her heart instantly filled with deep regret. Before coming here, Yue Dong had issued strict orders that she not speak. She wasn’t supposed to say even one thing. At first, she had obeyed completely. However, Feng Lintao’s soul spike had proved very effective, and the disturbance to her soul caused her fate threads to blur. In her moment of laxness, she had spoken those three words.

However, now wasn’t the time to ruminate on what she had done. Reaching out, she prepared to grab Feng Lintao.

Unfortunately, that was when a cool voice echoed out from the horizon.

“You finally spoke.”

The words became like an explosive sound wave, a tempest that converged on Lan Yao. Her face fell as a familiar figure walked out of the tempest.

He had a long robe, flowing hair, and beautiful facial features that formed the perfect contrast to the wind and the snow. He was none other than Xu Qing.

The moment Lan Yao saw Xu Qing, she took decisive action. She closed her eyes, whereupon her fleshly body withered up. In the shortest of moments, she collapsed into ashes! As it turned out, she was nothing but a clone! The moment the clone self-destructed, a storm wind blew through the area.

Xu Qing’s facial expression didn’t change. He had taken note of how Lan Yao didn’t speak, and that tipped him off that something strange was going on. It seemed obvious that the enemy had intelligence reports about him, and were aware that they should avoid making sound around him. That was why he hadn’t shown himself earlier. It was only when Lan Yao spoke that he stepped out into the open.

Although the enemy was only a clone, and her words had already dissipated, Xu Qing had heard enough of her voice... that her true form wouldn’t be able to escape him now. He looked up, sent out his god perception, and then unleashed his godly authority of sound. He used her words, the wind, the surrounding living beings, and all sound in the area... to track her down!

Feng Lintao had already fled over the horizon. But now, his face fell before he quickly flashed a fawning expression. Turning to the side, he said, “Is that you, Fellow Daoist Erniu? Xu Qing’s expression remained placid as he stood in the wind and the snow. Lifting his hand in the direction Lan Yao had disappeared, he gently closed his fingers into a fist. In that manner, he grabbed the air, pulling the dao lineaments there to him, and causing all of the sound that had once existed there to converge from all sides.

It was a process that required a much higher level of control of the godly authority of sound. He inquired of heaven: do you remember that sound?

He inquired of earth: where are the traces of that sound?

Countless images. Countless sounds. Heaven, earth, mountains, rivers. Living things. Wind and snow. All of them flashed through Xu Qing’s god perception, providing him with a very precise location in a mountain of ice!
