In the time of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity, immortal skills were created by a Grand Emperor by combining a host of other ancient arts and magics. That time period was one in which Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity’s war against the countless other species was reaching a critical point. Thanks to the immortal skills being distributed to humans and allied species, Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity ultimately conquered Revered Ancient, performing an amazing service for humankind.

However, the price to pay for the use of immortal skills was enormous. Immortal skills were categorized into levels, and the people who used them suffered ill effects depending on the level of the skill they used. Those who suffered minor injuries might lose some life force. Those who experienced serious injuries might end up with their foundation shattered.

After the war, the immortal skills were gathered into various Immortal Skills Halls, where they were sealed up as forbidden magics. Even later, when the broken face came, and Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity left with the emperors of various species, the immortal skills were taken away and circulated among the holy lands. That said, even in the holy lands, those who mastered them could be considered as rare as phoenix feathers or qilin horns.

Especially noteworthy was the fact that some of the immortal skills could only be passed down through a specific bloodline. In those cases, the vicious nature of immortal skills was made manifest, as the previous generation would die violently when the new generation took over.

And that was exactly the type of immortal skill being used by Yue Dong. It was Six Thieves Deceive Life! As her hands flashed in a double-handed incantation gesture, the seven-colored glow coming off her turned into a sea of light. Xu Qing and Erniu, who were both battering the Grand Emperor spell formation, felt fluctuations in their hearts and minds. Those fluctuations came from outside of them, shaking their thoughts and filling their bodies. They were unstoppable and impossible to defend against!

Yue Dong looked up at Xu Qing and Erniu. As the fluctuations rocked them, she lifted her delicate hand and... touched Xu Qing!

“Deprive the six sensory pleasures. Purge the seven emotions!”

1. Lu Lingzi: Lu is #47 on the list of common Chinese surnames. Ling means “insult, maltreat, intimidate, approach.” Zi is a utility character which essentially carries no meaning here. Madam Deathblade says the name sounds vaguely intimidating. ☜

2. I’m using “nearest and dearest” for a specific reason here. This newcomer actually uses the character for “wife” here. However, Chinese does not have plural nouns. The only way to tell if a noun is plural is by 1) looking at the context, 2) by adding specific numbers to them, or 3) in some other specific ways in certain circumstances. In any case, given the context, we have no way to know if this person is saying “wife” or “wives.” I think most people would probably assume he’s saying “wife,” but there’s no way to say for sure. There is no way to easily and smoothly create such vagueness in English with his question. This becomes relevant in the next chapter, and you’ll see why I went with this translation choice. ☜

As the only cultivator who had successfully become a god, the empress gave him a type of hope that defied description. In the time of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity, there was a distinction between east, west, south, and north in Revered Ancient. However, there weren’t clearly defined borders separating different areas. Dark Serenity himself didn’t want there to be hard-and-fast divisions between different parts of the land.

But then Dark Serenity left, and with the arrival of the broken face, everything changed. Catastrophe swept through the Revered Ancient mainland. Countless species experienced death and war. Some species ended up being wiped out forever, while other species rose to prominence. Eventually, there ended up being five top species.

In the east, the Firemoon Darkheaven people were the top species. In the north were the Northfate Kings. In the west were the Redland Nobleplexuses. To the south were the Netherworld Chasmcorpses. The central part of Revered Ancient was occupied by the number one species. Those five top species stood tall in Revered Ancient. They occupied the peak of the world.

Then Empress Summer Departure stepped into the Altar God level, and led humans to prominence. They allied with the Firemoons, and thus became one of the six top species in Revered Ancient. The result was that the east became stronger than the west, south, and north. And the east was now catching up to the number one species.

Thanks to the war with the holy lands, it was now possible to get an idea of how strong the various parts of Revered Ancient were. Not one holy land went to the central region. In the east, the fighting was restricted to areas outside of their defensive spell formation. As for the west, south, and north, the flames of war spread without cease, with deaths and casualties mounting on both sides.

That was especially true in the north. Over the better part of the past year, the four celestial-level holy lands that had come to the north waged war over and over again. Even if the Northfate Kings had been even stronger than they were, they would eventually have been put into a bad position. Taking in the north as a whole, the landscape now wasn’t pure white. Instead, there were many areas... that were stained with blood.

That was the state of things when Xu Qing and Erniu entered the north.

They felt the frigid wind, they saw the endless plains of ice, and they could smell the blood and gore. Even Erniu was uncharacteristically quiet. The whimpering wind seemed to carry with it a sense of decay and lifelessness. The ice below was red with blood, and it was possible to see quite a few corpses frozen in death. The mutagen wasn’t very strong here compared to other places. In the past, a lot of small sects had gathered here. However, when war came, some sects were conscripted while others moved away. “Well met, Master,” the disciple said. This was Long Jiu’s highest-ranking apprentice.

Noticing the anxiety on his apprentice's face caused Long Jiu’s eyebrows to shoot up. “Did something happen?”

“Master... just today another eleven inner sect disciples chose to leave the sect. As of now, we only have thirty-seven people left. What’s more, our cultivation resources are running extremely low. What are we supposed to do...?”

Long Jiu smiled. “Don’t worry. Everyone has their own aspirations. As for me, I’m just on the verge of achieving success.”

Upon hearing that, the apprentice sighed. He knew that his Master was in the throes of obsession, and that nothing could be said to dissuade him. All he could do was ask, “Master, how did the trip outside the sect go? Did you get anything good?”

Long Jiu laughed heartily. “One out of ten times that I leave the sect, I encounter danger. But I also encounter benefactors! This time, I got luckier than usual. In my travels, I actually ran into three benefactors!”

When the apprentice saw how pleased his Master looked, he thought back to all the tough times the sect had gone through and he couldn’t help but say, “Master, the disciples have run out of spirit stones for cultivation. Maybe... we should sell one of our command medallions? Just one...?”

Long Jiu frowned. “You’re as short-sighted as a rat! I’m going to rely on my own luck to become famous!

“You’d do well to know that the benefactors who saved me are all important people! With my command medallion in their possession, they’ll obviously realize how amazing I am. Then, when they visit the Northfate Kings, they’ll think of me, and then mention my name to the top experts of the species!

“At first, the important people in the species won’t have any idea who I am. But as more benefactors show up and talk about me more and more, the top figures in the Northfate Kings will eventually have a good impression of me. A very good impression! And then they’ll spread word in the species about who I am.

“Furthermore, every single benefactor can be considered an important connection for me. Because they saved my life, I have to pay them back. And that means karma! All the top figures will eventually become benefactors. Now, you tell me. How could I possibly not get famous this way? And once I am famous, how could I end up empty-handed?”

Long Jiu looked at his apprentice. It was true that his apprentice had been following him for years, and had gone through some really tough times.

“Just wait a bit longer,” he said comfortingly. “I have the premonition that by the time I give out the last seven medallions, it’ll be the time to strike! But enough of that for now. I need to rest and recover a bit. Afterward, I’ll go out and look for more benefactors.”

The apprentice wanted to say some more, but given his Master’s current mood, he knew that it wasn’t the time. That said, he had to admit that his Master had been quite lucky over the past few years. He had ended up in a lot of deadly chases, yet there always seemed to be an important person around to save him. As for his Master’s plan to become famous....

I just hope it works out.

The apprentice sighed again.

1. Long Jiu: Long is number 81 on the list of 100 common surnames. It means “dragon.” Jiu means “nine, ninth.” Hold on. 9x9=81. And the surname is the 81st most common??? Holy moly! Nine is a fairly auspicious number in China/Chinese, and of course, dragons are also auspicious, so combining them is... well, very auspicious indeed. Ever heard of Kowloon in Hong Kong? In Cantonese, kow is “nine” and “loon” is dragon, so basically, the reverse order of this person’s name. In Mandarin (as opposed to Cantonese) Kowloon is Jiulong. Incidentally, and this is a sort of minor obscure spoiler, but there is a character who has this same name in the classic wuxia novel I translated Dragon King with Seven Stars, although in that novel it seems to treat it more like a nickname than an actual name. And there is a connection between that character and another character in my other translation Seven Killers. ☜

In the lands where the east met the north, far beneath the glaciers, everything was pitch-black.

Successive sheets of ice formed the sky over the river, the water of which was bone-penetratingly cold. Considering that the air was also freezing, it was no surprise that the surface of the river was constantly freezing up.

However, the water was unusual, and had the aura of a god in the form of mutagen. It also had ordinary spirit power. Because of the varying interactions between all those things, the freezing point varied wildly. The further down one went, the more the freezing point surpassed understanding.

Even though Xu Qing and Erniu couldn’t sense even a bit of heat, and had to rely only on their cultivation base to keep themselves alive, the river water still didn’t freeze solid.

As they got deeper, the cold got more intense.

When they were down to about 30,000 meters, Xu Qing stopped briefly. If he went further down, his fleshly body would be able to sustain the cold, but his soul would start to feel the pressure. That said, it would definitely last until at least 60,000 meters.

Unfortunately, Feng Lintao and Yue Dong were at their full limit. If he continued, the two wouldn’t be able to unveil the immortal skill or the legacy.

In contrast, Erniu’s miraculous nature was fully on display. He... wasn’t being affected at all! In fact, Xu Qing got the feeling that Erniu felt more comfortable here than he did outside of this coldness.

Upon noticing Xu Qing looking at him, Erniu proudly said, “Your Eldest Brother will always be your Eldest Brother.”

Xu Qing’s look of admiration made Erniu feel incomparably pleased. However, he also knew that Feng Lintao and Yue Dong couldn’t go any further down.

Erniu and Xu Qing exchanged a glance, and in doing so, confirmed with each other that this was the place to activate Feng Lintao’s legacy.

Erniu waved his hand, causing Feng Lintao’s soul to appear in the ice river.

Feng Lintao immediately began to tremble, and it was obvious that he was already starting to freeze. An intense sensation of deadly crisis filled him, prompting him to unleash every scrap of soul power possible to fight back against the cold. The results were minimally effective.

Eventually, Feng Lintao had no other choice than to float up until he was higher than 9,000 meters before he was able to stabilize himself and stop the freezing process.

“So useless!” Erniu snapped with a frown.

Feng Lintao felt more than a little humiliated. He wanted to point out to Erniu that he was in soul form, without a fleshly body, which meant that he was obviously much weaker than he should be. And he wasn’t in this situation out of choice. It was because of everything that happened with the fishing expedition.... What was more, the way the two of them had sealed him along the way made him even less strong.

But in the end, he didn’t dare to give voice to all of that. Burying such feelings deep inside, he plastered an ingratiating look onto his face. Truth be told, what really worried him was the possibility that, after he handed over his legacy, he wouldn’t be valuable anymore.... And if he displeased his captors now, then it was entirely possible that they would put him to death then. He had put a lot of thought into how to extricate himself from the current situation. But in the end, he hadn’t come up with any solid plan.

Seeing Erniu and Xu Qing looking at him like tigers eying prey, Feng Lintao trembled inwardly. Not daring to be uncooperative, he cleared his thoughts and turned to Xu Qing.

“Fellow Daoist Xu Qing, going forward, I’ll act in complete sincerity and wholeheartedness. I won’t hide anything. I won’t try to pull any tricks. I’ll do everything possible to produce my legacy and help the two of you seal authority.

“I have no demands. I don’t even expect to get my freedom. I just want to stay alive. You can even enslave me if you’d like. That’s fine! And therefore, Fellow Daoist Xu Qing... I trust you! And I just hope you can promise me one thing!”

Feng Lintao wasn’t finished, nor had Xu Qing responded to him.

But Erniu, feeling a bit miffed, jumped in by saying, “What’s that supposed to mean? You don’t trust me?”

Feng Lintao shivered deeply and was about to offer an explanation when Xu Qing started talking.

“I’ll do everything in my power to get you back to humankind when this is all over. As for whether you live or die afterward, that’s going to be up to the empress.”

Xu Qing’s words caused Feng Lintao to calm down a bit and even breathe an inner sigh of relief. If Xu Qing had offered some long and glib response, it might have had the opposite effect. But his response seemed succinct and sincere.

Feng Lintao’s eyes filled with determination, and he didn’t make any more requests. He quickly performed a double-handed incantation gesture and then touched his forehead. His soul body shone with dazzling light, making him seem like a star within the pitch-black river. ŕÂNȰBƐS

Strands spread out, floating around his soul form, connecting with each other to make the shape of a flower. The flower even emanated a strange fragrance. It started expanding....

A primeval aura began to build on it. It was... the aura of a Grand Emperor. In the outside world, that aura would have been illusory. But here in this icy river with frigid surroundings, it was corporeal.... It became a ring made of countless sealing symbols, surrounding Feng Lintao and rotating constantly. The aura shone onto the flower. In the end, the ring, like the external manifestation of the flower, turned into a flower itself!

The sealing marks that made up the flower all pulsed with a sensation of a gathering dao. Close examination would reveal that the sealing marks were all empty, without any will, nor any sort of magical technique. All they had was the pure accumulation of a foundational dao.

“That is the manifestation of Grand Emperor Fardark’s authority. It’s empty, and can seal any appropriate magical technique or divine ability, and thus turn it into authority! It won’t work with all magical techniques. And every failure will cause the legacy sealing symbols to disappear forever. Therefore, succeeding on the first attempt is the best outcome.”

As Feng Lintao spoke, he grimaced. Clearly, manifesting this legacy in these surroundings caused him a lot of pain. “Fellow Daoists, I can only last for the time it takes an incense stick to burn! Quickly, decide which magical technique you want to seal!”

Xu Qing looked at Erniu. At this point, they could proceed with Yue Dong’s immortal skill....

“Yue Dong was working on her plan for a long time,” he said quietly, “and definitely made preparations to ensure she would succeed.”

Erniu’s eyes narrowed. “Something just occurred to me, little Ah Qing. Was Yue Dong’s plan really just to turn that immortal skill into authority...? Given all of our dealings with her, I get the feeling that her plan was probably much more complicated. Do you think it’s possible that there is more to her plan...? Maybe sealing authority was only the first step for her.”

Xu Qing considered the possibilities. For one thing, he thought back to how Yue Dong and Lan Yao had been working together. If Yue Dong wanted Feng Lintao for that purpose alone, then there didn’t seem to be any need to bring in the Lan Clan and Lu Lingzi. She surely could have come up with some way of avoiding dealing with the Lan Clan, but still getting Feng Lintao’s legacy. But she chose the path that would actually bring great benefit to the Lan Clan if she succeeded.

“She definitely had another objective!” Xu Qing said.

He and Erniu exchanged a glance. Then Xu Qing waved his hand, causing the shadow-wrapped Yue Dong to appear in the river.

Yue Dong shivered from the cold, and her eyes overflowed with venom. However, with Little Shadow controlling her, she couldn’t fight back. And Little Shadow could also force her to speak.

“Milord, this woman’s memories don’t contain any other purpose. Turning the immortal skill into authority was her only objective.”

Xu Qing looked coldly at the hate-filled Yue Dong. “Force her to use her immortal skill,” he said coolly. “Use the legacy authority to seal the immortal skill, and nothing else!”

Little Shadow complied. Yue Dong’s hands flashed as she unleashed the immortal skill of Six Thieves Deceive Life. As seven-colored light glowed, the venom in Yue Dong’s face turned into anxiety. However, there was nothing she could do other than watch her fleshly body act beyond her control to activate the immortal skill.

Soon, she was shimmering with seven-colored light, which created a dazzling sea around her and covered over the flower outside of Feng Lintao. Within the empty marks, color began to appear. Seven-colored light built up, until finally Little Shadow forced Yue Dong’s two hands up to sever the light.

The seven-colored light was ripped away from Yue Dong. All of it poured into the legacy flower of Feng Lintao, filling the sealing marks, and causing the flower itself to shine with seven colors.

Feng Lintao looked at the flower with mixed feelings. He felt the impulse to take it for his own. But an instant later, Xu Qing appeared behind him, and Erniu appeared in front of him. Xu Qing looked on coldly. Erniu smiled enigmatically. And then Feng Lintao had no choice but to put away such thoughts.

“Fellow Daoists,” he said sincerely, “the bestowal of holy fardark nectar will provide stability. That nectar is hidden in my soul. Being in this current state, no outsider could extract it. It would influence the formation of the authority. Therefore, I hereby request that you release the seals binding me so that I can take it out.”

Feng Lintao worked hard to make sure his expression was one of full sincerity. This was his final trump card. Unfortunately, he had made a very big miscalculation.... Xu Qing also had holy fardark nectar. And he had a lot more than Feng Lintao did....

Xu Qing pulled out a bottle, uncorked it, and then poured out ten times as much holy fardark nectar than Feng Lintao could have. There was plenty for the seven-colored flower, as the flower rapidly solidified and went from being illusory to being completely real.

Xu Qing reached out. Cracking sounds rang out as the flower separated from Feng Lintao and flew to Xu Qing. He grabbed it.

When Feng Lintao saw this scene play out, his heart lurched. So much....

He could instantly speculate about what was going on. Back in the Fardark Cistern, there hadn’t been nearly that much fardark nectar. Obviously Xu Qing must have taken it away earlier! His mind and heart reeled as countless emotions swept through him. In the end, he had no choice but to suppress them. He put away his humiliation and bitterness, and forced a fawning expression onto his face. Right now, all of his hope rested in the seven-colored flower.

The flower pulsed with a majestic aura, and the sensation of a great dao accumulation. It was becoming true authority. Right now, it was masterless, and thus, whoever fused with it would gain a dao lineament. Good fortune like this, if made public, would cause innumerable cultivators to descend into madness. Even gods would be moved.

But there’s only one available...

If Feng Lintao had the option, he would fight with his blood brother to get something like this, much less a fellow disciple. But what happened next caused his heart to pound.

Xu Qing took the seven-colored flower and tossed it to Erniu. Erniu took it, examined it, and then looked at Feng Lintao. Feng Lintao’s ingratiating expression grew stronger.

Erniu grinned. “I’m going to show you a little magic trick, Little Fengy. To be honest, this magic trick is only possible due to your great generosity.”

As Feng Lintao looked on in confusion, Erniu glanced at Xu Qing. It was on the journey to this place that he had figured out a way to deal with the fact that there would only be one portion of authority.

Xu Qing waved his hand, causing his sageheaven god vine to appear and fly over to Erniu. Erniu threw out his own sageheaven god vine. The two god vines had once been part of the same whole. Later, Erniu cut that whole into two halves. Now that they were close together again, they fused, once again becoming whole.

As Feng Lintao reeled in shock, Erniu took the seven-colored flower and tossed it toward the god vine. The god vine opened its mouth and devoured the flower. An instant later, seven-colored light flowed across the vine, turning into a dao lineament that covered the entire thing. After, the vine split into two parts again.

One merged with Xu Qing, the other with Erniu. Both of them shivered and closed their eyes, whereupon their auras started to climb.

The immortal skill of Six Thieves Deceive Life had been perfectly split in half!

Feng Lintao’s heart sank, all while filling with a sensation of extreme helplessness. Off to the side, Yue Dong’s eyes shimmered with similar emotions. As of this moment, for the first time in their lives, these two people were completely in sync.

In the end, they couldn’t change a thing. Both were shaken for a few dozen breaths of time. Then Xu Qing and Erniu both opened their eyes at the same time. Both immediately turned to look at Yue Dong.

“Oh, so that’s how it is,” Erniu said. “So you hid your true objective within the immortal skill. It was hidden so well... that without forming authority, it would be extremely difficult to uncover.

Xu Qing’s eyes flashed. “No wonder Little Shadow couldn’t find it in your memories....”

Yue Dong really did have a much more complicated plan. And that plan was the reason why she had chosen to cooperate with the Lan Clan. In a critical moment, she had taken that concept out of her own memories and transferred it to the immortal skill, thus preventing Little Shadow from detecting it.

Now, with Xu Qing and Erniu working together with authority, they figured it out.

Assimilating Feng Lintao’s legacy and using it to turn the immortal skill into authority was actually only the second step in Yue Dong’s plan. The first step was working with the Lan Clan to draw out the Grand Emperor’s apprentice, all while conspiring to seize Feng Lintao’s legacy. The second step was to absorb Feng Lintao, and turn Six Thieves Deceive Life into authority.

The third step was her true objective. Her agreement with the Lan Clan was that, after the Grand Emperor’s apprentice had his devil-eye extracted, she would get his fleshly body to turn into an emotion puppet. Then she would use that puppet to work with the Lan Clan to get close to the Grand Emperor’s secluded meditation facilities. The ultimate objective was to abscond with the supposedly perished Grand Emperor!

It was impossible to say what tricks the Lan Clan had up their sleeve to make them fully confident in succeeding. But they had revealed to Yue Dong that the Grand Emperor wasn’t ‘suspected’ to be dead. He really was dead. However, the secluded meditation facilities had been tightly sealed. The dao accumulation and cultivation base the Grand Emperor had left behind, if absorbed, could be used to advance by leaps and bounds in one’s cultivation. If things went as planned, she would be able to do just that.

Meanwhile, the Lan Clan would acquire the Grand Emperor’s other legacies and his remaining cultivation base. Then, Yue Dong could use her authority to seal the Grand Emperor’s corpse, and refine it into a Grand Emperor zombie puppet.

It was a complicated plan, with plenty of opportunities for either side to scheme against each other. After all, Yue Dong only had limited usefulness in the entire thing. But in the end, the Lan Clan still chose to work with her....

Of course, not all the details were visible to Xu Qing and Erniu. And they had no idea where such details were hidden. Perhaps they were in the emotions of some other person, or perhaps they were with the Lan Clan.

Regardless, even Erniu still found the plan to be a completely crazy one. It was actually quite moving to him.

“This Yue Dong is totally crazy! I mean, completely daring! I have to say... I’m a fan!” Eyes shining, he turned to Xu Qing. “Little Ah Qing, since Yue Dong is obviously connected to us by destiny, and since we’ve already reached his point in her plan, I say, why not help her finish things up? If we don’t, our consciences will definitely start bothering us.

“Besides, if that Grand Emperor’s secluded meditation facilities really have some dao accumulation and cultivation base that can be considered a destined opportunity and good fortune, then we might as well give it a shot. After all, cultivating the ordinary way is just too slow!

“There will be dangers, but it’s been a long time since we pulled off a really big job. If we back down now, then our dao hearts are definitely going to become unstable!”

Erniu licked his lips as a crazy look overtook his eyes.

The fact that Erniu spoke of the dao heart becoming unstable just showed how absolutely determined he was to go to the Devilbird holy land.

Xu Qing was aware that he had essentially fallen into a rut when it came to cultivation base progress. He had over a hundred. Although that would give him incredible battle prowess, it also was holding him back significantly.

The only way to break through into the Smoldering God level would be for him to gain enlightenment of all those types of authority. He would be a type of Smoldering God without parallel in history, surpassing all others in that level. In fact, he would be immeasurably close to the level of an actual god. Seven days later, Long Jiu stood atop an expanse of shattered ice, his face pale. He looked neither servile nor overbearing as he clasped hands and bowed to an old man who was a one-world Smoldering God.

“Your humble servant is disciple Long Jiu from the Northfate Kings. Many thanks for the grace of saving my life, Senior! The kindness you have shown me will be forever engraved on my heart. Benefactor, if you ever come to visit the Northfate Kings, you can use this medallion to track me down. Unfortunately, I’m on an important errand right now, and therefore, I must hurry on my way.”

With that, he placed a command medallion down in front of him, took a few steps back, and bowed. Then he sped off into the distance.

The Smoldering God looked at the command medallion with the same expression as Erniu on that day recently....

Up in the canopy of heaven was Xu Qing, his aura concealed as he watched what he was saying. He had tracked down Long Jiu on the very first day he went looking for him. After that, he followed him secretly and learned his routine.

This Long Jiu... had encountered three dangerous situations that could easily have proved fatal if he slipped up in any of them. In each situation, someone eventually came along and saved him. None of the situations seemed to have been set up by him. They all seemed to be random chance. Every time someone saved him, Long Jiu would give them a command medallion.

With each medallion he gives out, his godly authority fluctuations get stronger.... That godly authority is almost mature....

Xu Qing kept his eye closely on Long Jiu as he followed him around. After a few more days of observation, he got some more information.

Why would a godly authority related to good luck manifest on a cultivator who doesn’t have even a hint of godliness? It’s very clear that this godly authority is fragmented. Incomplete. It’s as if some unknown entity has taken the actual godly authority of good luck, broken it into parts, and scattered it. One of those parts is now inside of Long Jiu.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. The only way to know the details would be to get more familiar with the godly authority in him.

Xu Qing took a step forward and then vanished. He continued to secretly follow Long Jiu around for about half a month.

Similar situations occurred with Long Jiu several times. Eventually, he only had a single medallion left. As Xu Qing looked on, he ran into another benefactor. Long Jiu bowed, offered thanks, handed over the medallion, then left. Shortly after, the godly authority fluctuations on him erupted.

They didn’t spread out very far, but they did cause ripples to appear in the sky. An aura of return then rose from Long Jiu, like something calling out to beyond the heavens....

Long Jiu himself didn’t notice that. He just kept going on his way, his flesh clearly withering, and his quintessence fading. It was as if his soul, body, and everything else about him had turned into nutrients for another.

They were threads that began stretching out to the starry sky. All the while, he was unaware of what was happening. His own perceptions were being clouded.

When he lost about half of his total energy, he slumped forward unconscious, a contented look on his face....

Around that time, Xu Qing stepped over to Long Jiu’s side, reached out, and touched his head.

“The three poisons are foolishness, love, and desire. Renouncing life and choosing the heart. That is called foolishness. Having a thing, then letting it go, yet continuing to obsess about it. Fearing that others will surpass you. That is called jealousy. Seeing someone’s goodness, but not using it to safeguard their splendor. That is called envy.

“The five dogs are stinginess, greed, foolishness, depravity, and austerity. The inability to abandon things. That is called stinginess. Having insatiable desire. That is called greed. Renouncing the rules of life. That is called foolishness. Arguing without understanding the facts. That is called depravity. Renouncing the three paths of hell before attaining lifelessness. That is called austerity.

“As for the seven banes and eight evils, Yue Dong doesn’t really understand them. Her memories are mostly focused on the western Devilbirds’ Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

“That particular immortal skill can be summed up in this way: the stingy dog cleaves to a place and loses treasure; the greedy dog cleaves to a place and is bound; the foolish dog cleaves to a place and falls into death; the depraved dog cleaves to a place and falls into hell; the austere dog cleaves to a place and forever loses the body.

“It sounds like a very extraordinary magic. Deathblade's Thoughts

You might remember a translator note many chapters ago in which I mentioned that some chapters take a lot longer to translate than others. This is such a chapter. Erniu’s explanation of the suite of immortal skills (some of which is based on some real Buddhist doctrines/sutras), was so complicated that translating that one section took probably 3 times as long as an ordinary chapter. And yeah, I’m just talking about that one section, not even the rest of the chapter. What’s more, I had to come back four or five times to make changes based on later wordplay of certain sections. Suffice it to say, this chapter was very frustrating. I don’t get paid more if I spend more time on a chapter, but that’s just how things work in this industry. I hope the effort I put into it made for a good reading experience. And yes, there are things in this chapter that will be important later, heh heh....

Deathblade's Thoughts

This chapter is very nearly 1,000 characters longer than average.

To the Devilbirds, whether they were from the east or the west, the Immortal Skills Halls were places of pure holiness. The grand immortal adept of every generation might not necessarily have an Imperial Sovereign cultivation base, but in terms of status, was just as important as an Imperial Sovereign.

Nowadays, the decline of the eastern Devilbirds, as well as the death of their grand immortal adept, had caused the eastern Immortal Skills Hall to lose some of its glory. The immortal adepts there were constantly at odds as they tried to outdo the others and become the new grand immortal adept.

Although Yue Dong was the apprentice of the grand immortal adept, she wasn’t the only person who qualified to be the successor. That was why she’d started working with the Lan Clan. If the crazy plan to get Grand Emperor Netherflame’s corpse worked... then she wouldn’t just qualify to take over the Immortal Skills Hall. She and the Lan Clan could theoretically seize control of all the eastern Devilbirds. But now... there were some dramatic developments.

Thankfully, Erniu was around. He was a virtuous person who liked to help others, and therefore, he wanted to see Yue Dong’s plan through to the end. Erniu actually wasn’t very surprised to hear that Xu Qing wasn’t planning to join him.

“You’re right,” he said. “Settling your identity is the most important thing. You’ll come back right away?” freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing shook his head. He had his own things to deal with. And similar to his Eldest Brother and the Immortal Skills Hall, this situation was something that had been bothering him for a long time. He had thought about the issue for a long time, but had never figured out a way to deal with it. But then... Sir Blood Dust showed up, and he got an idea.

“I’m not sure when I’ll be back,” he said. “That Sir Blood Dust has something of great interest to me, Eldest Brother. I’m going to go look more closely into the situation. Once I have the information I need, I’ll track you down.”

Of course, Erniu was now feeling very curious. “Something of great interest? What exactly?”

Xu Qing looked off into the distance. He could sense that the tracking mark he had put on Sir Blood Dust was already wearing off. Thankfully, he had also put one of Little Shadow’s shadow eyes on him. That meant that he would have no trouble tracking down Sir Blood Dust. After confirming that he could sense Sir Blood Dust’s location, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered.

“Something karmaless,” he said. With that, he took a step forward and then turned to leave.

“That’s fine,” Erniu said. “After all, given the level of your cultivation base, little Junior Brother, as long as you’re careful, you should be fine. Besides... here among the eastern Devilbirds, we have Lu Lingzi to back us up, right?”

Licking his lips, Erniu turned in the direction of the Immortal Skills Hall and started moving.

In that manner, Qing and Niu split up to work on their own respective tasks.

A few hours later, Xu Qing flew through the air concealed in invisibility. Using his connection to the shadow eye, he was making his way through the lands of the eastern Devilbirds. As he got closer and closer to his quarry, his heart started to beat faster. The moment he encountered Sir Blood Dust, he sensed something special about him. It was quite unexpected. That was why his heart was racing.

Right now, the biggest difficulty he was facing was his own cultivation base. He had died in the imperial capital of humankind, whereupon his Master resurrected him in a new body created from the flesh of the broken face. Although he had benefited greatly because of that, it had also created certain shackles. One of them was the fact that his soul and fleshly body were not fused.

The most urgent problem now was that his cultivation base was stuck! If he wanted to break out of the Void Returning level, then he needed all one hundred bits of godly authority in his sea of consciousness to be shining brightly. Right now, that was a problem.

He wanted to get stronger. He wanted to reach Smoldering God. Whether it was because of the threat posed by the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan, or the war that gripped Revered Ancient, he needed to get stronger. That was the only way to make true progress. What was more, Xu Qing wasn’t interested in constantly relying on the help of his Master. Unfortunately, godly authority wasn’t something he could get just by working hard.

Whether it was gaining enlightenment or seizing authority from other gods, they were things that weren’t certain. When it came to improving his cultivation base, Xu Qing couldn’t just accept uncertainty.

This body is strong enough to keep me safe from anything under the Imperial Sovereign level. And it has limitless potential.... But it’s also created some limitations for me. Godly authority... can improve my battle prowess. But each instance of getting some more requires a destined opportunity. My successes are because of godly authority. But my challenges are because of godly authority.

He had thought a lot about how to deal with the situation, and had come up with some good ideas.

Back in South Phoenix, he had also consulted with Master Seventh, who had informed Xu Qing that when dealing with a path of unlimited potential, it was impossible for anyone to give completely accurate advice. He would need to do his own study and research. The only thing Master Seventh had been able to provide was the profound sun immortal light to fuse his soul and body.

In the last few months in the imperial capital, Xu Qing had been focused on Feng Lintao, but had also been spending time thinking about how to deal with his challenging situation. He had come up with a good idea, which was to make a clone that could practice cultivation separate from his true form. The goal would be to work toward a breakthrough.

Ultimately, he gave up on that idea, as he realized that using a clone for cultivation would be highly unlikely to work.

The main reason was that he simply had too many karmic connections. There was karma from the outer sea. Karma connecting to gods. Karma with Zi Qing. And most importantly... there was karma with the broken face of Eminent Desolation. Even if he did create a clone, all of that karma would be around, and it would cause problems for the clone. Because the clone couldn’t escape from that karma, it would ultimately lead to the clone’s destruction. The Grand Emperor’s shears were sharp, but not sharp enough to sever karma like that.

Because of all that, Xu Qing had given up on the idea of using a clone. But then he ran into Sir Blood Dust!

When Sir Blood Dust showed up, and they clashed inside of those blood clouds, Xu Qing noticed something unusual. The fate threads attached to Sir Blood Dust were different from those of an ordinary person. When Xu Qing used his authority of erasure, he could see that Sir Blood Dust’s fate threads had some sort of white dust on them. It was very faint. But it was there, and it was the first time Xu Qing had seen anything like that.

The young man in the fancy robe had interrupted Xu Qing and Erniu when they used Six Thieves Deceive Life on Sir Blood Dust.

But during the process of using the immortal skill, Xu Qing sensed that white dust, and could tell that it was fighting back. It made it difficult for the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures to be sealed.

It was something very unique that caught Xu Qing’s attention. When the young man in the fancy robe interfered, Xu Qing intentionally let Sir Blood Dust escape. Afterward, it had seemed like he was just quietly following along as they traveled. But as he listened to what the young man said to Erniu, he also pondered the situation with Sir Blood Dust. Eventually, he reached a conclusion.

Something karmaless.

Around evening, as the glow of the setting sun faded, he looked at a low-lying mountain off in the distance. He started moving in that direction.
