In that low-lying mountain was a mansion grotto, outside of which were hosts of spell formations that concealed the place and created powerful defenses.

Inside the mansion grotto was Sir Blood Dust, seated cross-legged in meditation. After escaping from Xu Qing and Erniu, he didn’t return to his original mansion grotto. After purging himself of any tracking marks, he switched mansion grottos a few times in a row before settling on this one.

His face was ashen, as if he had sustained damage to his vital energy. Veins bulged on his face, and fluctuations of instability pulsed off him. Previously, he had seven major worlds. But now he only had five, and they were all very dim. He had lost two of them after detonating them in the fight with Xu Qing and Erniu.

Something was off about Yue Dong! That slut was doing a lot more damage than she used to. And that corpse puppet of hers.... Why did it leave me feeling so jumpy? And it was actually working with Yue Dong to unleash Six Thieves Deceive Life.... Dammit!!

Sir Blood Dust felt full of defiance and fury. However, he didn’t suspect that Yue Dong was anyone other than herself. After all, Six Thieves Deceive Life was the signature ability of the eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall, and it was also Yue Dong’s signature move.

That whore was one of the scouts that got sent to Revered Ancient. After she arrived there, she must have come across some amazing destined opportunity! Killing her is going to require some clever planning.

Right now, Sir Blood Dust could do nothing but focus on healing. As he did, he took out a jade slip. It was a mission jade slip that the Devilbird holy land had given out. It listed all sorts of available missions, as well as the battle credit that would come upon completing them.

I need to keep racking up battle credit to get access to other pocket realms. Thankfully, there are a lot of humans out there, and there are plenty of weak ones that I can kill. The more I kill, the more battle credit I’ll earn.

Sir Blood Dust had no choice but to suppress the killing intent toward Yue Dong. He was fundamentally a patient person, otherwise he wouldn’t have waited so long before suddenly making a lightning-like attack out of nowhere. Unfortunately, he knew that he wasn’t strong enough right now. He needed to stockpile resources and get stronger before he sought revenge.

As he scanned the jade slip with divine will looking for an appropriate mission, he suddenly sensed fluctuations from outside the mansion grotto. They started very faint, but quickly grew so strong that the entire mountain was shaking violently. The spell formations were being attacked.

An instant later, the mansion grotto’s main door cracked open.

The sudden development caused Sir Blood Dust’s face to fall, and he extended his right hand, and a teleportation symbol appeared under it on the ground. All he had to do was touch that symbol, and he would be teleported away.

Unfortunately, Sir Blood Dust’s hand was about three inches away from the ground when he suddenly stopped moving. There, in his shadow, was an eye.

It was Little Shadow. Although it didn’t have complete control over Sir Blood Dust, it had enough control to stop his hand from moving.

Sir Blood Dust’s heart lurched in his chest, and he instinctively roared in rage, all while trying to send his left hand out to touch the teleportation symbol on the ground.

That was when a cold voice echoed out from within his roar of rage.

“Found you.”

To Sir Blood Dust’s astonishment, Xu Qing had used some incomparably gruish method to appear right out from within the sound of the roar. In the blink of an eye, Xu Qing materialized, reached out, and grabbed Sir Blood Dust by the throat. He slammed him into the wall.

RUMBLE!

The mansion grotto shook. The mountain trembled. Sir Blood Dust’s eyes went wide with astonishment. He wanted to fight back. But the hand latched onto his throat was causing a wild influx of mutagen to invade him. Scared witless, he instinctively tried to unleash some hidden trump cards. But then, to his terror, he realized... he couldn’t even move. Now, countless eyes were visible within his shadow.

When Xu Qing attacked, Little Shadow had taken advantage of Sir Blood Dust’s unstable mental state to possess him.

The terror in Sir Blood Dust’s eyes grew more intense. This person in front of him was both familiar and unfamiliar at the same time. Those two sensations mixed together, until something occurred to him. In his effort to earn a lot of battle credit, he had killed a lot of humans. And of course, he had scanned through all of the missions, including those that listed bounties for famous humans. The person in front of him... was a person whose image he had seen before in that list! He was a human who ruled over two regions! He was Imperial Tutor Xu Qing! Xu Qing was not only in the holy land in person, he was right inside of Sir Blood Dust’s mansion grotto, attacking him....

This revelation struck Sir Blood Dust like a bolt of lightning. And as it did, he realized that this whole thing must be related to Yue Dong. There was no doubt about it: Sir Blood Dust was quick on his feet. Sadly for him, he still reacted too slowly.

Xu Qing’s face was completely expressionless as he turned and left the mansion grotto with Sir Blood Dust in tow. He stayed invisible as he traveled for several hours. Eventually, he found a vast wilderness, where he was able to dig a cave under the ground. Once inside, he released his grip on Sir Blood Dust and sat down cross-legged. He said nothing.

Sir Blood Dust’s eyes filled with despair and madness. Unfortunately, he couldn’t even move. He could only watch as he dropped to his knees in front of Xu Qing.

The cave was completely silent.

Shortly after, Xu Qing imprinted a blank shadeheaven demonmoon pill with Sir Blood Dust’s appearance. Then he used the authority of erasure to inspect Sir Blood Dust’s fate threads. As Sir Blood Dust trembled, Xu Qing reached out, grabbed one thread in particular, and studied it closely. Just as before, Xu Qing could see some white dust on the thread. The bits of dust were illusory, and were apparently an integral part of the threads.

When Xu Qing tried to extract the dust from the thread, it quickly disappeared. He frowned.

This white dust was very important to him. He needed to identify the origin so that he could collect that dust. With enough, he could tap into its karmaless qualities, and thus make it possible to go forward with his idea of using a clone to further his cultivation.

Sometime later, the dao lineament in his left eye flared. It was the authority of the Six Thieves Deceive Life immortal skill.

Sir Blood Dust trembled inwardly. One reason was that he was now convinced that Xu Qing and Yue Dong were working together. The other reason was that he was shaken to the core by Xu Qing’s authority. For someone to have two types of authority before even being an Imperial Sovereign was something that Sir Blood Dust couldn’t even remember having happened before. It was unprecedented! Before he could reel in astonishment for long, the dao lineament in Xu Qing’s eyes caused Sir Blood Dust to lose consciousness.

Of course, Xu Qing’s research was only just beginning. He wanted to know exactly what that dust was.

The dao lineaments in his eyes ensured that Sir Blood Dust’s fate threads weren’t just fully visible. They were covered with color. That color included karma, and it included the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures. Xu Qing reached out to grab the threads and study them one by one.

In that manner, five days passed.

Xu Qing didn’t rest that entire time. He was fully immersed in his study. Unfortunately, no matter what he tried, the white dust would always disappear after he extracted it. Nothing he did could prevent that.

Xu Qing’s frown grew deeper and deeper.

Don’t tell me I’m pursuing the wrong idea...?

As the dawn of the sixth day broke outside, Xu Qing suddenly reached out and snapped one of Sir Blood Dust’s fingers off to study his flesh and blood. Not wasting even a drop of blood, he started studying every aspect of Sir Blood Dust’s fleshly body. He started with a finger, then moved onto a hand. Then an arm. Ultimately, he even studied his five yin organs and six yang organs. He even looked into his major worlds.

Eventually, he found the white dust inside of Sir Blood Dust’s flesh, which caused his eyes to light up. And yet, even the white dust in Sir Blood Dust’s flesh and blood did the same thing. As soon as it was extracted, it vanished. It was as if Sir Blood Dust’s body itself was the origin. freewebnovel.com

A few more days went by. Once the work on the fleshly body was done, Xu Qing force-fed Sir Blood Dust some medicinal pills to keep him alive.

His fate threads have it. His flesh and blood has it. But his major worlds don’t have it. What about his soul...?

After that, he started studying his soul. One had to be very meticulous when studying the soul, as using slightly too much force could result in irreversible damage. As a result, Xu Qing had to slow down a bit.

About ten days later, he retracted his divine will. His frown was even deeper this time. He had thoroughly studied Sir Blood Dust’s soul and found no trace of white dust.

Very strange. In some ways, Sir Blood Dust seems like the origin. But in other ways, he doesn’t.

After some thought, Xu Qing waved his hand to release the godly authority of misfortune. As it covered Sir Blood Dust’s fate threads, he also used Six Thieves Deceive Life. He paid very close attention to what happened next. A few days later, he ended the session of research and closed his eyes to think.

After days of observation, he had come to understand why the white dust seemed karmaless. It was actually the white dust devouring karma. The invasions of the misfortune and the Six Thieves Deceive Life were both devoured.

I can’t extract it.... In that case, I guess I only have two options. If either works, I can accept it.

Xu Qing looked at Sir Blood Dust.

Sir Blood Dust was a mangled mess. He had flesh growing chaotically all over him, making him look horrifying. There were also chunks of gore scattered around. His expression was blank, and he was struggling to breathe!

However, Xu Qing was making sure that the flame of his life force kept burning.

When Xu Qing looked at him, Sir Blood Dust responded with numbness. After what he had gone through over the last month, he now just wanted to die.

Xu Qing reached out, grabbed Sir Blood Dust’s soul, pulled it out, and sealed it off to the side. He was going with the first option. He would assimilate Sir Blood Dust’s fleshly body, and use a secret magic from the Xeno-Immortal School to turn it into a clone for himself.

The difficulty lay in the fact that he and the clone would still be very similar. Dealing with the special qualities of the white dust was also going to be challenging. But if he succeeded, he would have a karmaless clone. And if that clone practiced cultivation, it could bypass the limitations that constrained his true form. With such thoughts in mind, Xu Qing performed a double-handed incantation gesture, causing soul threads to fly out, pierce into the fleshly body, and start refining it.

Three days later, the humanoid form in front of Xu Qing collapsed into a pile of blood. The refining had failed.

So it can’t have the same origin as me.... Not even sending soul threads into the flesh can result in forming my soul. And that white dust is just too unusual. That’s another reason for the failure.

Xu Qing took a deep breath and massaged the bridge of his nose. Then he looked over at Sir Blood Dust’s soul.

I guess I only have one option left.

Eyes flashing with determination, he started a soulsearch, despite knowing it could end up completely wiping Sir Blood Dust out of existence. He was hoping that would reveal the true origin of the white dust on the fate threads.

With Sir Blood Dust’s soul in hand, he sent his god perception out. Sir Blood Dust’s soul wailed as it was invaded. Bit by bit, memory fragments came and went as Xu Qing dug destructively through Sir Blood Dust’s past. He saw Sir Blood Dust as a child. He watched him grow up. He saw the grudge form between him and Yue Dong. He also saw how he had earned battle credit by slaughtering numerous humans. Countless memory fragments rippled like water in front of Xu Qing.

In the end, Xu Qing found what he was looking for in a memory from three months ago. At that time, Sir Blood Dust used battle credit to gain entrance into the World Origin Pocket Realm, which was a very special location among the eastern Devilbirds. The place had strong world auras, as well as large amounts of natural and magical laws. As a result, it was a very useful place for Smoldering Gods trying to form their worlds.

It used to belong to the Lan Clan. But when the Lan Clan fell from power, it became the property of Lu Lingzi.

In the past, the pocket realm wasn’t made available to the public. But after the war started, entrance could be purchased with battle credit. As a result, many Devilbird cultivators gained access.

In fact, that was how Sir Blood Dust managed to create his seventh major world. It was after emerging from the pocket realm that the white dust appeared in Sir Blood Dust’s fate!

After close inspection to confirm that, Xu Qing destroyed Sir Blood Dust’s soul. Then he opened his eyes.

Something happened to Sir Blood Dust in a valley in that pocket realm. Unfortunately, he has no memories of what happened inside. But that’s definitely where the white dust came from. The World Origin Pocket Realm.... It seems I need to take a trip there. If I can find that valley, then I can figure out exactly what happened to Sir Blood Dust....

After thinking the matter over, he took out Sir Blood Dust’s mission jade slip, which was how he was able to confirm that getting into the World Origin Pocket Realm required a large amount of battle credit.

The top mission on the list was the bounty on Feng Lintao. Xu Qing scanned the entire list with divine will. Eyes narrowing, he made a decision. With a blur, he vanished and reappeared outside the cave. Flying up into the sky, he transformed into Sir Blood Dust.

The Garmentfolks’ special medicinal pill ensured that he looked exactly like Sir Blood Dust down to his aura. Thanks to what happened over the past month, Xu Qing knew everything there was to know about Sir Blood Dust. By adding in the effects of the Grand Emperor’s needle, he was able to impersonate him with complete accuracy.

It was dawn, and the radiance of the morning light spread out as Xu Qing flicked his sleeve. Blood clouds formed around him as he shot over the horizon.

The eastern Devilbirds originally had nine Imperial Sovereign mountains.

After Grand Emperor Netherflame’s tenth apprentice Lu Lingzi returned, the Lan Clan fell into decline. As a result, many of the resources previously controlled by the Lan Clan came to belong to Lu Lingzi.

In fact, the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain wasn’t very far away from Lan Clan territory. The mountain towered high into the clouds, making its majesty visible from a great distance away. The pressure of an Imperial Sovereign pulsed out of it, weighing down on everything in its vicinity. It suppressed heaven and earth in all directions.

As a result of its presence, there was a massive vortex in the sky, which had been spinning endlessly for a couple of months now. It emanated loud rumbling sounds, and was filled with endless bolts of lightning.

Fifteen hundred kilometers away from the base of the mountain was a perimeter that stretched around the entire mountain, creating something like a forbidden region. On the other side of the perimeter, there were already large numbers of Devilbird cultivators gathered. There were well over ten thousand of them, and they seemed to be engaged in various types of meditation, all focused on the mountain itself.

From a high vantage point, the crowds were numerous as they covered the lands. Some of them were rogue cultivators who had previously been affiliated with Lan Clan organizations. Right now, they were hoping to become subordinates of this tenth Imperial Sovereign.

In the Devilbird holy land, whenever a new Imperial Sovereign showed up and created a mountain, things like this would happen. New Imperial Sovereigns didn’t just get personally stronger. They would also expand their influence, and use their newfound power to recruit large numbers of followers.

As a result, streams of cultivators were arriving at the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain on a daily basis. Given the couple of months that had passed, the crowd was sizable. After all, being the subordinate of an Imperial Sovereign would make a cultivator completely different. And given that there was a war going on, who wouldn’t want the added level of safety of being protected by an Imperial Sovereign?

However... up to this point, the new Imperial Sovereign Lu Lingzi hadn’t actually recruited anyone. In fact, he hadn’t even called his previous subordinates to any sort of meeting.

As of now, there was only one person who had entered the enormous mountain, and that was Lu Lingzi himself. There were so many cultivators at the foot of the mountain that they had created a small city where people would trade goods and information while they waited to become disciples of the Imperial Sovereign.

As time passed, the city became an increasingly bustling place. However, none of the cultivators present dared to cross the perimeter into the forbidden region that surrounded the mountain.

When Xu Qing arrived looking like Sir Blood Dust, he looked at the bustling scene fifteen hundred kilometers away from the mountain. After taking in the city and all the local cultivators, he didn’t hesitate for a moment. Flying at top speed, he headed toward the forbidden region. At first, few people noticed his presence. But when he zipped through the city and crossed the perimeter, many gazes shifted in his direction. Nothing happened beyond that.

In the two months that had passed, there had been other cultivators besides Xu Qing who approached the mountain in the hopes of getting an audience with the Imperial Sovereign. However, every single one had been ignored, and had eventually crossed back over the perimeter to wait. Therefore, nothing happened other than some people looking over at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing ignored the gazes. Face completely expressionless, he approached the mountain, then stopped and hovered in midair. His eyes glittered profoundly for a long moment before he took a deep breath. Looking very determined, he bowed formally, then spoke in a voice that boomed like thunder and attracted a lot of attention.

“Sir Blood Dust here, seeking an audience with the Imperial Sovereign!”

This was a bit of a test. If it worked, then maybe he could achieve his goal with words. If it didn’t work, then he would have to try another angle. Enough time passed for an incense stick to burn. Even then, there was no response from the Imperial Sovereign mountain.

Many of the people who had turned to look at Xu Qing shifted their gazes away. There was a bit of discussion.

“Some people just don’t get it.”

“That’s Sir Blood Dust, right? Does he really think his cultivation base and battle credit are enough to attract the attention of the Imperial Sovereign?”

“We’re obviously all sitting around waiting. But he just has to go and offer greetings. And why is he talking so loud...? If I were the Imperial Sovereign, I definitely wouldn’t want to be disturbed like that.”

“If you want to become the subordinate of an Imperial Sovereign, you need to prove your sincerity! That’s why the best tactic is to just wait patiently. Eventually, that will prove to the Imperial Sovereign that you really are sincere.”

In the end, most people just shook their heads and turned their attention elsewhere. As far as they were concerned, it would only be a matter of time before Sir Blood Dust retreated in dejection.

Xu Qing turned a deaf ear to all the chatter. Looking just as calm as before, he stayed in place and maintained a deep bow. There, he waited.

This time, another incense stick’s worth of time passed. At this point, hardly anyone was paying attention at all, and the city had gone back to its previous bustle.

But then... Xu Qing spoke again.

“Sir Blood Dust here, seeking an audience with the Imperial Sovereign!”

As the words echoed out, people once again looked over, and this time there were quite a few irritated expressions.

A buzz of discussion rose up again.

However, only an instant later, the cultivators present stopped talking, as something dramatic suddenly happened. The Imperial Sovereign mountain rumbled loudly! The entire thing started shaking back and forth! At the same time, the lightning in the vortex above began to increase in intensity, to the point where it was spilling out of the vortex. The sound of it was absolutely deafening.

Then, an enormous pair of eyes appeared in the vortex. The eyes were silver, and were incredibly cold as they looked down on the lands below.

Every single person looking on was shocked to the core, and, acting on pure instinct, ducked their heads and bowed.

A majestic will filled the area, its terrifying pressure causing the ground to quake. Countless cultivators struggled to breathe, all while reeling in shock. Then, Lu Lingzi’s voice spoke coldly from within the Imperial Sovereign mountain.

“Enter.”

The word boomed louder than heavenly thunder, becoming an infinitude of sounds that slammed into the ears of those present and shaking them down to the soul.

As everyone trembled in astonishment, Xu Qing took a deep breath and strode forth. As everyone looked on, he flew to the Imperial Sovereign mountain. Shortly after, he disappeared into the mountain.

The cultivators in the area watched it play out, astonished, various emotions playing out on their faces, and their eyes burning with passion. It was a complete surprise to all of them that Sir Blood Dust had been summoned. And yet, the end result was that people started to get excited. After all, once a first person had been summoned, it meant that there would likely be a second person summoned after that. And that meant that the long wait would soon be paying off.

Meanwhile, the developments were very thought-provoking to Xu Qing, as his first test had provided a preliminary explanation to some of his questions. After reaching the mountain, he sped right toward the summit.

Before long, he caught sight of a hall. It wasn’t fancy and extravagant. Instead, it seemed utilitarian. It rested at the very summit of the mountain, and its entrance was open. Upon getting close, he saw that there was a person inside, located at the position of honor, resting cross-legged in meditation. freewebnovel.com

It was none other than Lu Lingzi.

Xu Qing ducked his head, stepped forward, and stopped just outside the entrance. There, he bowed at the waist. He didn’t say a word.

A moment passed, whereupon Lu Lingzi opened his eyes. They didn’t contain even the slightest hint of emotion.

“What do you want?” The voice seemed to thrum with natural laws, as if when this person spoke, their words would be enforced to the letter.

Reacting instantly, Xu Qing said, “Imperial Sovereign, I would like to request that you grant me entrance into the World Origin Pocket Realm.”

Lu Lingzi’s facial expression didn’t change at all. Looking at Xu Qing, he said, “Present your battle credit.”

Shaking his head, Xu Qing calmly said, “I have no battle credit.”

He really didn’t have any. After checking the mission jade slip, Xu Qing had identified all sorts of missions that were there for the taking. Unfortunately, the vast majority were related to the war. And most involved fighting and killing top experts among humankind. As for those missions that weren’t related to the war, they all required significant investment, would take a lot of time, and didn’t provide much battle credit as a reward.

Meanwhile, getting into the World Origin Pocket Realm required a vast amount of battle credit. In fact, it required so much battle credit that collecting it via missions would take months at the very least. Given all that, Xu Qing felt that, rather than go do missions, it made more sense to just go directly to Lu Lingzi and ask permission. That seemed a lot simpler.

After all, he and Erniu had analyzed the situation well enough to have some suspicions about Lu Lingzi’s identity. If he really was Lu Lingzi, then the fact that he had become an Imperial Sovereign based on his own personhood indicated he wouldn’t reveal his true karmic connections. In that case, it would have been very unlikely that he would summon Xu Qing into his presence just based on a simple request for an audience.

But if this person wasn’t actually Lu Lingzi, then that meant... he was either the empress or someone very close to her.

And that gave Xu Qing the impression that he probably could gain entry to the pocket realm. That was what led to the current situation. As of right now, he still wasn’t really sure if the Lu Lingzi in front of him was the same Lu Lingzi he had encountered before.

Could he actually be the empress...?

Because of that lack of clarity, he was taking things slowly.

A powerful will spread out, enveloping the entire Imperial Sovereign mountain. The vortex in the sky spun, shaking the mountain as a sealing barrier was created.

Upon hearing Xu Qing’s response, Lu Lingzi thought for a moment, then said, “You have no battle credit to get into the pocket realm, yet you boldly demand entrance. You’ve got guts, Xu Qing. In fact, you’ve got more guts than your Elder Brother!”

Hearing his secret identity spoken out loud caused Xu Qing to blink a few times. And for him to be described as ‘having guts’ was very meaningful. He looked up at Lu Lingzi.

“Your Majesty....” After saying those two words, Xu Qing said nothing further.

A moment later, as the immense pressure continued to weigh down, Lu Lingzi spoke again.

“Where’s your Elder Brother?”

Xu Qing blinked and then answered truthfully. “He went to the Immortal Skills Hall.”

Lu Lingzi thought for a moment, then snorted coldly and waved a hand. A command medallion flew out to Xu Qing.

Xu Qing grabbed it. It was an entrance medallion to the World Origin Pocket Realm.

“Many thanks, Imperial Sovereign!” Xu Qing bowed, then turned to leave.

“Don’t stir up too much trouble!” said Lu Lingzi.

Xu Qing stopped in place, nodded, then continued on his way. After he was gone, Lu Lingzi kneaded the bridge of his nose.

At least Xu Qing knows how to mind his p’s and q’s. But that Elder Brother of his... is always getting up to mischief.

Among the eastern Devilbirds, the World Origin Pocket Realm was immensely beneficial to Smoldering Gods in the making of new worlds. As a result, it was very famous. It was located in the north of the Lan Clan’s ancestral lands, about 3,500 kilometers away in the World Origin Wilds.

From the outside, the wilds was a place of barren hills and wild rivers. It contained dangerous animals and toxic miasmas, and was surrounded by a powerful sealing magic that prevented cultivators from entering it casually.

Even an extremely powerful expert who tried to enter by force would find such efforts useless. Without an entry medallion created by Grand Emperor Netherflame of the Lan Clan, any cultivator who wasn’t at the Grand Emperor level wouldn’t be able to see through to the true nature of the place. They would only see the barren hills and wild rivers.

However, with one of those special entry medallions, someone who entered the wilds would suddenly see something very different. Instead of the rugged terrain, dangerous animals, and toxic miasmas, they would see an enormous geographical basin. In the middle of that basin was a shockingly enormous object. It was some 30,000 meters tall, long and thin, and covered with massive amounts of magical symbols. Upon first glancing at this object, anyone who saw it would be shaken to the core. The reason was that it was a jade slip! Put most precisely, it was an ancient jade slip with a snapshot in it.[1][2]

No one knew who originally created it, but given how big it was, it was obviously someone terrifyingly powerful. Based on the records kept by the Devilbird holy land, the jade slip came from beyond the heavens during the time of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity. It originally came to Devilbird lands, but was later borrowed by Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity.

Some years after that, the Grand Emperors of the Devilbirds earned enough battle credit to get the jade slip back from Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity. From that point on, it became a holy relic of the Devilbirds.

When the broken face came and the Devilbirds left with Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity, they built their holy land beyond the heavens. After various twists and turns, the jade slip became the sole property of Grand Emperor Netherflame. That was how it eventually came to belong to the Lan Clan.

The unique and unusual thing about it was the snapshot stored inside. With an entry medallion from the Lan Clan, one could enter the jade slip, passing from reality into illusory as they stepped into the world of the snapshot.

As for the details of the snapshot.... Some people said it depicted the creation of worlds.

For years, the Lan Clan controlled the pocket realm, and thus, any outsider who wanted to gain entrance would have to pay a considerable price. And ultimately, it came down to whether the Lan Clan felt like letting them in. If the Lan Clan wasn’t willing, then you couldn’t get inside no matter how much you offered to pay.

At the moment, Xu Qing was flying through the air to the border of the barren hills and wild rivers. As he neared, he slowed to a stop and hovered in midair. There were virtually no signs of life; there definitely wasn’t anyone guarding the border. After all, few people could gain entrance, and given the odd nature of the area, there wasn’t really a need for anyone to stand guard.

A few breaths of time passed, whereupon Xu Qing’s eyes gleamed. Taking out the entrance medallion the empress had given him, he unhesitatingly walked into the wilds. It was like walking through a sheet of water. The hills, rivers, animals, and miasmas all vanished. Then Xu Qing saw the enormous basin and the shocking jade slip.

So, I need to enter the snapshot....

Even just looking at the jade slip, Xu Qing could sense an ancient aura coming off it. His gaze drifted to the base of the jade slip.

About thirty percent of it is under the ground... the portion visible above accounts for seventy percent. Just what kind of entity could create a jade slip this big? And what sort of being would be able to leave a snapshot of the creation of worlds?

Xu Qing knew some of the details of the pocket realm from Sir Blood Dust’s memories. Although he had a bit of experience going into places like this, it was obviously his first time coming to this specific location.

After confirming that the area was generally safe, including everything around the jade slip, he hefted the entry medallion and proceeded inside. He didn’t slow down at all, and the moment he made contact with the huge thing, he vanished. It wasn’t that he entered the jade slip. Rather, it was more like he had simply been erased. By some gruish means, he had disappeared from the world!

And when he reappeared... he was inside the snapshot. What he saw in front of him caused waves of shock that shattered any sense of calm within him.

“Is that...?” he murmured in a choked voice.

Xu Qing was a person who had experienced many things in life, and seen quite a bit, so normally he wouldn’t react like this. But the scene in front of him was just stupefying.

It was a massive void! And in the depths of that void was a gargantuan candle. It was bright red, and it was currently burning. As it burned, the candle’s flame illuminated the surroundings, creating something like a glowing halo that filled the void and flickered with unstable, glimmering light. Astonishingly, there were countless planets and innumerable worlds visible, forming out of the dust that surrounded them.[3]

It was literally impossible to count them. In the area toward the edge of the halo of light, the planets and worlds formed out of the dust, but then collapsed and turned back into dust. As the process went on, infinite natural and magical laws were born, only to be destroyed and sent back into the dust. The same thing happened over and over again.

Even just at first glance, Xu Qing saw what had to be hundreds of thousands of worlds to come to existence, and then be destroyed. But that was only what was happening at the periphery. Closer toward the red candle, the planets and worlds formed more slowly, and it also took longer for them to be destroyed.

In fact, Xu Qing was even able to see some planets and worlds that were very close to the candle and seemed almost totally complete.

What am I looking at...? Xu Qing wasn’t sure if he was actually looking at worlds being created. But he was certain that this snapshot contained a very strong world aura.

Natural laws. Magical laws. Essence. Such things were visible everywhere.

But it’s all illusory....

Though it was definitely an illusion, and though he was inside that illusion, he knew that this was clearly a place where Smoldering God cultivators could seek unprecedented levels of enlightenment.

This place must also house immense danger.

Xu Qing sent out his god perception before carefully proceeding. Based on Sir Blood Dust’s memories, the valley where he had experienced those transformations to his fate was located somewhere here, in one of the planets located in the halo cast by the candle.

For all Xu Qing knew, that specific planet might have already ended its life cycle in the months that had passed. It might have collapsed and turned back into dust.

Not wanting to waste any time, he shot forward. As he neared the halo, he sensed heat. It came from the burning red candle, and within it were the embryonic forms of innumerable natural and magical laws. As he moved forward, he carefully avoided the collapsing worlds and focused on his destination.

About an hour passed, at which point he caught sight of the same planet from Sir Blood Dust’s memories. It was in the process of collapsing. However, in that specific area, time moved slowly, and thus, it was only about half-collapsed. Although it was clearly a dangerous place, there was reason for hope.

Xu Qing breathed a sigh of relief and was just about to proceed when his expression turned grim. Then his right hand shot out to his side and clenched down. A cold sensation passed through his palm. His hand clamped down onto absolutely nothing.

The two dao lineaments in his eyes flickered as he looked around. Based on Sir Blood Dust’s memories, he knew that there was a dangerous type of entity that lurked in the World Origin Pocket Realm called a grieve.[4]

Unfortunately, Sir Blood Dust didn’t know what they looked like or how many there were. All he knew was that, though you couldn’t see them, if you got close to them, you would sense some coldness within the heat of this place. That was what Xu Qing had just sensed.

Though Sir Blood Dust didn’t know what they looked like, he did know where they came from. In short, grieves were the shades of cultivators of the past. They were a representation of another of the dangers of this pocket realm. You could easily get absorbed. If you stayed too long in the snapshot, or if you got too close to the red candle, there was a strong chance you would be absorbed.

After that happened to a cultivator, it was as if they were erased and turned into something else impossible to see, and would remain stuck in the snapshot, unable to escape. Though most cultivators knew about that risk before coming in, over time, there were people who, for various reasons, ended up being absorbed and stuck inside. After they were erased, a Grand Emperor would be able to tell if they had become a soul or something else. But Sir Blood Dust had no way of understanding.

Xu Qing looked around coldly. Then, rumbling sounds echoed out as a blood aura spread around him. Thanks to the unique nature of his body, he was confident that he wouldn’t be tainted by the grieves. With that, he continued on his way, getting closer and closer to the collapsing planet.

Soon, he stepped onto its surface. The moment he did, all sensations of heat disappeared. Instead, endless cold surrounded him. Although he didn’t see anything in the vicinity, he could sense that there were countless grieves surrounding him!

Astonishingly, this planet was chock full of grieves!

***

Outside of the World Origin Pocket Realm, beyond the area controlled by the eastern Devilbirds, were the lands of the western Devilbirds. There, the enormous dao altar shaped like a wing was glowing with dazzling light.

High atop the dao altar was an octagonal platform where a figure was seated cross-legged. This person was mostly a blur, like an outline, with no facial features visible. However, despite just being an outline, they pulsed with fluctuations that contained something indescribably terrible. Anyone who came into the presence of this person would tremble and not dare to look at them.

At the moment, one of the western Devilbird’s Imperial Sovereigns was kneeling in front of the platform in just that manner.

Unable to stop his heart from pounding, he quietly said, “Grand Emperor, we’ve searched the holy land from east to west. We’ve looked just about everywhere, with the only exception being the secluded meditation facilities of Grand Emperor Netherflame. Unfortunately, we were not able to find that which you seek.”

Grand Emperor Devilbird said nothing in response.

The kneeling Imperial Sovereign waited for a moment, then slowly got to his feet and respectfully withdrew.

Sometime later the silence of the platform was broken as Grand Emperor Devilbird murmured, “Does it actually exist?” freewebnovel.com

As his words echoed out, the sound of clinking chains could be heard on the platform. Then, a black-cloaked figure appeared out of nowhere. He was bound with chains, and his fleshly body was in a state of decay. And yet the figure didn’t seem to be in any discomfort at all.

“As I previously said, the Mask of Wishes is intelligent. And it’s never been found when looked for. It can only be encountered randomly. If it doesn’t want to be found by you, then given the level of your cultivation base, you wouldn’t be able to see it even if it was right in front of you. Considering how long you’ve looked for it unsuccessfully, Grand Emperor Devilbird, I think that indicates... you are not meant to find it.” [5]

1. Jade slips are so ubiquitous in xianxia that I’m sure most of you know what they look like. That said, who doesn’t love some cool pictures? And I don’t think I’ve shared any pictures of jade slips so far in this translation. Jade slips are fancier versions of the more common bamboo slips. Whether jade or bamboo, they are long, thin slips that would be bound together to form a scroll. Here is an image collection of actual jade slips and jade scrolls. As you can see, there is actually quite a variety in the possible sizes and shapes. ☜

2. The reason I’m using the seemingly anachronistic term ‘snapshot’ is because the author used a seemingly anachronistic word in Chinese that means... snapshot. If the author does anachronistic things in Chinese, I will do the same in the translation. ☜

3. In reality, instead of the more common word for planet, the author uses the very nebulous term that I usually translate as ‘heavenly body.’ This term can cover everything from stars and moons to planets and asteroids. Given how this scene plays out, I’m going with the ‘planet’ interpretation for ease of translation and reading. What’s more, generally speaking, the term I’m rendering as ‘planet’ tends to be applied (at least by Er Gen) to huge spherical objects, whereas ‘world’ could refer to things like land masses (i.e. Flat Earth type worlds). ☜

4. There is more to come about what exactly the “grieves” are. The Chinese is a word that basically just means “fantastic/bizarre.” However, similar to both the grues and ghasts, the author has turned this word into the name of a specific entity. What’s more, it contains a character that is shared with grues and ghasts. Because of that, I wanted to have a word that starts with G and has a similar feel to the grues and ghasts. ☜

5. There are different words/characters in Chinese that can mean mask or face depending on the context. In this paragraph, it uses the same character that I render as ‘face’ when translating ‘broken face.’ In other words, without context, you could also render this Face of Wishes. However, context makes it clear that the object referred to in this paragraph is a mask. There is a bit more to this situation linguistically that I will explain in a footnote in chapter 1038. ☜

In the World Origin Pocket Realm, Xu Qing felt immense coldness building on the collapsing planet that was located roughly in the midpoint of the halo cast by the red candle.

Only moments ago, there had been immense heat surrounding him. But now, there was frost on the ground, and the cold was getting more intense. Within that coldness was a boundless killing intent, rushing toward Xu Qing from all directions.

Eyes glinting, he lifted his foot and then stomped it onto the ground. The frosty ground trembled, and cracks spread out from where Xu Qing had stomped down. They spread quickly, making the ground look like a spiderweb or a shattered mirror. The air flowed chaotically around him, forming into a tempest. Mud splattered everywhere as the tempest grew in size, picking up countless bits of frost as well.

Xu Qing tapped into the power of the tempest to leap up into the air to start moving.

However, the killing intent of the invisible grieves had been stoked by what just happened, and they were converging within the tempest. Cracking sounds echoed out from the wind, which froze, turning into a huge ice column that connected to the ground. The freezing extended rapidly toward Xu Qing, as if he were being chased.

Xu Qing frowned. According to Sir Blood Dust’s memories, he had originally come to this place to avoid other dangers. It had mostly been an accident, and there hadn’t been anything particularly dangerous on the surface of the planet.

Things had gone very smoothly when he just entered that one large valley. But now things were different.

Is it that something around here changed recently? Or is it... my presence that’s causing things to happen?

As Xu Qing accelerated, the frigid coldness behind him grew more intense. The lands behind him were being frozen, and even the wind was becoming solid. Some of the frozen gusts of wind fell to the ground. Some converged into curved shapes like claws that connected to the sky. In fact, even the dome of heaven seemed like it was on the verge of being frozen.

Apparently, it was killing intent from the grieves, and it came from the sky, the land, the wind, the void. In fact, it came from everywhere as it closed in on Xu Qing.

I’m really in a passive position at the moment.

He passed a lake, and as it froze solid, he stopped midair to survey his surroundings. After confirming there were no cultivators present, he unleashed his godsource, causing boundless golden light to spread out from him. The godly authorities of sound and the violet moon became a deadly force that swept in all directions. Wherever it passed, the areas that had been frozen solid exploded. The ice in the sky became violet as a violet moon rose within the snapshot, and the color violet filled the collapsing planet. Massive amounts of xeno-immortal soul threads shot out from Xu Qing, like a flooding river that replaced the tempest, becoming a vortex that shredded everything in its path.

Even a five- or six-world Smoldering God who encountered force like this would be shocked. But here... even though the power of Xu Qing’s godly authority was destroying the heavens and crushing the earth...

The frigid and freezing aura didn’t go away. Though it was temporarily rebuffed, it swept around and then converged on Xu Qing yet again.

In fact, the fluctuations rolling out seemed to be attracting more grieves, who raced from all directions toward the planet. Though the grieves weren’t visible, the frigid cold coming from the starry sky made Xu Qing realize something.

They can’t be destroyed?

Xu Qing’s eyes gleamed. Instead of using godly authority, he took a deep breath. Then, within his sea of consciousness, a sun rose, casting out profound sun immortal light. As it swept forth from Xu Qing, it created boundless light and heat in the surroundings.

The result... was middling at best. Although it kept Xu Qing safe temporarily, it was clear that the invisible grieves were still coming for him.

If things keep going like this, then even if I find that valley, I won’t be able to focus on finding the source of that white dust I found on Sir Blood Dust.

After the successive clashes with the grieves, Xu Qing had come to some realizations. Being absorbed by this place involved losing one’s fleshly body and being turned into a grieve by the red candle. When that happened, one gained the attribute of indestructibility.

However, that attribute was relative. After all, Xu Qing had encountered a lot of beings in his life and none of them, not even gods, could be considered eternally indestructible. Not even True Gods. Otherwise, why else would Yu Liuchen have targeted a True God?

In other words, it doesn’t matter if you’re talking about being undying or indestructible, both can only happen under certain circumstances. In that case, what are the circumstances that allow these grieves to be undying and indestructible?

A few breaths of time passed as Xu Qing kept moving. Then he suddenly looked over his shoulder, and his eyes shone with an aggressive light.

Now I see it! The grieves are undying and indestructible when they’re invisible! You can’t see them, therefore you can’t kill them! In other words, if you want to kill them, you need to be able to see them first!

Almost at the same moment that Xu Qing realized that, he felt some emotional fluctuations from Little Shadow.

“Milord... is correct... I can fuse... and thus see....”

Xu Qing frowned. Little Shadow’s fluctuations had come at a very opportune moment. It was almost as if the shadow had been waiting on purpose.

“Why didn’t you say something earlier?” Xu Qing said in a cold voice.

The shadow nervously stammered, “M-milord... I... couldn’t... this place... image candle... limitations... unable say....”

Xu Qing knew what it was trying to convey. The so-called ‘image candle’ in this place imposed limitations that the shadow wasn’t able to explain. Because of that, Xu Qing needed to react before it could say anything. At some other time, Xu Qing would want to look further into the situation with the shadow. But right now there wasn’t time. Suppressing his curiosity, he quickly gave some orders to Little Shadow. Little Shadow’s aura surged as it spread out over Xu Qing.

Many years ago, Xu Qing and the shadow had created the Shadow Fusion Secret Magic, which allowed him to fuse with the shadow in moments of crisis. The downside was that most divine abilities didn’t work in that state. However, it provided a massive boost to fleshly body power. As Xu Qing’s cultivation base grew, he found fewer reasons to fuse with Little Shadow. In fact, this was the first time in a very long time that he used the Shadow Fusion Secret Magic.[1]

In the blink of an eye, the shadow became like a black cloak that covered Xu Qing. Something like a black cape flapped behind him, and as his violet hair rippled, terrifying fleshly body power pulsed off of him. Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Winds screamed.

Even more terrifying were his eyes, which were pitch black. Now he could look out at the world using shadow eyes. It was as if a veil had been removed from the world around him, allowing him to see what was really there!

The dome of heaven was empty. The starry sky was a void. Everything was jade.

The dust, the planets, and everything else formed a painting. Even the terrain features and lands were part of it. The only thing that looked the same as before was the red candle, which burned its gruish flame as normal.

What was more... the previously invisible grieves... were now completely visible! What was even more astonishing was that they were black shadows being cast by the candle flame! They came in a variety of shapes and sizes. Some looked humanoid. Others looked like animals. Sometimes they were made of strange shapes, or even just threads. Fantastic oddities were visible everywhere. And all of them were pitch black, as if they were substructurally nothing more than shadows!

Over the countless years that had passed, the cultivators who had been absorbed by this pocket realm ended up losing their fleshly bodies and leaving behind only... their shadows. In reality, this pocket realm was really just a painting made of shadows!

That discovery caused his heart to leap in his chest. He had long wondered about the true origin of Little Shadow. And today... he had found a clue.

He turned to look at the distant red candle. He looked at the countless shadows in the area, looming over him.

Then Xu Qing’s profound sun immortal light erupted, causing light and heat to spread out. Screams rang out everywhere. It was almost like a special divine ability. Even being fused with Little Shadow, he was able to send out the immortal light.

Before, he couldn’t kill these shadows. But as the immortal light shone, they screamed and vanished like smoke in the wind.

The heat levels started rising.

Xu Qing flew into motion, sending immortal light out around him. He passed the painting of the lake and flew into the painting of a mountain. He destroyed the shadows he passed. Then, after enough time passed for an incense stick to burn, he spotted a huge valley.

Just like the lake and the mountain... the valley was a painting.

Although it looked very real, it wasn’t possible to enter it. He stood at the edge of the painting and mulled over the situation. Immortal light once again flared, and he sent it into the valley, where it swept back and forth. After doing that a few times in a row, the blackness retreated from his eyes as he unfused with Little Shadow.

His view of the world returned to normal. The valley was no longer a painting. Instead, it looked like an ordinary valley. With the blackness in his eyes, he couldn’t see the tangible.

After studying the valley for a long moment, he walked inside. Keeping his god perception out, he began searching. He wanted to find the place where that white dust originated.

Unfortunately... after about two hours passed, he flew out of the valley. Hovering above in midair, he frowned. The valley was deep, but not very big. In the two hours that had passed, he had thoroughly searched the place with god perception and hadn’t found a single thing.

There was no indication of any sort of white dust there, nor any evidence that there had been in the past. He even wondered if he had come to the wrong place.

Is this not the place? But Sir Blood Dust’s memories indicate that this very valley is where that dust became attached to his fate.

After a moment, he flew high up into the air and studied the area from above. Nothing seemed out of the ordinary.

He flew higher, until he left the planet. From that vantage point, he studied it, only to find nothing.

“In that case....”

He once again fused with Little Shadow. When his eyes became black he hovered high above the planet and looked down.

This time, his eyes went wide. Using shadow eyes, he now saw a painting of a planet... in which the valley was a big mouth. The mountain was a nose. The two lakes were eyes. The painting was not of a planet. It was of a face! [2]

2. As I mentioned in the footnote in the previous chapter, there are different words/characters for ‘face’ in Chinese. In the last chapter, the ‘Mask of Wishes’ has one of those characters that could be rendered as ‘face’ depending on the context. A different word is used in this paragraph. In other words, the planet/face here has a totally different set of characters from the broken face or from masks. I’m not saying this to spoil anything or give wink-wink-nudge-nudge clues. I’m just pointing out something that’s obvious in Chinese but not in English. If we later found out that the planet/face was actually a mask, it wouldn’t be a surprise. Or if we later found out it’s somehow connected to the broken face, it also wouldn’t be a surprise. But based on the characters alone, there is no reason to assume that there are any such connections. And incidentally (and completely not related to this chapter, but it just occurred to me), though context (and also official art) makes it clear that the broken face in the sky is indeed a face, if it later turned out to be a mask, that also wouldn’t be a surprise. Again, this is not a spoiler or a clue, just something linguistically that is obvious in Chinese but not necessarily English. ☜

Xu Qing’s heart was racing.

Naturally, the scene playing out in front of him was not something from Sir Blood Dust’s memories. His search had ultimately led him to find a face made of a planet, and that led him to realize something....

This definitely had to be the origin of the white dust he’d found in Sir Blood Dust’s soul!

Yet he wasn’t willing to just give up. That was especially true considering that the white dust had not fused with any fate threads, and thus existed in a different form. All of a sudden, he realized he knew exactly where that white dust in Sir Blood Dust had come from. Earlier, he had noticed other planets and worlds collapsing, but never had any white dust appeared. The white dust shows up with the destruction of a planet or world that resembles a face! Unfortunately, even though I went all out, I was only able to collect a small amount. It disappeared too quickly. I hardly have any....

Then Xu Qing checked the jade bottle and found that, despite the bottle being bolstered by godsource and authority, the white dust inside the bottle was still disappearing. The process was going slow. But at the very most, it would be completely gone in a day.

One day....

Xu Qing frowned. There wasn’t any time to lose. His cautious nature ensured that he wasn’t going to simply fuse the white dust with his own fate threads without doing some experimentation and research first.

When it comes down to it, what’s most important here isn’t the white dust. It’s the face....

He looked around.

Is there a second face around here?

Xu Qing thought for a moment, then sent some divine will out to Little Shadow. Instantly, Little Shadow fused with Xu Qing, causing Xu Qing’s eyes to turn pitch black. His plan was to use those shadow eyes to search through the pocket realm in the hopes of finding a second face.

Xu Qing didn’t waste any time. Now that the pocket realm looked like a painting again, he immediately started his search.

Time passed.

The World Origin Pocket Realm wasn’t a static painting. Instead, it was constantly moving. Most importantly, as Xu Qing searched, the heat, light, and danger of the red candle grew more intense.

Two days later, he had no choice but to leave the area of light and heat. Once outside, he looked back grimly.

Two days, and I only managed to search about a third of it. And most of those areas were close to the periphery. If I want to search more deeply, it would take more than ten days for sure. And the closer I get to the red candle, the more danger there is of being absorbed. This isn’t going to work.

The most ideal situation was to observe laws from the moment they appeared until the moment they vanished. Only by witnessing all of its transformations and variations could one gain enlightenment of that variety of natural law.

Xu Qing tried to suppress his astonishment at the results of the godly authority of good luck. Stopping in place, he turned to look in the direction of a collapsing planet. In the middle of that planet was a continent that was only about half-intact thanks to the way the planet was falling apart.

On that continent was a mountain and some lakes that made a face. Thanks to the collapse of the planet, the continent couldn’t stay in one piece. And even if it had been in one piece, the cloud cover would have made it difficult to spot the face. Nevertheless, Xu Qing spotted it.

However, right when he was just about to go through the rift, he suddenly sensed an aura behind him that was familiar and unfamiliar at the same time. The moment he sensed it, his cultivation base erupted. Two types of authority flared, and he spun in place to look out into the void.

Some distance away, he saw ripples spreading out. The moment he spotted them, he could see that there was something right in the middle of the ripples.

It was a mask! And it looked exactly like the face that Xu Qing had personally seen twice. This time, however, it had materialized in the form of a mask. From the look of it, this was its true form. It was facing Xu Qing, as if inspecting him. At the same time, it was swaying back and forth like grass in the wind, as if it were just waiting to speed off into the distance.

Xu Qing’s guard went up and he refrained from taking action. He just waited in front of the rift, watching.

When I went looking for it, it hid from me. But when I gave up, it appeared.

An incense stick’s worth of time passed. Neither party moved an inch. They just inspected each other. The mask had stopped swaying back and forth. Apparently, the fact that Xu Qing held back from taking action caused it to lower its guard.

Eventually, Xu Qing narrowed his eyes and began to devise a plan about how to get the mask. Almost as if it had sensed his thoughts, the mask blurred as if it was about to disappear.

Xu Qing frowned and cast aside any thoughts of making a move on the mask, and instead focused on the concept of not searching for it.... In fact, he even went so far as to abandon any sort of desire for the mask.

The moment he did that, the mask went from blurry to clear again. It looked at Xu Qing for a moment. And then its lips moved as it spoke in an emotionless voice.

“What is your wish?”

Xu Qing’s sense of vigilance grew. Considering he had no idea what this mask was, there was no way he was going to reply to it. He had seen many gruish things in his life, and as a result, he knew that there were certain things that were best left unsaid. As Xu Qing thought about that, the mask seemed to decide that, since he wasn’t responding, it would leave, and it started to blur again.

Eyes flashing, Xu Qing suddenly said, “I wish for....”

When those three words left his mouth, the mask became crystal clear again. As it looked at him, he backed into the rift. He vanished. When he reappeared, he was no longer on the level with the star chart. He was back on the level with the red candle.

Heat and light battered against him. Ignoring that, he looked at the rift to see if the mask would follow him. Before long... ripples pulsed out of the rift, followed a moment later by the mask.

It looked at Xu Qing. It seemed to be waiting for him to finish explaining his wish.

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing shot off into the distance, all while keeping an eye on the mask.

The mask seemed to hesitate briefly before chasing after him. Perhaps it was because of what he had said. Perhaps because he had not actually stated his wish, some karma had developed.

The mask didn’t flee. It kept following him. It lasted for about half an incense stick’s worth of time. At that point, Xu Qing suddenly reversed momentum, shooting backward toward the mask. And thus, before the mask could successfully blur away, he grabbed it. There it rested, looking at him, apparently waiting for him to finish stating the contents of his wish.

No expression could be seen on Xu Qing’s face as he casually put the mask into his sleeve. He didn’t feel comfortable putting it into his bag of holding, as it was a living thing. And sealing it might be taken as a malicious act that could break the equilibrium he had created. What was more, based on the little test he had just carried out, he got the feeling that the mask would stick with him until he finished stating his wish. And thus, his sleeve seemed like the most suitable storage place. freewebnovel.com

As for what the mask was, and the karma of the wish, and even the white dust, Xu Qing decided that it would be best to try to learn more about them only after he left the World Origin Pocket Realm. Seeing that he had accomplished his main goal, and that staying in this place meant risking absorption, he took out his World Origin Pocket Realm entrance medallion and triggered the exit function.

Unfortunately, the moment he did, the distant red candle flared brightly, and the light seemed to focus direction on him. Whether it was because of that light or because of some other reason... the medallion didn’t do anything!

Xu Qing looked at the red candle off in the distance.

Is the candle preventing me from leaving because I have the mask? Or was it something else that caused it to start shining more brightly...? Maybe it’s all just a coincidence.

He tried to use the medallion again, and again, the candle flared. Nothing happened. Something malicious seemed to be going on, and it caused Xu Qing’s expression to turn grim.

It’s not letting me go?

Keeping his eye on the distant red candle, Xu Qing backed up a bit. Then, skirting the halo of light surrounding the candle, he flew in the direction of the rift leading to the second level. Upon nearing the area, he found... that the rift was gone.

Not only is it not letting me leave, but also, the rift to the second level vanished. But why...?

Looking grim, he pondered the situation, eventually coming up with three possibilities.

First, it could be related to the mask. Maybe it’s the karma I developed with the mask. Or maybe the mask is incapable of leaving the pocket dimension. Perhaps the power of the mask itself is preventing me from leaving until I complete my wish.

Second, it could be related to the candle. I do have a special body, so maybe it has malicious intentions directed at me. Maybe it wants me to stay so it can absorb me.

Third, maybe it’s that godly authority of luck from before! Although I have a bit of control over that godly authority, in the end, it’s not complete. Maybe it evolved in some unexpected way. Or maybe the luck causes misfortune later on.

Xu Qing checked his godly authority of misfortune to see if it was any more active than before. Unfortunately, all he had were speculations that couldn’t be proven or disproven.

I suppose it’s also possible that it’s a combination of all three possibilities. In that case, the way to deal with this situation is....

As Xu Qing frowned in thought, an icy will suddenly gathered around him. Instantly, he shot backward. Loud cracking sounds rang out from the spot he had just occupied, as that entire area froze solid.

Xu Qing’s eyes turned pitch black as he used the Shadow Fusion Secret Magic. In an instant, a host of grieves became visible to him, surging maliciously toward him from all directions. From the way they were acting, it seemed as if they were being controlled by some external force.

A moment later, a huge sun rose within Xu Qing, and the profound sun immortal light shone out. Beams of immortal light stabbed out in all directions, shattering the ice, and causing countless shadows to howl in grief. In the blink of an eye, more than half of the grieves around Xu Qing were gone.

He blurred into motion. However, the remaining shadows were still racing toward him.

How can there be so many? It doesn’t seem possible!

Xu Qing fled while simultaneously emitting immortal light. At the moment, he was in quite a passive position, and all the while, the flame of the red candle sent its light pulsing out. With every pulse of light, the surrounding painting of stars transformed. And when the candle light touched Xu Qing, his soul started sizzling.

These shadows aren’t just cultivators from the Devilbird holy lands that died here! The World Origin Pocket Realm is extremely old. Older than the holy land. Before it came to the Revered Ancient mainland, it definitely passed through other worlds. It stands to reason... that that’s why it accumulated so many of these shadows!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with killing intent. He could tell at a glance that these shadows were trying to kill him. Therefore, since Xu Qing could see them, he could kill them, not only with immortal light, but with other methods. Rumbling sounds echoed out as masses of xeno-immortal soul threads shot out from him, accompanied by godly authority. Wherever they passed, shadows exploded.

Unfortunately, the sense of crisis within Xu Qing didn’t lessen at all. Instead, it grew more intense. And that was because the flame of the red candle was causing his soul to feel more and more like it was burning. At the same time, the star painting that was the World Origin Pocket Realm was changing rapidly. It was almost as if painted eyes were opening and staring at him with boundless greed.

The sense of crisis they imparted to Xu Qing continued to grow. In addition to burning, his soul was starting to crack and crumble. It was as if the painted eyes were exerting a terrifying force onto his soul, to try to drag it out of him.

There was more. What caused Xu Qing’s heart to sink even further was the sensation that his soul was transforming from something formless into something with a form.

And it was the form of a painting! He was currently transforming into a painting! Put precisely, it was a canvas made from a fleshly body with a design painted on it that resembled a soul.

Being fused with Little Shadow makes it possible to see all these other shadows. That’s why I can attack them. However... there is balance in all things. Because I can see them, the red candle can also see me... and that’s why I’m being absorbed so quickly. But if I exit this state, then I won’t be able to see the shadows, and I won’t be able to wipe them out!

It was like a deadly paradox.

Looking very grim, Xu Qing unfused with Little Shadow. As his eyes ceased to be pitch black, he also ceased to feel the sensation of his soul being ripped out of him. Unfortunately, because he couldn’t see the grieves around him, and thus couldn’t fight back against them, he had no choice but to just run away and try to find a way to escape the pocket realm.

Sadly, the red candle ensured that every attempt he made met with failure. Whenever he activated the medallion, it failed to work.

Eventually, despite not being fused with Little Shadow, he could see the signs that he was being absorbed by the red candle. His fleshly body seemed fine. But his soul was gradually being affected. In fact, even his thoughts were being influenced, as if they were starting to corrode.

Beyond that, the fate lineaments from Xu Qing’s incarnated form of Sir Blood Dust were unexpectedly being melted by the gruish candle. As a result, he couldn’t maintain the form. His disguise, and everything he had done to connect himself to the real Sir Blood Dust, were being undone.

Of course, when it rains, it pours. Either that, or the third possibility Xu Qing had considered was coming true. After all of the luck he had experienced, he started to see signs of very familiar misfortune...

A cultivator appeared in front of him! This was the first living person Xu Qing had encountered since coming to the pocket realm.

It was a three-world Smoldering God cultivator. Apparently, he hadn’t been here for very long, and was in the middle of seeking enlightenment. However, the dramatic things that were going on caused him to emerge from his enlightenment and look around suspiciously. He quickly caught sight of Xu Qing. The Devilbird cultivator’s jaw dropped, and his expression became one of utter incredulity.

“Xu Qing?”

Given how utterly famous Xu Qing was among humankind, now that his disguise was gone, he was recognized instantly. And it made complete sense that, as soon as the cultivator recognized him, he took out his medallion and activated it to leave. The medallion immediately caused a vortex to appear.

It looked like he was about to make his escape. But then Xu Qing’s eyes glinted with cold light, and he shot forward with a burst of speed. Rumbling sounds accompanied his movement. Unfortunately, as he neared the vortex, the red candle pulsed with light, and the vortex was wiped out of existence. The Devilbird cultivator’s teleportation portal had been severed.

Xu Qing was still stuck.

It was hard to say if the misfortune was striking Xu Qing or the other cultivator. Maybe it was hitting both of them at the same time. After all, Xu Qing did command the godly authority of misfortune....

Xu Qing didn’t have time to break down the exact reason right now. Seeing that the other cultivator’s teleportation had been unsuccessful caused a grimace to appear on Xu Qing’s face.

As for the Devilbird cultivator, he was backing away in astonishment. However, before he could get more than thirty meters away, a tremor passed through him, and his eyes went black. It was as if something else was controlling him. Suddenly looking at Xu Qing with deep greed, he shot forward and began a self-detonation.

A rumbling boom echoed out. A moment later, Xu Qing was fleeing the area.

The detonation of a three-world Smoldering God couldn’t harm his fleshly body. But it would have an effect on his soul, which was currently in the middle of being absorbed. Thankfully, after that, he didn’t encounter any other cultivators seeking enlightenment. After all, getting into the World Origin Pocket Realm required a huge amount of battle credit, so it wasn’t common for cultivators to come in.

Unfortunately, Xu Qing still hadn’t come up with a plan to get away. More grieves were chasing after him. The absorption effects were getting more severe.

Eventually, Xu Qing could sense very clearly that the entire pocket realm was pulsing with malicious intentions. In fact, as he went along, there were planets and worlds that, despite clearly not being about to detonate, would be influenced by the flame, and would explode.

There were even empty spots with nothing in them, where planets would appear out of nowhere and then explode. The destructive forces unleashed by such detonations were impossible for Xu Qing to defend against. Most ridiculous of all was that the red candle seemed to be losing patience. Every pulse of the flame would cause explosions.

The candle was like a volcano, sending intense light throughout the World Origin Pocket Realm, which melted everything. From the look of it, everything inside the pocket realm was going to end up melted.

Planets. Worlds. Dust.... The red candle was burning with such intensity, that the candle itself was starting to disappear.

It wants to exterminate me. It doesn’t want any trace of me left alive. My only options are to somehow get the empress to realize that something unusual is going on, or to last until the candle burns itself out.

In the case of the former, I’m in a passive position. In the case of the latter, well, I have no idea how long that will take. Besides, what if the candle just resets after it burns out? After all, this could all be because of the karma of the mask! Most importantly of all is that I really can’t afford to wait around.

After trying many options, none of which worked, Xu Qing’s eyes erupted with killing intent. There was only one option left. Stopping in place, he turned to look at the burning candle with determination filling his gaze. Going forward, everything pointed to disaster.

“Since you won’t let me leave, and want to absorb me...”

Xu Qing’s eyes filled with ferocity and a crazy look. And then he shot toward the core of the World Origin Pocket Realm, which was none other than the red candle.

This final option was going to be extremely dangerous. Maybe it wouldn’t work. After all, the three possibilities he had considered all ended with him being absorbed. Whether it was the karma of the mask or the influence of the candle, he couldn’t leave this place.

The greedy candle wanted to absorb him. The godly authority of good luck was followed by misfortune.

“... well, I’ll absorb you!”

His eyes were completely bloodshot as he shot toward the flickering candle flame, followed by countless shadows. He was like a shooting star, or perhaps a moth flying toward the flame. Either way, he was... pressing forward!

Xu Qing moved with stupefying speed, flitting through the light cast by the red candle. He was like a meteor shattering the void and shaking the cosmos. As he neared, he was moving so fast his entire body started glowing red. Boundless light and heat battered his face.

In the blink of an eye, he was completely enveloped. Countless grieves charged in his directions, all while planets and worlds exploded to block his path. From the look of it, everything in the entire pocket realm was trying to stop him.

It didn’t seem to make sense! If this candle really wanted to absorb him, why was it blocking his path? After all, he was literally acting like a moth rushing toward the flame. It should have welcomed him. Yet, not only was it very clear that he was being blocked, but also, as Xu Qing sped forward, the effects grew even more pronounced. Planets blew up constantly. And the candle’s flame danced more violently.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered, and without any hesitation, he sent his divine will out. An instant later, he and Little Shadow fused, causing his eyes to turn pitch black. As a result, all of the explosions transformed into a painting. That allowed him to avoid their effects.

Also, the previously invisible grieves were now visible en masse to Xu Qing. He could sense their anxiety and madness. They were trying to block his path, all while ganging up on him from behind.

Seeing all that, Xu Qing just accelerated. He tapped into his cultivation base, godly authority, and cultivator authority. The sun rose within him, and regardless of how red his fleshly body glowed, or his soul burned, he viciously charged forward.

You don’t want me to go forward? Then I’m gonna go forward!

All of a sudden, the shadows surrounding him began dissipating. As the candle flame flickered, Xu Qing reached a point only 3,000 meters away from the candle itself! At that point, his fleshly body was doing well, but his soul was having trouble. Countless flames seeped through the cracks in his skin, converging in his sea of consciousness and burning his soul.

The effects of absorption and melting spread dramatically. In that moment of crisis, a crazy look flashed in Xu Qing’s eyes. Then, his soul flickered, transforming into millions upon millions of soul threads that swept through his sea of consciousness, becoming a vortex that fought back against the candle flames.

Relying on that, he continued onward. He was now only 1,500 meters away.

Soul threads were being wiped out of existence with every moment that passed, either turning into ash that disappeared, or becoming grieves. Yet Xu Qing was only accelerating. Screaming onward, he reached 900 meters. Then 600 meters.... About ninety percent of his soul threads had disappeared. With only a small portion left, he finally bridged the gap.

He was now right above the red candle, directly over its flame. There, he settled down cross-legged, closed his eyes, and then dropped into the fire. He was planning to use his own fleshly body to extinguish the flame!

The flame flickered dramatically, almost as if it had a will of its own, and had been caught completely by surprise by this action. It simply couldn’t understand why someone would rush headlong right into death.

The flame of the red candle burned wildly, forcing Xu Qing to a halt. Then it burned many times hotter than before, causing the flames to spread out and completely cover him. His fleshly body dealt with the onslaught. But the flames seeped into him, filling his sea of consciousness and spreading out over his void soil. What remaining xeno-immortal soul threads he had left were being rapidly wiped out.

But then, Xu Qing’s eyes opened, and he looked down at the red candle.

“I don’t know if you have a connection to the mask. But I know you have your own will. That’s why I mentioned absorbing you. I was hoping you would let me approach you. And though I wasn’t lying...” his eyes glittered. “... do the two of you really think I was only thinking about a wish?”

Xu Qing had benefited greatly on this trip into the World Origin Pocket Realm.

First, he encountered the star chart of the thirty-six star rings. The majestic map had really opened his eyes about the world he lived in.

Next, he found the true origin of the white dust he’d found on Sir Blood Dust. It came from the Mask of Wishes!

For unknown reasons, the candle maliciously prevented him from leaving. And yet, Xu Qing still wasn’t inclined to use that wish. And that was because... he had a speculation that had been turning around in his mind for a while now.

Now, things had been made clear. When analyzing previous events from every possible angle, the only explanation seemed to be pointing to the wish as the only way out. Or at least, that seemed to be what the red candle was forcing him to do! That was why Xu Qing was even less inclined to do it.

Before fully studying the mask, he didn’t want to casually use it. After all, it was a gruish thing, and based on Xu Qing’s understanding, there was nothing in the world that came easily and didn’t have consequences. That was especially true when it came to things like wishes. A wish would definitely come with a cost. And it made sense that, the greater the wish, the greater the price to be paid.

That was especially true considering that the mask had a certain level of consciousness. It wasn’t inanimate. And therefore, it was highly likely it could resort to schemes and trickery.

All of those things, including the price to be paid for using the mask, were unknowns.

Perhaps the price to be paid for the wish was longevity. Maybe it would come with some sort of tribulation. Maybe you would have to give up a person or object that you cared deeply about. Maybe you would lose memories or even your soul. All of those things were within the realm of possibility. Therefore, he wanted to know the precise details of the price to be paid.

If he made a wish, and was then forced to pay the price no matter what, it could lead to very dire consequences. That was why he had just put the mask away without stating his wish. Logically speaking, if he wanted to leave this place without making the wish, there was only one option.

And that was to charge right into the source of all the danger, which was the candle itself! He would use his fleshly body to extinguish the flame! He would use death to seek life. He would make an opportunity in the moment of most extreme danger. Of course, doing that required coming to the candle itself.
