When Xu Qing spoke the word ‘absorb’ out loud, he was hoping to convince the candle to let him get near it. There was another reason for his decision. He believed in the strength of his fleshly body!

In the star chart depicting the thirty-six star rings, the Ninth Star Ring featured Eminent Desolation, which exerted a force of attraction on the symbols to the east, west, south and north. That alone went to show how terrifying the broken face was. Considering that hīs flesh and blood had been used to make Xu Qing’s fleshly body, it could definitely stand up to the flame of this candle.

The only weakness in the plan was his own soul! His soul couldn’t stand up to the flame. But Xu Qing had already made his decision!

“We’re going to see which will be extinguished first. My soul, my fleshly body, or your flame!”

Even as the words left his mouth, and as the flames burned in his sea of consciousness, Xu Qing unhesitatingly activated all of the one hundred faint godly authority lineaments in his void soil. Those lineaments came from the flesh and blood of the broken face, and Xu Qing had not yet gained enlightenment of them all. Although they increased the upper limits he could reach in terms of strength and power, they also created an obstacle that he had to break through. Therefore, if he could burn them away, it would be a good way to achieve a level of balance.

Xu Qing was partly correct in this line of thinking. But he was also partly incorrect!

The nearly one hundred lineaments of godly authority really could be ignited and used to fight back against the candle flame. However, they were not true godly authority. They were just illusory sealing marks that were similar to snapshots. No matter how they burned, such sealing marks were fundamentally impossible to erase. At the very most, any impurities within them would be removed. As a result, the flames did not achieve the result Xu Qing had anticipated.

Although that was disheartening, he had a backup plan!

“Godly authority of good luck!”

Without any hesitation, he sacrificed the godly authority of good luck by throwing it into the flames. The godly authority ignited, sending out massive amounts of godliness, which fought back against the candle fire and protected Xu Qing’s soul.

It was a crazy plan!

It could well be said that, whether in ancient times or modern, it was a very rare thing to burn godly authority. For one thing, no god would be willing to give up godly authority. Furthermore, any flame that could actually burn godly authority would be extremely precious, and running into it would require a destined opportunity.

Thanks to burning the godly authority of good luck, Xu Qing was able to buy some time. Rumbling sounds echoed out as his fleshly body came into a sitting position atop the candle flame.

The flame flickered wildly as it sank down. It wanted to immolate this fleshly body, but it couldn’t. All it could do was sink down under its weight. That said, the candle still fought back just as hard as before, by sending more fire into Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness.

Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness was full of towering flames. The godly authority of good luck continued to burn until about ninety-nine percent of it was gone. Only a scrap remained. That scrap glittered with golden light; apparently, it wasn’t possible to completely wipe it out.

Upon seeing this, Xu Qing’s thoughts raced. However, there wasn’t time for contemplation. Next, he tossed out the godly authority of misfortune as a sacrifice, causing it to spread out and resist the flames. Rumbling sounds filled his sea of consciousness as more flames entered it, adding to the conflagration. The godly authority of misfortune rapidly disappeared until there was only a scrap left!

Without any hesitation, Xu Qing sacrificed his next portion of godly authority. That was the violet moon! The godly authority of the violet moon surrounded him and fought against the candle flames.

Xu Qing’s fleshly body had now completely sunk down into the flame of the red candle. Now, the wick was right underneath him! As the candle flickered violently, the godly authority of the violet moon in Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness dissipated rapidly. In the end, it ended up just like the previous two types of godly authority. It was only a golden thread!

Xu Qing gritted his teeth as he prepared to sacrifice more godly authority. But then something gruish happened to the candle that completely surpassed anything Xu Qing had predicted would happen.

Luck. Misfortune. Violet moon.... The three golden threads of godly authority suddenly spun into motion and began to interweave with each other. Thēy didn’t fuse. It was more like a braid, and it emanated dazzling golden light.

As a result, the candle flame was halted.

A terrifying aura erupted from the interwoven threads of three types of godly authority. The aura seemed to exist on a higher level than space-time, as if it could control all living beings. Yet it didn’t seem complete. Despite being incomplete, the aura it emanated was immeasurably terrifying, and surpassed any and all godly authorities that Xu Qing had ever encountered.

Before Xu Qing could perceive any details about it, the aura began to dissipate as surely as the night queen flower that only blooms for an instant. They had only formed because of a freak combination of factors, and could not fuse permanently. Because they weren’t complete, they were apparently going to unravel.[1]

Before they could, the shaken Xu Qing pulled them back into his sea of consciousness, and the candle flame there, so that they could sustain the force of the flame instead of his soul. The fire raged. Outside, the candle was just on the verge of being extinguished. At that point, the candle went all out, sending flames shooting out madly into Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness. This effort surpassed anything from before.

As they burned, the three portions of godly authority that had been just about to unravel... suddenly started fusing together.

1. The ‘queen of the night,’ which I’m rendering in a slightly nonstandard way as ‘night queen flower,’ is a species of cactus that blooms in the night and wilts before dawn. More information here. ☜

Although Xu Qing only had a limited understanding of godly authority, he did have significant experience with it, whether because of his own godly authority, or by means of interacting with other gods.

For instance, he knew that godly authority and essence were different. Godly authority was much more ancient, and it was an authority that was unique to gods. Thēy could influence all things. They could affect any living being. And they were spread throughout the thirty-six star rings in the starry sky. That was because this was a universe of gods.

Simultaneously, godly authority was divided into two levels. The first level was the type that was split between those who qualified to use it. The other was the type that was unique to an individual. When it came to the former, it led to a situation in which various gods were forced to either cooperate or compete over it. Only by devouring all other gods with the same type of godly authority could the second level be reached. Anyone who succeeded at that would be the sole possessor of that type of godly authority.

Based on Xu Qing’s earlier understanding, the rare individuals who reached that level were the True Gods. Furthermore, based on Xu Qing’s previous understanding, godly authority wasn’t classified as being weak or strong. Rather, it came down to the level of control one had over it. And also... the range! Range was a very important factor when it came to godly authority.

However, just now, that previous understanding within Xu Qing was shaken. And that was because those three types of godly authority had weaved together to form a unique godly authority that emanated a terrifying aura that surpassed anything he had ever encountered. And it was enough for him to be able to easily distinguish the difference between weak and strong.

Xu Qing wasn’t sure what this new type of godly authority was. The best he could do was make an educated guess based on the characteristics of good luck, misfortune, and the violet moon.

Of course, there wasn’t time right now to delve into the details. As the candle flame erupted, his fleshly body sank down further toward the wick, pushing the candle ever closer to being extinguished....

Within Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness, the red candle’s flame was fighting back ferociously, and the flames were going absolutely wild.

This fire had no choice but to try to incinerate those three strands of godly authority. After all, those three types of godly authority had weaved together to make an unfamiliar godly authority that had surrounded his soul protectively. It was resisting the fire.

Despite that, the intensity of the heat was still harmful to Xu Qing’s soul. His soul threads were disappearing rapidly. And when their number dropped to 10,000... his clothing was completely burned out of existence! His body, bright red from the heat, landed onto the candle wick.

RUMBLE!

The moment he landed on the wick, a heaven-rending, earth-crushing boom swept through the World Origin Pocket Realm, causing everything to shake violently.

The candle flame was extinguished!

When it happened, the fire in Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness suddenly disappeared. His void soil, pockmarked with severe damage, and the unfamiliar godly authority formed from three strands of other godly authorities, then experienced a dramatic transformation.

Before, thēy had been unable to fuse, but thanks to the heat of the fire, they now appeared to be ten percent fused. A majestic aura of godly authority rose up from them, filling Xu Qing’s entire sea of consciousness.

Meanwhile, the extinguishing of the fire caused external transformations as well. As the last bits of light flowed out, the planets outside vanished. Some that were visible to the naked eye simply collapsed. Others, visible to the shadow eye as paintings, went away as if they had been erased. Simultaneously, all of the grieves faded away like smoke in the wind. It was as if the entire illusory world had become a thing of the past once the candle flame went away.

Everything sank into complete darkness. It was as if the entire World Origin Pocket Realm were vanishing into nothing.

Sometime later, Xu Qing, who was still in a cross-legged position, slowly opened his eyes. They were bloodshot and full of exhaustion. His soul was so weak that he felt like his head was spinning. He was surrounded by darkness. He couldn’t see anything in the distance, nor anything near him. There was no light, and even using the eyes of a god would reveal nothing but a void.

There was no trace of the candle beneath him. However, the sensation of having just barely survived a deadly crisis filled Xu Qing.

When the candle flame disappeared, the snapshot vanished....

He reached into his sleeve, felt the mask there, and then relaxed a bit.[1]

Xu Qing was not interested in staying in this place any longer than necessary. For all he knew, the candle might reappear soon, and everything might go back to exactly the way it had been before. He quickly took out the pocket realm medallion to leave.

But then, his expression flickered, and he looked over his shoulder. Other than the darkness, there was nothing out there behind him.

But Xu Qing was a vigilant person. And just now, he had sensed... something that indicated the candle had reappeared.

“Wait. No!”

He reached behind himself to touch his back, and as he did, his fingernails scraped against something unfamiliar. His heart lurched. The red candle actually hadn’t disappeared! For some unknown reason, the candle had been imprinted onto his back. To Xu Qing, it felt almost like a tattoo that filled his entire back. Thankfully, after feeling around a bit, he could confirm that the candle on his back was extinguished.

He frowned. Then, mind abuzz with countless thoughts, he pushed down on the medallion. Unfortunately... there was no response from it.

Previously, there had at least been a reaction from the medallion. The problem had been the candle interfering. But right now, it was as if there wasn’t even a connection between the medallion and the World Origin Pocket Realm.

“World Origin Pocket Realm...” he murmured. He pushed down on the medallion again.

***

Outside of the World Origin Pocket Realm, some astonishing things happened when the candle was extinguished.

First, the massive jade slip that contained the World Origin Pocket Realm, which usually shone with dazzling light, suddenly went dim. At the same time, the lands around it, which were usually lush and verdant, dried up so badly that the ground cracked. In fact, ravines spread out through the entire basin, and when they reached the mountains at the end, the mountains crumbled. It was as if the spirit energy had been sucked away.

As for the sealed area that housed the jade slip, it disappeared. As of now, any cultivator, even those who didn’t have entrance medallions, could look in and see the jade slip.

The Devilbirds who had gathered in the area to practice cultivation in the strong spirit energy were shocked to the core as they looked inside.

“The spirit energy here just vanished....”

“The sealing mark protecting the World Origin Pocket Realm just disappeared!”

“What just happened?”

***

On the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, ‘Lu Lingzi’ opened ‘his’ eyes in the hall at the top of the mountain. A frown appeared. Then, ‘he’ surreptitiously sent some divine will toward the location of the World Origin Pocket Realm to lock the area down. In the blink of an eye, the heaven and earth surrounding the World Origin Pocket Realm went still.

The divine will then entered the jade slip itself. And then, the empress, who despite being an extremely valiant person, was stricken with astonishment. It was only natural that shē had gone into the World Origin Pocket Realm, so shē knew a good deal about it.

But now, scanning the place with divine will revealed nothing but pitch black. The red candle was gone. The planets had vanished. Everything was a void.

However, there in the spot where the red candle had existed was Xu Qing, hovering cross-legged, clutching the medallion and trying one thing after another to get it to work.

The empress was taken aback. Then a moment passed, and hēr voice echoed into the void.

“What are you doing?”

Xu Qing went still. Inside, he was feeling very pleased. Looking out into the void, he said, “Well met, Your Majesty! Some strange things happened here earlier, so I tried to use this medallion to leave. Unfortunately, the medallion... just didn’t work.”

Xu Qing got to his feet, clasped hands, and bowed. He was well aware that the empress’ arrival meant that he had a way to get free now.

The empress didn’t respond to his words. It was only when Xu Qing was starting to formulate some more words that he heard a sigh.

“You didn’t listen to a thing I said, did you?” the empress said. “After you’re out of here, come see me immediately!”

At the same time, a majestic force swept through the void, swirled around Xu Qing, and turned into a huge vortex. A gravitational force sprang into being, dragging Xu Qing into the vortex. Then he and the vortex both disappeared.

After Xu Qing was gone, the empress appeared in blurry form. It was only a divine will clone. After looking around for a while, shē shook hēr head.

I used to think the Eldest Brother was the only one I had to worry about. I never could have guessed that Xu Qing’s just as bad.

The empress took a step forward and vanished. Upon reappearing in the outside world above the jade slip, shē pushed hēr hand down. Instantly, the jade slip lit up again. The sealing barrier once again sprang into being. Everything looked exactly as it had looked before. However, if anyone was able to enter and look inside the jade slip, they would find... that the World Origin Pocket Realm wasn’t there.

Of course, the empress couldn’t let that state of affairs continue to exist. Therefore, it wasn’t long before a dharmic decree was issued from the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. The World Origin Pocket Realm had run short of spirit energy, and would need a hundred years to recover. During that time, no one would be permitted entry. The World Origin Pocket Realm was now the property of the tenth Imperial Sovereign, and thus, Lu Lingzi’s dharmic decree would be honored.

It was a time of war, and though the World Origin Pocket Realm had been listed as a reward, the fact that Lu Lingzi was a new Imperial Sovereign meant that no one would bicker over such a dharmic decree. Imperial Sovereigns naturally had special privileges.

Of course, in order to truly cover up what really happened to the World Origin Pocket Realm would require further work on the part of the empress.

***

Xu Qing appeared on a plain about 50 kilometers away from the World Origin Pocket Realm. He looked nervous. As soon as he materialized, he once again assumed the form of Sir Blood Dust, then looked over his shoulder in the direction of the World Origin Pocket Realm.

At the moment, he wasn’t really sure how much he had benefited. He had the mask, but apparently, had also ended up with that gruish candle imprinted on his back. He had also made things more difficult for the empress, which he already regretted. That was his personality. He was the type of person who knew whom to show gratitude to, and whom to feel resentment against. And he didn’t like being in the debt of others.

After a moment he took a deep breath.

I need to go help the empress in whatever way I can. At the very least, I do whatever shē asks me to do.

With that, he shot off in the direction of the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain.

Along the way, he focused on the unfamiliar godly authority within him. Good luck was easy to understand based on its own name. It was the same with misfortune.

As for the godly authority of the violet moon, it involved violet moonlight shining down on living things, looking for flaws in their life force, and upon finding them, invading them with taboo poison.

It’s command of fortune, and also command of the flaws in life force. When thēy combine, thēy become a godly authority....

As Xu Qing raced along, he suddenly lurched to a stop. Hovering in midair, he struggled to control his breathing, all while his eyes shone with a bizarre light. All of a sudden, one word was echoing in his mind.

Is this... fate?[2]

1. His clothes were destroyed earlier, but apparently they are back now. ☜

2. This footnote gets into some nitty gritty stuff that most readers probably won’t care about. There is a bit of wordplay going on here, the type that often frustrates me. In this case we have a term (fate) that is actually made of two Chinese characters. The author has used this term for multiple series and thousands of chapters without doing a wordplay explanation (at least, not that I remember). Then, all of a sudden, he throws in some wordplay. Well, it is what it is. In this case, ‘fate’ is made up of two characters. Both of them can be interpreted in different ways. The first one could mean life, but also can mean fate/destiny/command as well as other things. The second character can mean even more things, but among them are fortune/fate/luck. So in the paragraph above we have multiple levels of wordplay, in which Xu Qing mentions command, life, fortune, etc. Long story short, all of his thought process revolves around the two characters that I normally render as ‘fate.’ That’s why his conclusion in Chinese seems to make more sense than it does in English. Of course, all of this is further complicated by the fact that there are a host of Chinese words and characters that all mean fate/fortune/destiny, etc. The next chapter will have more information about the wordplay explanation of ‘fate’ as used here. And incidentally, later wordplay makes it very clear that the correct interpretations are the ones I’ve picked (life and fortune), although the ‘fortune’ one is more open to translator preference. ☜

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered, and his heart pounded. He was reeling mentally.

Although he couldn’t be totally sure of the level of this godly authority... the fact that it was a combination of three other types of godly authority was a clear indication of the personhood involved.

But is it fate or not?

He lifted his right hand, and the unfamiliar godly authority that resembled fate glittered brightly, then vanished from within him. When it reappeared, it was in the middle of his palm. And it took the shape... of a carving knife![1]

He could actually feel it, as if it were a corporeal object, yet at the same time, it seemed illusory. The moment it appeared, the air around it seemed to become sticky, as if it had been affected by the knife.

Xu Qing got the sensation that this knife could cut anything, whether that be the land, the sky, the grass, or the mountains.

One swipe of this knife could alter a trajectory. And the new trajectory would be completely outside of the scope of the original trajectory. It was a vague feeling, so vague, in fact, that Xu Qing couldn’t mentally grasp the totality of it. It was as if there were a veil covering the substructure of this godly authority, making it impossible for him to fully grasp it.

However, there was one thing he was certain of.

It seems highly likely that this is the godly authority of fate. However, it’s a bit different from fate as I currently understand it....

Xu Qing was reeling so much he simply couldn’t maintain a state of calm. That was because, when he thought back to everything he had experienced, and everything he understood, he realized that he had encountered a person who seemed to have abilities that were similar to a godly authority that affected fate.

And that person was the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan! Zi Qing could command fate!

Xu Qing took a deep breath as he thought back to what he had seen Zi Qing accomplish. Everything was there in his memories.

Zi Qing used the broken face of Eminent Desolation to effect a resurrection of himself. Does that mean his godly authority is somehow connected to the broken face? As for me... my fleshly body comes from the flesh and blood of Eminent Desolation. And now, due to a freak combination of factors, I’ve acquired something akin to authority over fate.

Is there some sort of karma at play here? What’s more, Zi Qing’s fate magic also relates to time. In that case... what does my godly authority do?

A moment later, he cleared his mind. He knew that he didn’t understand this new godly authority well enough. And if he wanted to understand it, he needed to learn more about it.

Instead of blindly groping on his own, it made more sense to ask for help. And since his Master wasn’t around, the best person to ask was the empress. The empress was a god, and an Altar God at that. Asking the empress about godly authority might even yield better results than asking for information from his Master.

With that thought in mind, Xu Qing looked up, then blurred into motion toward the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. Along the way, he didn’t spend time thinking about the godly authority that seemed to relate to fate. Instead, he nourished his soul and observed his other godly authorities.

Sound. Taboo poison....

After some observation, he was certain that this godly authority of fate was definitely very strong. Next, he focused on his back tattoo of the candle, as well as the mask.

Thus, time passed. Two days.

Given how fast he was moving, he was now only about an hour away from the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. By now, he had reached some conclusions about the candle.

The candle has thoroughly fused with my fleshly body. It’s as if it changed carriers. Before, the carrier was the snapshot jade slip. But now it’s my fleshly body. Maybe the way to shift carriers is to extinguish it. Even though it’s extinguished, I get the sensation that it could be lit again. However, I need to make some special preparations beforehand. And I need more time to ascertain the details.

What was more, his study up to this point seemed to indicate that the tattoo wasn’t going to harm him.

And then there’s the mask.

Xu Qing pulled the mask out and looked at it. It was looking back at him, seemingly still waiting for him to state his wish.

It’s made from an unknown substance. It does have intelligence of its own, but not much. If I don’t make a wish, it will just keep following me around. I still don’t know what price needs to be paid for the wish. But given how intent it is on following me around, that price must be significant.

In reality, the reason he started making a wish wasn’t because he actually had a wish he wanted granted. He had another purpose. From the very beginning, he’d had only one purpose in mind. And that was... to acquire a way to avoid karma. That white dust had been the focus from the beginning.

Xu Qing looked up, and authority glittered in his eyes as he looked at his own fate threads. The threads connected to things in all directions, and they were dazzling to say the least. There were also a few of them that were completely terrifying. However, as of now, Xu Qing realized that upon some of those fate threads, he could see... white dust. The white dust had appeared without fanfare, and was on the very edges of his fate threads.

Could it be that merely contacting the mask caused the white dust to appear in my fate?

After some thought, he looked away from the mask. That was when, prompted by a sudden impulse, he thought about his godly authority that was apparently related to fate.

If I could take that godly authority and put it into my fate threads, what would happen?

The moment the thought occurred to him, it rapidly became the only thing he could think about. And the desire to test it out caused his eyes to shine with determination.

I guess I’ll test it out!

Without the slightest hesitation, he waved his right hand, causing what seemed to be the godly authority of fate to fly out and form a carving knife in front of him. Then he sent it flying toward his fate threads. It entered the threads, and then Xu Qing carefully restrained the knife so that it didn’t cut anything. He just kept it there, motionless.

When the carving knife entered his fate, it hovered... until something unbelievable happened. A black stream of light emerged from the carving knife, covering Xu Qing’s fate threads. Next, the white dust vibrated, then floated up, separating from the fate threads until it hovered in the air, completely alone.

The sensation that filled Xu Qing next rocked him to the core. His expression flickered, something that rarely happened, and his jaw nearly dropped.

When the light from the carving knife covered his fate threads, the sensation he experienced was like bursting out of water and suddenly being able to breathe.

His soul felt unbounded and free. And his body felt far more unrestrained than before. In fact, he had the strong feeling and perception that, previously, he had been living in a state of asphyxiation. It was like he had been stuck in the mud, bound and restrained.

Without having experienced the current sensation, though, he would never have been able to realize that his past state had been one of asphyxiation and restraint. Clarity was only possible through comparison between the two! It seemed as if, only as of this moment was he able to control his own fate.

Xu Qing struggled to control his breathing. The comparison between these two states was completely unexpected. At the same time, a new type of perception filled him.

Is this the sensation of being able to control fate?

At the same instant in which Xu Qing gained control of his fate, far away in the Revered Ancient mainland, other entities sensed what was happening.

***

In Revered Ancient, there was a region full of dark mist, where the mutagen levels surpassed all other areas. Terrifying howls rang out everywhere, echoing back and forth so that there was never silence.

Within the boundless black haze, there was an imperial palace that was so massive it was like a city. A deathly silence filled the grand hall of the imperial palace.

An unusually handsome man sat on the imperial throne. His forehead was currently resting on his hand, and his eyes were closed. A moment later, his eyes opened, and he looked up into the sky. He frowned.

“You’re cutting ties?” he murmured. A moment later, his expression softened, and he smiled faintly. “How amusing, lil’ bro.”

***

Waves rolled across the surface of the depths of the outer sea. Black threads rose up, converging in midair to form Yu Liuchen, who hovered there cross-legged. Hē was currently absorbing what hē had acquired recently.

Normally speaking, hē shouldn’t have woken up before the absorption process was complete. But now, an indescribable feeling had filled hīm, something hē had never experienced before. Having been woken up, hē looked up into the sky.

A character from one of my stories just disappeared....

***

In the Devilbird holy land, at the summit of the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, the empress in Lu Lingzi form opened hēr eyes. Shē looked down the mountain, hēr expression quizzical. About an hour later, a voice rang up from that area.

“Sir Blood Dust here, seeking an audience with the Imperial Sovereign!”

After some thought, shē reached down and made a grasping gesture. A moment later, Xu Qing appeared in front of hēr in the grand hall. He immediately bowed at the waist and opened his mouth to speak.

Before he could, the empress’ voice echoed out. “My clone was present in that pocket realm but didn’t see any clues about what was going on. It was only when the godly authority was used that I sensed it.... Xu Qing, you have a new type of godly authority. Its name is... fate!”

Xu Qing looked up at the empress.

The empress had answered the very question he came to ask. Clearly, shē had a much deeper understanding of godly authority than he did.

Taking a deep breath, he respectfully said, “Your Majesty, could you explain a bit more?”

The empress looked down at him for a moment.

“Fate, predestination, luck. All refer to the trajectory of constants and variables among living things in the world. They are also paramount godly authorities in the cultivation system of gods.

“However, life and fortune are two completely different concepts.

“Life is a constant, and it relates to a specific trajectory. It fundamentally contains various paths.

“During the battle in which I reached godly ascension, you personally witnessed the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan control the fate of another. In the hands of Zi Qing, the fate of others takes the form of a book. By means of fate, hē can see the past, and can thus deduce the future. The future contains infinite possibilities, and yet fundamentally speaking, they all exist. What hē does is take one future, extract it, and use it to replace all the others. By doing so, hē can transform and influence the fate of another person.”

Up to this point, Xu Qing felt like he mostly understood what was being said, and it felt like everything was becoming clear. At the same time, he was reeling mentally. He could still picture the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan taking action, and remembered the power of his godly authority.

“Do you mean,” he murmured, “that the trajectories of the countless futures that Zi Qing can perceive are all real? They’re all constants? At the same time, they are all part of the ‘life’ that exists in the godly authority of fate?”

The empress nodded. “Meanwhile, fortune acts as the variable. It refers to the lineaments that exist outside the constants. Put more precisely, they are other paths that might be hewn out. They are paths that didn’t previously exist. But by the mixture of good luck and misfortune, they are created, and they surpass the range of what is set. That is what is meant by variables. Your godly authority relates to the fortune within fate. The variables!”

Xu Qing took a deep breath as his train of thought grew clearer. “Your Majesty, do you mean that my godly authority of fate uses good luck and misfortune to tamper with someone’s destiny? It creates a new fate that’s outside of the constants?”

The empress nodded. “Your understanding is correct. You and Zi Qing both have a godly authority of fate, and though they both have the same origin, they go in different directions. Yet both can be described in the same way.

“Anything and everything is possible. When talking about constants, there are infinite trajectories, any one of which could become manifest. When talking about variables, it’s only natural that it’s possible to create a new path to replace the original.”

Xu Qing closed his eyes to digest what the empress had just told him. After a while, he opened his eyes, and they shone with bright clarity.

“In other words, the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan has a godly authority of fate that resembles a book. The reason is that it deals with fate that has already been written. Zi Qing can flip through that book and find one page that hē finds suitable.

“In contrast, my godly authority of fate resembles a carving knife.... And īts function isn’t to flip through a book. Rather, īt functions to carve a new trajectory of fate to become a new page.”

1. The ‘carving knife’ here could also be rendered as ‘burin,’ ‘graver,’ or ‘engraving knife.’ If you do an image search, you will see that all these types of knives are basically the same thing. I would call it a hobby knife or craft knife. I watch a lot of YouTube hobby and crafting channels, and this is the type of knife you see people use when doing fine detail work to cut or carve small things. If you’re not familiar with this type of knife, here is a small image gallery. I don’t think the author envisions it as being a modern hobby knife, though. I think he just envisions a small knife with a delicate blade that could be used for carving things, thus, I’m going with ‘carving knife’ as the translation choice. Also, in a really weird coincidence, right before posting this chapter, a YouTuber I subscribe to released a video in which he used a hobby knife to carve a knife from wood. ☜

As Xu Qing’s voice echoed within the grand hall of the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, the empress looked up at him.

“It’s a paramount godly authority,” the empress said, “especially the variables of fortune. Not even I can see that clearly. All I can tell you is that the godly authority of the broken face Eminent Desolation is, put precisely, fate.

“When it comes to you and Zi Qing, one of you has a body made from Eminent Desolation’s flesh and blood. The other gained a new life as a family member of Eminent Desolation. At the same time, thanks to your Master’s saber strike, you were able to seize some of the destiny aura of the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan. As a result, the return of the sovereign kingdom wasn’t complete.

“And thus, in this life, you and Zi Qing are yet again closely related. All of it is because of the entanglements of fate. And all of it will come together at some point in the future. This discussion of constants and variables is also a debate between life and fortune. Or you could say that it’s a battle of fate between you and Zi Qing.”

The empress looked away from Xu Qing and into the sky, hēr eyes glistening... as if shē could already see that day. Those eyes quickly returned to normal.

Xu Qing didn’t say anything. When he saw the empress’ eyes go back to normal, he decided not to ask any further questions. Regardless of anything, whatever the empress could see would fall into the realm of constants. Shē could not see variables. Since Xu Qing himself had some control over fate, then when it came to the future, he would have to use his carving knife to make changes on his own behalf. After all, it could be used on his own life as well as others.

Looking very calm, Xu Qing clasped hands and bowed deeply to the empress. “Thank you, Your Majesty, for dispelling my confusion. By the way, is there anything else I can assist you with here in the Devilbird holy land? If there is, I will do everything in my power to be of benefit.”

The empress gave a slight nod. “Previously, I would have said no.”

Xu Qing blinked a few times. The implications of the empress’ words were evident.

“However,” the empress continued, “considering that you have a tendency to get restless, you’ll stick by my side going forward.

“Three days from now, I’ll be taking a trip as Lu Lingzi to the western Devilbirds. The plan is to offer formal greetings to Grand Emperor Devilbird and discuss the particulars of opening the secluded meditation facilities of Grand Emperor Netherflame. When the time comes, I want you to accompany me. For now, you can rest and recuperate outside of the hall. Your soul is obviously very weak, and it needs to recover.”

The empress waved a hand, sending a pill bottle and a jade slip flying over to him.

He caught them. Senses alone told him there was a medicinal pill in the bottle, and it was clearly something designed to nourish and replenish the soul. The jade slip served the same function. Feeling deeply appreciative, he bowed again, and then left the hall.

Outside, he took a deep breath, sat down cross-legged, and then consumed the pill. The pill entered his mouth and turned into streams of warmth that flowed into his sea of consciousness to bolster his soul. It was an extraordinary pill. When the effects reached his sea of consciousness, they became like rain falling onto withered plants and vegetation. Xu Qing’s dim and feeble soul immediately began to recover.

Three days passed.

Thanks to the medicinal pill, Xu Qing’s soul had recovered by about fifty percent. Although he wasn’t back to the same condition as before, his battle prowess hadn’t been affected very much. With a bit more recovery time, and the help of the jade slip, it wouldn’t take more than a month for him to be fully recovered.

After those three days passed, the empress emerged from the hall and floated up into the air.

Xu Qing rose and followed.

At the foot of the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, the gathered Devilbird cultivators looked up into the evening sky and bowed respectfully. The Imperial Sovereign was rising into the air. It was the first time ‘Lu Lingzi’ had made a public appearance after establishing the Imperial Sovereign mountain. Of course, everyone quickly noticed Xu Qing, and all of them were shaken. Some of them knew Sir Blood Dust, and quite a few of the people present had seen him go into the mountain before. That alone had been a shock.

But what was happening now was different. ‘Sir Blood Dust’ was following ‘Lu Lingzi.’ That meant that he had become an official attendant!

Going forward, ‘Sir Blood Dust’ would have a status and position that were completely different than before. In the future, even if he left the mountain alone, all of the gathered cultivators would bow worshipfully to him. Mixed emotions, including feelings of defiance, rose up in the hearts of many. But in the end, they suppressed such emotions. They didn’t dare to reveal how they truly felt. They only dared to reveal... respect.

As everyone bowed, Xu Qing followed the empress over the horizon.

The empress didn’t move at a high rate of speed. Yet every step shē took caused heaven and earth to blur, and sent visible Imperial Sovereign fluctuations rolling out in all directions. The empress’ actions were immediately noticed by the other Imperial Sovereigns among the eastern Devilbirds, and many gazes locked onto hēr.

Xu Qing instinctively retracted his aura. However, when he realized the empress didn’t seem worried at all, he felt more at ease. After all, shē was a peak Altar God. Clearly, shē was fully confident in going to see Grand Emperor Devilbird. Given that, he didn’t need to overthink things. Having reached this point in his train of thought, he looked up, and this time, he seemed very relaxed.

As the Imperial Sovereigns looked on, the empress took Xu Qing over the horizon. With only a few paces, they left the territory of the eastern Devilbirds and entered the lands of the western Devilbirds.

The moment they arrived, the gazes of even more Imperial Sovereigns locked onto them. In an instant, the lands began to tremble, and the air distorted. Traces of natural and magical laws glittered, as well as domineering streams of divine will. There wasn’t any ounce of courtesy being shown to the empress.

The empress’ face was completely expressionless as shē proceeded on hēr way. Xu Qing’s face was similarly blank as he kept his head bowed and followed hēr.

The western Devilbirds had more Imperial Sovereign mountains than the east did. They had twenty-one. But Xu Qing could sense from the gazes that they didn’t care about him very much at all. After merely glancing at him, they focused solely on the empress.

Xu Qing felt hardly any pressure at all. He was just a mere attendant. However, it was still clear to him that these gazes were not packed with good intentions. In fact, they were scornfully offering a warning to this new Imperial Sovereign from the east. That scorn contained deeper implications, of course, and thus, it didn’t just come from the Imperial Sovereigns.

It also came from Grand Emperor Devilbird. It didn’t seem to make any difference that the empress came to respectfully offer greetings.

After arriving at Grand Emperor Devilbird’s dao altar, the empress stated hēr purpose in coming. This Grand Emperor also had an apprentice present, who was a middle-aged cultivator that had also just recently become an Imperial Sovereign. He was the one who responded to the empress’ self-introduction. It came in the form of an order.

“Wait a moment!” The new Imperial Sovereign looked imperiously at the empress and coldly continued, “Lu Lingzi, you and I clashed years ago, and neither of us came out on top. Now that you’ve experienced a breakthrough, why don’t we settle things once and for all!”

His words boomed like thunder, and came with immense pressure.

The empress’ expression hadn’t changed at all the entire time. Nor had shē even glanced at Grand Emperor Devilbird’s apprentice. Turning to Xu Qing, shē calmly said, “Sir Blood Dust.”

“Here, sir!” Xu Qing bowed at the waist.

“Go swap pointers with all of the Smoldering God subordinates of the western Imperial Sovereign. While you’re at it, don’t besmirch the name of the eastern Devilbirds.” [1]

Those words caused all of the local Imperial Sovereigns to look at Xu Qing. Even the Imperial Sovereign who had voiced the order of the Grand Emperor looked over at him.

Xu Qing’s gaze hardened. He could tell what the empress wanted. Shē wanted him to make a scene. However, his most deadly abilities related to godly authority and cultivator authority. Therefore, the biggest problem was going to be not revealing the truth about his assets.

The empress had given orders, though, and there was no time to sit around contemplating matters. Without the slightest hesitation, he let loose a somber and desolate aura and said, “Your orders shall be followed!”

Then he blurred into motion and shot over the horizon.

The empress closed hēr eyes and said nothing further.

Meanwhile, Xu Qing was scrambling to make a plan. On the one hand, he was wondering what the empress might have done to make sure his true identity wasn’t revealed. At the same time, he was pouring through Sir Blood Dust’s memories to find information about the western Devilbirds.

The western Devilbirds have twenty-one Imperial Sovereign mountains. The strongest is the second. After that come the first, the third, and the seventeenth. The empress said to swap pointers. In that case, the most suitable first challenge will be...

Xu Qing looked north. That was where the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain was located.

That direction. As for how the empress is planning to keep my identity a secret, the most likely explanation....

Xu Qing rubbed the jade slip the empress had given him. He had assumed that jade slip was to nourish his soul. But now that he thought about it, it seemed highly likely that it was a special item that the empress had prepared for him to keep his true identity a secret.

Convinced that this assessment was correct, he unhesitatingly shot toward the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. He accelerated to top speed, causing a sonic boom to echo out. After the time it takes an incense stick to burn, he caught sight of the towering mountain up ahead.

As he closed in, he spoke in a thunderous voice that slammed into the mountain.

“I am Sir Blood Dust, subordinate of the tenth Imperial Sovereign of the eastern Devilbirds. I hereby challenge the Smoldering Gods of the western Devilbirds’ seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain!”

The response to his words was a cold snort that echoed out from the seventeenth mountain.

“Chen Fei, you go crush this kid!”[2]

Obviously, the local Imperial Sovereigns had all heard what the empress said to Xu Qing earlier. Since Lu Lingzi wasn’t personally making challenges, but was sending a subordinate out as a champion... then all they had to do was crush the subordinate, and Lu Lingzi would have no way to get out of fighting.

Even as the cold snort still echoed in the air, someone flew out from the mountain. It was a burly middle-aged cultivator whose cultivation base fluctuations were that of a seven-world Smoldering God. He glittered with dazzling light as he flew out, clasped hands respectfully to the mountain, then turned to look sharply at Xu Qing. Then he advanced at top speed. Seven major worlds erupted with power, creating a terrifying pressure.

At the same time, Xu Qing casually lifted his right hand, extended it in the direction of this Chen Fei, and then closed his fingers into a fist. His sound authority swept out.

The sound around Chen Fei became a deadly attack that swept him up. It was like a huge sphere around him in which all the sound waves became deadly ripples. Chen Fei’s face fell and his heart started pounding. However, what he saw wasn’t a sound attack. Instead, it was a host of shocking blood-red sealing marks. The blood seals pulsed with a gory sensation, as well as extraordinary power. And they made him feel very uneasy. In the blink of an eye, he lost the initiative.

At that moment of crisis, his seven major worlds surged with light, and at the same time, he performed a double-handed incantation gesture. Astonishingly, within his seven worlds, seven gruish statues appeared, each different from the other. Then all of them burst into motion, emerging from the worlds to attack Xu Qing with deadly force.

Xu Qing’s face was completely expressionless as he looked at the seven statues. Then, astonishingly, he vanished into the sound, only to reappear right behind Chen Fei.

Two types of authority glittered in his eyes. Looking at Chen Fei’s karma threads, he stirred the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures. Karma clamped down onto life, and the emotions went wild. It was a mental attack.

Next came the profound sun immortal light in the form of a huge sun rising above his sea of consciousness. It cast boundless light and heat that surrounded Chen Fei and then crushed down on him.

Rumbling booms rose into the sky as the authority of sound caused Chen Fei to lose any chance of fighting back. He staggered, and before he could even make a move, found that he was seriously injured by the profound sun immortal light. An instant later, he slammed into the ground below.

Xu Qing raced after him, clenching his hand into a fist that he slammed into Chen Fei’s chest, worsening his injuries.

All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint.

What was more, when Xu Qing unleashed his godly authority and cultivator authority, the jade slip the empress had given him surreptitiously worked behind the scenes to disguise the true nature of what he was doing. His authority of sound became blood sealing marks. His cultivator authority became a daoist magic. The sun of immortal light became a secret technique.

The fact that the fight ended so quickly caused the cultivators who had been watching the fight to feel shaken to the core. All of them were struck speechless.

Thinking back to what the empress had asked of him, Xu Qing hovered in the air looking down at Chen Fei.

“You... are too weak.” Then he launched a kick that sent Chen Fei flying back to the Imperial Sovereign mountain. “Are there any other Smoldering Gods in this mountain who want to fight?”

Chen Fei wanted to speak up. He had other assets at his disposal, and was convinced that his defeat was the result of some minor slip-up. However, his injuries from his fall were so severe that when he opened his mouth to speak, blood sprayed out.

At the same time, a grim voice spoke from the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. “I’d hoped to avoid looking like a bully. But since you asked for this, Sir Blood Dust... I suppose I have no choice other than to crush you.”

An aura far more terrifying than Chen Fei’s erupted from the mountain, accompanied by an old man. He had scarlet hair, and pulsed with a nine-world aura. That aura came from the worlds that floated behind him. It was an energy that made this old man feel very much like an actual god.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered slightly. He actually wasn’t confident at all in his ability to defeat a nine-world Smoldering God. Looking at the cultivator, he shook his head.

“You’re not a match for me either. But since you’re the one who brought up bullying, I’ll just stand here and let you unleash three moves on me. If you can hurt me, then you win.”

Xu Qing landed on the ground, clasped his hands behind his back, and looked at the old man.

1. Presumably most readers of wuxia and xianxia know this, but just in case there are some out there who don’t, whenever you hear something like “swap pointers” or “exchange advice” or something like that in a context like this, it’s usually referring to going out and challenging people to fight. Because the two parties are “swapping pointers,” it’s obviously not supposed to be a duel to the death, but rather, a quasi-friendly match, almost like sparring, to see who is stronger or better. Of course, it could be that the person issuing such challenges has ulterior motives and will push things beyond the level of a friendly match. But the presupposition is that it’s not a death duel. ☜

2. Chen Fei: Minor spoilers, but probably no surprise, that this character isn’t really important. However, what is interesting is that he bears the exact same name as a minor character from A Will Eternal, someone who first appeared in chapter 12 of that novel. No, they’re not supposed to be the same character. Just the same name. What’s more, the characters are the same exact characters as the first two from the character Chen Feiyuan of this novel. ☜

Deathblade's Thoughts

This chapter was 1,000 characters longer than normal.

There wasn’t much Xu Qing could do. Normally speaking, he wasn’t the type of person who would act in this manner. But right now... he was acting on orders from the empress. The empress had hinted to him that he should make a big scene, and considering how much shē had helped him, he couldn’t refuse. Therefore, all he could do was do his best to act and speak in the way his Eldest Brother would. That was what led to his words from earlier, as well as his current prideful attitude.

All onlookers couldn’t help but think of him as being lofty and unyielding. It could even be considered arrogant!

He stood at the foot of the Imperial Sovereign mountain, his hands clasped behind his back, looking completely and utterly domineering. This was all despite being up against an almighty nine-world Smoldering God expert.

An instant later, the cultivators in the mountain angrily flew up into the air and stared down at him.

Given the pressure weighing down on him, Xu Qing kept his guard up in every respect. However, he didn’t reveal that on his face. In fact, he actually closed his eyes.

The nine-world Smoldering God barked an angry laugh. “Excellent. Excellent!”

Xu Qing’s dramatic words and behavior caused the old man’s eyes to glitter coldly. It wasn’t that he had never encountered brash people like this in his life. He had. And all of them had ended up as corpses.

Seeing that Xu Qing had gone so far as to close his eyes, the nine-world Smoldering God lifted his right hand, then dropped it. Instantly, the dome of heaven changed colors, the lands rumbled, and a screaming wind kicked up. The moment his hand dropped, a huge hand appeared behind him, so large it filled the sky. And then it moved forward, passing through the man and... rumbling directly toward Xu Qing.

The palm strike contained the power of a nine-world Smoldering God, fully unleashed. It was a destructive power that could destroy the heavens and extinguish the earth, something that was capable of shattering natural and magical laws. Even the air shattered.

It headed right toward Xu Qing. The wild winds kicked up Xu Qing’s hair and robes, yet his closed eyes didn’t even flutter. As the palm descended, heaven and earth trembled.

Then, as everyone watched on intently, black fire erupted around Xu Qing, which rapidly spread out beneath his feet to form a black lotus. As it bloomed, countless flower petals of fire spread out, with Xu Qing being at the very center. That lotus of black fire created a perfect defensive barrier around him.

The massive palm hit it. Deafening rumbling sounds echoed out. The black lotus continued to burn, and its flower rotated gently, like a dance. Inside, Xu Qing’s hair didn’t even stir. However, his eyes finally opened.

“You get two more moves,” he said coolly. freewebnovel.com

Up above, the old man’s eyes hardened. All of the cultivators on the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain were visibly surprised. It wasn’t just any ordinary person that could withstand an attack from a nine-world Smoldering God. The only type of person who could was someone incredibly strong.

That was especially true considering... that some of the more knowledgeable among them realized that this black lotus was something familiar to them. It was something they had read about.

Before long, someone realized what it was, and they cried out, “That’s the Netherlotus technique! It’s a secret defensive magic used by Grand Emperor Netherflame of the eastern Devilbirds!”

As that voice reached the ears of everyone else, people began to think back to ancient records they had read, and the various stories they contained about Grand Emperor Netherflame.

“Sir Blood Dust actually knows that secret magic!”

“No wonder Imperial Sovereign Lu Lingzi brought him along!”

“And now it makes sense why Sir Blood Dust is acting so brazen!”

As the crowd reacted, Xu Qing stood in place, his eyes closed. Up in midair, the nine-world Smoldering God frowned. He had heard of the Netherlotus, and knew that it was a secret magic that provided astonishing levels of defense. Eyes narrowing, he suddenly threw both hands out and performed an incantation gesture. Instantly, nine major worlds appeared behind him, scintillating brilliantly as massive mountains rose up within them.

There were nine mountain peaks, all of them transforming from illusory to corporeal. Emerging from their respective worlds, they became like a string of beads that influenced the surrounding magical laws, and caused thunder and lightning to go wild. The old man pointed out with each of his index fingers, and the nine mountain peaks screamed toward Xu Qing.

However, before that second attack could land, the old man touched his forehead with his right hand, whereupon his nine major worlds rumbled again. From within, countless magical and natural laws emerged, all of which were daos the old man had gained enlightenment of in his life.

When they were in the open, he shouted, “Use daos to make the tip!”

The daos converged, transforming into the tip of an enormous spear!

The man continued speaking in a growl. “Use worlds to make the haft!”

The nine major worlds lined up in a row, and from a distance, they looked like the haft of a spear!

“Use burning magics to form the tassel!” he roared. Countless magical techniques erupted, creating a multicolored glow that surrounded the spear haft like a tassel.

Finally, the old man’s eyes glittered with killing intent as he shoved his hands out. The massive spear then shot through the air toward Xu Qing. The old man was planning to unleash his second daoist technique and his third divine ability at the same time. He was hoping to use that method to break through the legendary Netherlotus.

Countless spectators watched as the nine mountains slammed into Xu Qing. They looked enormous, but they shrank down as they neared him, ultimately turning into nine enormous swords that slammed into the lotus of netherflame. It was mountain-toppling force and sea-draining momentum.

Xu Qing shivered. At the same time, the Netherlotus flickered, and the flames danced. However, not even the nine mountain peaks turned into razor-sharp swords could do a thing to Xu Qing. The Netherlotus’ flames burst upward, and the nine mountain-swords went from being corporeal to illusory. Then they disappeared.

However, that was when the terrifying spear pierced through the air toward Xu Qing’s head. The tip of the spear glowed brightly, becoming an apex manifestation of explosive strength. Intense rumbling sounds became like an attack of its own.

In the face of this attack, Xu Qing couldn’t just stand in place. He fell back. As he did so, the terrifying spear advanced like a boulder crushing a drinking glass.

Xu Qing’s eyes widened, and he prepared to lift his hand to defend himself. Unfortunately, the spear was too fast. Before he could move his hand, it stabbed into his chest. The spear tip shoved him back farther.

30 meters. 300 meters. 1,500 meters. After each retreat came another retreat. The spear tip seemed unstoppable, and yet, it couldn’t actually penetrate Xu Qing’s fleshly body. After falling back a full 3,000 meters, the spear’s momentum died down, and Xu Qing came to a halt.

Then, the spear tip in his chest vibrated and emitted cracking sounds. After that, it started shattering. It started from the tip, spreading backward into the haft, until the entire spear... collapsed into pieces.

The power of the spear was that of a peak Smoldering God. However, it was not at the level of an Imperial Sovereign.

As the wind blew across the lands, Xu Qing said, “It’s over.”

Silence reigned.

The nine-world Smoldering God looked down at Xu Qing with a complicated expression. A moment passed, and then he shook his head, turned, and went back to the mountain.

Xu Qing advanced. Quickly crossing back 3,000 meters, he reached the foot of the Imperial Sovereign mountain. There, he stepped onto the staircase, where he sat down cross-legged and looked up the mountain.

Thinking back to how his Eldest Brother would usually act, he said, “I’m going to sit here for the next three days. If anyone under an Imperial Sovereign can break my defenses without using an Imperial Sovereign treasure, then I’ll admit defeat.”

No one on the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain said a thing. If a nine-world Smoldering God couldn’t break Xu Qing’s defenses, then the only thing other Smoldering Gods could feel was helplessness. Attacking him again would be pointless.

There was more than one nine-world Smoldering God on this mountain. But given what had just played out, it didn’t seem like ‘Sir Blood Dust’ could inflict dangerous injuries. But his defenses were just too extreme. If they could take a page from ‘Sir Blood Dust’s’ book, and just sit there waiting to be attacked, maybe they could come out on top. But ‘Sir Blood Dust’ was already doing that, which put them in a no-win situation. Anyone with a higher cultivation base than Sir Blood Dust would be forced to admit their inferiority, and nobody wanted to do that....

Considering the cultivation base disparity, it was obvious that Sir Blood Dust couldn’t break their defenses. That made sense. But they would have to rely on sneaky tricks to achieve victory... which would be the same thing as losing. The loss of face would be too severe.

Most importantly, this only seemed like a contest between cultivators. The reality was that it was a struggle between the Imperial Sovereigns of the eastern and western Devilbirds.

The Imperial Sovereign mountain remained silent.

Three days passed.

The western Devilbirds were really riled up by now.

Xu Qing opened his eyes and stood. Then, as all the cultivators on the mountain looked on, he left without a word for the sixteenth Imperial Sovereign mountain.

When he arrived at the sixteenth mountain, the cultivators there glared at him antagonistically. Xu Qing, meanwhile, just sat down on the staircase.

“You know how this is going to work. I’m going to sit here for the next three days. If anyone under an Imperial Sovereign can break my defenses without using an Imperial Sovereign treasure, then I’ll admit defeat.”

***

Three days later he shook his head and left. During that time, quite a few cultivators had attacked him. All of them met defeat. In the end, they chose to imitate the seventeenth mountain and just bite their tongue.

Xu Qing went to the fifteenth mountain, sat down, and made the same challenge. He continued in that manner, spending three days at each mountain. About half a month later, he reached the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. By that point, people throughout the western Devilbird lands had heard of Sir Blood Dust.

Everyone knew his name. He was the focus of all attention.

At the same time, news finally got back to the eastern Devilbirds. The cultivators there were very excited, and many of them crossed the border into western Devilbird lands to watch things play out.

***

In the lands of the eastern Devilbirds, in the Immortal Skills Hall, ‘Yue Dong’ sat cross-legged in a hall. The reek of blood was just barely detectable from outside. Before long, footsteps echoed out, and Yue Dong’s beautiful eyes focused on the outside.

A young man in a fancy robe appeared there, his face full of emotion. He held a severed head in his hands.

After reaching Yue Dong, he softly said, “Dong’er, this scuzzball dared to call your identity into question. I got rid of him for you. Don’t worry. With me around, nobody among the eastern Devilbirds will dare harm you.

“However... something unexpected happened. Do you remember that Sir Blood Dust? I guess it’s my fault that you failed to kill that son of a bitch. I interrupted just at the wrong time. Ai.

“Who could have guessed that the little bitch would actually stumble into a destined opportunity! He became an attendant of the tenth Imperial Sovereign! And he went to the western Devilbird lands, where the beeotch is actually making a name for himself! Argh! But, don’t worry. I’ll definitely help you kill the bitchy son of a bitch!”

The young man seemed very sincere.

As for Yue Dong, she blinked a few times in surprise. She had already received help to seize power in the Immortal Skills Hall, and thus, had started studying the important immortal skills. As a result, she was completely ignorant of events among the western Devilbirds. Upon hearing the news, Yue Dong’s heart started pounding.

Little Ah Qing actually started rolling with the empress? And he’s gotten famous already?

Upon thinking about his little Junior Brother eclipsing him, Erniu took a deep breath. All of a sudden he felt a lot of pressure, and at the same time, quite a bit of humiliation.

Hold on, you’re hogging things already? I can’t believe the two of them teamed up and left me behind!

Xu Qing had no way of knowing how forlorn Erniu felt. For the past half a month, he had been dutifully carrying out the empress’ orders. He had challenged all of the Smoldering Gods among the western Devilbirds. Of course, his challenges didn’t involve fighting them. They involved defending against them.

As that half of a month went by, word spread far and wide about Sir Blood Dust being able to use the Netherlotus secret magic of Grand Emperor Netherflame. As a result, Sir Blood Dust became well and truly famous in the Devilbird holy land.

Some people were a bit suspicious about how he acquired Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secret magic. But then they considered that he was Lu Lingzi’s attendant, and the only person Lu Lingzi had brought to the western Devilbirds. Given that, it seemed obvious that the secret magic must have been given to him by Lu Lingzi.

Xu Qing continued with his challenges. He went from the ninth Imperial Sovereign mountain to the eighth. Then he proceeded toward the seventh.

There were a lot of cultivators gathered by the seventh mountain, most of them western Devilbirds, although there was also a contingent from the east. When Xu Qing arrived, it caused quite a commotion. Some people denounced him, others welcomed him joyously. Either way, there was quite a buzz. Of course, that made quite a contrast to the mountain itself, which was dead silent.

Everyone watched as Xu Qing approached the mountain itself. He said the same thing as before, then sat down cross-legged at the bottom of the staircase, his defenses active as he waited for someone to meet his challenge. This time, things went differently than from before.

Given all the public discussion about the matter, there were some Smoldering Gods who, whether of their own volition or because they were following veiled suggestions, finally chose to break the rules and do something. The time had come to end this outright humiliation of the western Devilbirds.

Almost exactly as Xu Qing sat down, a cold snort echoed out from the seventh Imperial Sovereign mountain.

“Enough of your arrogance, Sir Blood Dust!”

A figure appeared, shooting from the top of the mountain down toward Xu Qing. He looked like a young man, and he had seven major worlds glittering radiantly around him. They created a mountain-toppling, sea-draining pressure that could crush anything in its path, and it was weighing down right on Xu Qing.

The young man didn’t hesitate for a moment. Eyes glittering coldly, he lifted his right hand and pushed it toward Xu Qing. A huge palm formed in front of him, filling the sky. It also descended toward Xu Qing. Although this was a Smoldering God palm attack, it was actually very different from the palm attack that the other Smoldering God cultivator had used on Xu Qing some time back. It was much more clearly visible, with obvious palm prints on it. There wasn’t anything about it that could be said to be blurry. And most importantly, it had natural and magical laws that were exponentially more terrifying than any Xu Qing had encountered.

Most astonishing... was that it contained fluctuations of authority! They were gruish fluctuations, and though they were clearly coming from the seven-world young man, if you looked closely, you would realize that the true origin was the palm. Astonishingly, visible on the palm was a diaphanous glove.

It was... an Imperial Sovereign treasure! What was more, it pulsed with power that surpassed that of an Imperial Sovereign!

A Smoldering God would obviously have to pay a high price to get such a treasure. Yet right now, the seven-world young man’s eyes shone with determination as he seemingly threw caution to the wind and unleashed all of the power of his cultivation base to activate the glove.

The illusory palm erupted with a terrifying aura, crushing everything around it as it bore down on Xu Qing. He slowly opened his eyes and looked at the incoming palm. Inside of him, The Emperor’s Sword vibrated. With a thought, he could send it out to slash the palm apart.

But he didn’t do that. He had been prepared all along for something like this to happen. He had actually planned for the enemy to break the rules of the challenge at some point. There was no need for him to do a thing. He would be able to handle anyone under an Imperial Sovereign. Besides, Xu Qing was convinced... that the empress actually wanted someone to attack him with Imperial Sovereign power. The challenges he had been making were really just the introduction to the main event.

The empress had come to the western Devilbirds to see Grand Emperor Devilbird. However, the Grand Emperor was taking his time agreeing to the meeting, and obviously, was using the opportunity to probe for information.

Maybe the Grand Emperor would make the empress wait for a day. Maybe a month. Maybe indefinitely. That was why the empress hadn’t chosen to accept challenges from other Imperial Sovereigns, but rather, gave the responsibility to Xu Qing. That was because... the empress didn’t like being in a passive position. Shē liked having the initiative. How to make a move. When to make a move. The methods and rationale behind making a move. Shē liked to be in control of such things. All of this was for the purpose of getting Grand Emperor Devilbird to issue orders for a meeting.

Xu Qing could pick up on all of these clues. And the western Devilbirds weren’t fools, so they likely could reach the same conclusion as him. Therefore, after this cultivator appeared with an Imperial Sovereign treasure, it wasn’t necessarily possible to tell immediately whether he had ill intentions or not. There was the distinct possibility... that an Imperial Sovereign was actually behind this. Perhaps that Imperial Sovereign was actually helping the empress, by providing a reason for hēr to take the initiative.

When the hand with the Imperial Sovereign glove was only about 300 meters away from Xu Qing, the palm shivered and lurched to a halt in midair. Then, just as Xu Qing had predicted would happen, Lu Lingzi appeared right beneath that palm. With a slight wave of his hand, he completely dispelled the power of the attack.

Everything went silent. Xu Qing stood and bowed to Lu Lingzi. The seven-world young man was inwardly relieved, and quickly inclined his head and bowed.

The gaze of Lu Lingzi looked at the Imperial Sovereign mountain ahead, and though he didn’t say anything, a great pressure began to build up in the area.

All of a sudden, a majestic figure materialized atop the mountain. It was an old woman with cold eyes that were currently fixed on Lu Lingzi. The ground trembled.

Two types of Imperial Sovereign power pulsed from those auras and gazes. And when they clashed, the air shattered, causing rifts to open up everywhere, and sending screaming winds out into a huge vortex. Innumerable bits of rubble floated up into the air, and the Imperial Sovereign mountain rocked back and forth.

The confrontation immediately attracted the attention of the other Imperial Sovereigns in the west. Numerous streams of divine will surged into the area, further increasing the space-time chaos. Threads of natural and magical laws appeared and shattered constantly. A stifling sensation weighed down on all of the cultivators present, who were shaken to the core.

Then, the empress spoke with Lu Lingzi’s voice. “Sir Blood Dust, produce the command medallion I gave you.”

Xu Qing immediately complied and held the medallion overhead. The empress waved a hand, causing the medallion to release a bit of Imperial Sovereign aura. Everyone could immediately sense that the medallion contained the might of an Imperial Sovereign.

“Did you ever use that medallion when exchanging pointers with the western Devilbirds?” shē asked.

Xu Qing didn’t hesitate to respond, “Never.”

“Did you kill anyone when exchanging pointers?” shē continued.

Xu Qing shook his head. “I just tried to quickly determine who would achieve victory and who would be defeated. I never put anyone in danger.”

The empress’ gaze shifted to the seventh Imperial Sovereign mountain. Sounding very cold, shē said, “This competition between western and eastern Devilbirds was merely an exchange of pointers between members of the same species. Just as our ancient teachings assert, there must be fairness and balance in all things.

“Sir Blood Dust had an Imperial Sovereign treasure, but never used it. Exchanging pointers is about determining victory or defeat. It’s not about a duel to the death. With the exception of the first fight, Sir Blood Dust never even made a move on anyone.

“However, the western Devilbirds secretly prepared an Imperial Sovereign treasure to use. Had I not personally interfered, it’s entirely likely Sir Blood Dust would have lost his life. What’s the meaning of this? Why did you possibly treat a fellow member of your species in such a ruthless way?”

The streams of divine will from the other Imperial Sovereigns seemed to go still. Lu Lingzi’s words had really caused the atmosphere to become tense. That was when a calm voice drifted down.

“Come to my dao altar to see me, Lu Lingzi.”

The chaos in space-time was quelled. The collapsing natural and magical laws went back to normal. The tense atmosphere faded away. All of the Imperial Sovereigns revealed themselves as shadowy projections and quickly bowed to the wing-shaped dao altar off in the distance.

The words that had just been spoken came from Grand Emperor Devilbird.

The empress looked up with a very calm expression, then took a step forward. Shē had achieved hēr objective.

The Imperial Sovereigns all exchanged glances, then dissipated. The old woman who had come out from the seventh Imperial Sovereign mountain also disappeared. The only person left behind was the young man who had attacked Xu Qing. He clasped hands, bowed to Xu Qing, then turned and left.

Xu Qing remained behind at the foot of the mountain. He had done his job and didn’t need to make any more challenges.

So now what...?

A thought occurred to him.

I’m here in the lands of the western Devilbirds, and have the empress backing me up. I caused a bit of a stir just now. Given how things have played out, I suppose... there’s a certain location I ought to explore.

He hadn’t forgotten the information his Eldest Brother had given him about the two Immortal Skills Halls in the Devilbird holy land.

Five Dogs Six Thieves....

He had already mastered Six Thieves Deceive Life, which came from the eastern Devilbirds. As for Five Dogs Cleave Immortals, it came from the western Devilbirds. Normally speaking, studying it in detail would be extremely difficult. But now....

Given how famous the empress has become, and considering the reputation I’ve built in the last half month, I might as well go take a look!

After making some plans to ensure that he didn’t slip up and reveal his true identity, he flew up into the air. As the numerous cultivators in the area looked on, he flew off into the distance.

He was heading... in the direction of the western Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall! It wasn’t very far from the seventh Imperial Sovereign mountain, and was located in a lake called Immortal Cleaving. The lake was pitch black, while the Immortal Skills Hall was crafted from pure white stone. It was exquisitely constructed, and cast flowing light in all directions. The contrast it created with the lake made for a very gruish sense of peace.

At the moment, there were a few hundred cultivators seated on the surface of the lake. They included men and women, old and young. All of them wore white clothing and had their eyes closed as they practiced cultivation. The fluctuations of an immortal skill were very prominent.

When Xu Qing arrived, he realized immediately that these people were the immortal adepts of the western Devilbirds!

His arrival did not attract any notice. After looking around, he focused on the pure white Immortal Skills Hall in the middle of the lake. Clasping hands, he bowed.

“I am Sir Blood Dust,” he said, “here representing an Imperial Sovereign to take a look at Five Dogs Cleave Immortals!”

Atop the black lake were the white-robed immortal adepts, seated cross-legged as they pursued enlightenment. None moved, and none reacted at all to Xu Qing’s arrival. The white Immortal Skills Hall was just as still and silent.

Xu Qing hefted his Imperial Sovereign command medallion as he hovered in midair for about three breaths of time. Then, his face completely calm, he said, “Before being summoned to meet Grand Emperor Devilbird, my Imperial Sovereign emphasized to me that, since he sadly couldn’t come in person, I should represent him to visit the Immortal Skills Hall. My task is to commit to memory everything that I can study, so that I can explain the details to him later.

“If the Immortal Skills Hall doesn’t mind, then I, Sir Blood Dust, will seek enlightenment on my own. As for the Imperial Sovereign, he will come back at a later date.”

Having said that, Xu Qing kept his gaze fixed on the Immortal Skills Hall. He knew that he couldn’t just casually barge into a place like this. If calling on the name of Lu Lingzi didn’t get him inside, then he would have to think of some other strategy to gain entrance. After all, him coming here was a clear case of taking action when borrowing a tiger’s skin.

What was more, Lu Lingzi had made his reasons for coming very clear at the seventh Imperial Sovereign mountain. It was that event, plus the fact that Lu Lingzi had seized the initiative, which resulted in him being summoned by the Grand Emperor. As a result, all of the top experts among the western Devilbirds had a fairly good understanding of this new Imperial Sovereign.

Therefore, it was no surprise that, after a long moment passed... the main entrance of the Immortal Skills Hall slowly opened. A young man and woman walked out, both of them clad in long, white robes. In the lead was the man, who was quite handsome. He was followed by the woman, who was very beautiful. The moment they appeared, the immortal adepts all opened their eyes and bowed their heads respectfully.

Xu Qing looked at them.

The young man looked up at Xu Qing.

“Normally speaking, no one may seek enlightenment of immortal skills other than immortal adepts. But since you’re here on the orders of an Imperial Sovereign, we will give you a special, one-time authorization. That said, anyone who seeks to learn immortal skills must first experience five deadly tribulations. You might live through them, or you might die.

“Pick a spot anywhere on Immortal Cleaving Lake, sink down beneath the water, and wait for the five tribulations. That will be your chance to study the immortal skill.”

The young man stopped speaking and stared coldly at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he looked down at Immortal Cleaving Lake.

“What’s wrong,” the young man asked coolly. “Scared?”

Xu Qing studied his surroundings. Then, a moment later, he shot down to the lake, settled onto the surface, then sank beneath the water.

When he was gone, the surrounding immortal adepts exchanged glances. Some of them shook their heads. Some of them sneered.

“This Sir Blood Dust must be feeling suicidal.” freewebnovel.com

“It’s impossible to say how many people have been buried at the bottom of the lake after failing to pass the five tribulations. Even if he somehow manages to stay alive, he won’t succeed at the task.”

With that, everyone looked away and paid no further heed to what was happening. Although Sir Blood Dust had become very famous lately, the people here were more concerned with gaining enlightenment of their immortal skill.
