As for the young man who had come out of the Immortal Skills Hall, he continued to sneer. In contrast, the young woman seemed apprehensive.

“Elder Brother, our Master went wandering and hasn’t returned. And that new Imperial Sovereign from the eastern Devilbirds has really taken the spotlight lately. What’s more, this Sir Blood Dust is an extraordinary individual who made a name for himself in the last half a month. Someone like that, with a background like he has, should really just be allowed to study our immortal skill. Is there really a need to make him go through such a dangerous trial? [1]

“Immortal Cleaving Lake contains the Five Dogs Heavenly World. People who go in there rarely come out alive, and even if they do, they don’t ever succeed at gaining enlightenment. After all... gaining enlightenment of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals requires a special ceremony.” She sighed.

The young man’s eyes were just as cold as before. “I warned him of the danger. Everyone here bore witness. He went in despite knowing all that. I didn’t force him. If he wants to court death, it has nothing to do with me.”

With that, he flicked his sleeve and walked back into the Immortal Skills Hall.

The young woman looked at the surface of the lake and shook her head. She knew that it was pointless to say anything further, and thus, she simply went back to the Immortal Skills Hall.

Meanwhile, Xu Qing was under the surface of Immortal Cleaving Lake. So far, he hadn’t noticed anything unusual. The water was pitch black, but it didn’t contain mutagen. Instead, there was something lively about it. However, it restricted divine will, making it impossible for someone to use divine will to see the whole lake at one time.

After taking a moment to check his surroundings, Xu Qing sent his divine will out to search the area. After enough time passed for an incense stick to burn, his gaze hardened.

By means of divine will, he had noticed that there were a host of corpses on the bottom of the lake.... The more he looked around, the more corpses he saw. In the end, he came to the conclusion that there were several thousand of them. They included the bodies of men and women, old and young. All had their eyes open, and those eyes were pure white. So was their skin and hair. As for the looks on their faces, they were gruish expressions that were strange mixtures of crying and laughter.

What was more, Xu Qing realized that there was a huge magical symbol on the bottom of the lake. It was white, and it took up more than half of the lake. It pulsed with an ancient sensation, and what was most strange of all was the fact that... the corpses were part of it.

Xu Qing looked at it for a while. Then he approached cautiously. As he got close, he examined it with divine will, taking in the entire thing a few times over. He did not gain any enlightenment from doing so. After about ten breaths of time passed, his eyes shone with determination.

Continuing to get even closer, he ultimately stepped onto the symbol. When he did, he shivered mentally. Feeling like he was sinking, he watched as his vision blurred. When it cleared again, he wasn’t on the lake floor.

He was in the sky! It was blue and full of fluffy white clouds. Down beneath him, there was no land. Instead, there was a 300-meter wide white thread that snaked off into the distance. It looked almost like a white hair that was countless times larger than normal.

Xu Qing didn’t blindly take action. Instead, he sent his divine will out to examine the white thread. It didn’t take much observation for him to realize that the white thread was actually made up of magical symbols. Each of them looked exactly alike. It was the very same magical symbol from the bottom of the lake.

This has to relate to the ‘five tribulations’ that the young man was talking about. He obviously didn’t have good intentions. However... I’m here, so I shouldn’t let some malicious intentions get in my way.

He didn’t immediately start walking along the white thread. Instead, he looked at it, all while the authority of Six Thieves Deceive Life glittered in his eyes.

It is not possible to live eternally thanks to the six thieves that deceive life. The eyes deceive sight. The ears deceive hearing. The nose deceives smelling. The mouth deceives taste. The body deceives labor. The mind deceives thought. Thus, all is lost.

His dao lineament stirred as the Six Thieves immortal skill arose within him. Threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures spread out around him.

Six Thieves and Five Dogs. Together as one....

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he started walking along the white thread. Thanks to the Six Thieves authority, he could sense everything around him clearly. Meanwhile, the information his Eldest Brother had given him about Five Dogs Cleave Immortals swirled in his mind.

The five dogs are stinginess, greed, foolishness, depravity, and austerity.

The inability to abandon things. That is called stinginess. Having insatiable desire. That is called greed. Renouncing the rules of life. That is called foolishness. Arguing without understanding the facts. That is called depravity. Renouncing the three paths of hell before attaining lifelessness. That is called austerity.

As for the seven banes and eight evils, Yue Dong and her Junior Sister didn’t really understand them.

This particular immortal skill can be summed up in this way... the stingy dog cleaves to a place and loses treasure; the greedy dog cleaves to a place and is bound; the foolish dog cleaves to a place and falls into death; the depraved dog cleaves to a place and falls into hell; the austere dog cleaves to a place and forever loses the body.

He thought while sensing, while advancing. However, at a certain point, he stopped walking. The threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures around him were vibrating violently, almost as if to block his path. Except... there was nothing in front of him. A moment later, those threads went back to normal.

Keeping his guard up, he looked around. Yet no matter how he studied his surroundings, he couldn’t find anything out of the ordinary. After confirming that there was nothing blocking his path, he frowned and then kept moving. After taking only three steps, his expression darkened.

No. Six Thieves Deceive Life creates threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures. I can’t be experiencing this sensation for no reason. So what’s the problem here...?

His frown deepened, and he put more thought into the situation. However, nothing occurred to him. Unfortunately, the uneasy sensation wouldn’t go away. Instead of continuing on his way, he stayed put and thought back to everything he had done up to this point.

That was when he realized that the strange reaction from the threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures actually came when he thought about the information his Eldest Brother had given him.

He immediately thought back to those same things. A moment later, his gaze sharpened.

There’s something wrong with those memories of mine....

There was something strange about them, yet he couldn’t put his finger on exactly what it was. Therefore, it was without any hesitation that he opened the eye of Hellfei! That eye could penetrate illusory obstacles!

The moment he opened the eye, he realized what was going on. In his memories, Yue Dong had a Junior Sister. But the real Yue Dong didn’t have a Junior Sister![2]

Lan Yao wasn’t actually Yue Dong’s Junior Sister!

However, that Junior Sister obscured Xu Qing’s sensations, merging with them and becoming part of his memories. In fact, she even pierced all of the memory images he had of Yue Dong. When he thought back to meeting Feng Lintao, Lan Yao, and Yue Dong for the first time, his memories contained a clear image of a fourth person. Yue Dong’s Junior Sister. Later, when he and his Eldest Brother captured Yue Dong, they also took her Junior Sister captive. However, because of the soulsearch, Yue Dong’s Junior Sister ended up dying.

That memory caused Xu Qing’s pupils to constrict. He was sure that this memory was real. And yet, Hellfei’s eye was telling him something else. It was telling him that the memory came from somewhere else!

In that case, who exactly put a memory of Yue Dong’s Junior Sister into me?

His expression became even more grim as he realized that, even though Hellfei’s eye was telling him that the memory was false, he actually couldn’t get rid of it. Eyes flashing coldly, he activated the godly authority of fate within him.

It turned into a carving knife that could pierce fate. And with that knife, he slashed at the memory of Yue Dong’s Junior Sister. A loud crunching sound rang out. The image of the Junior Sister shattered.

And yet, Xu Qing’s heart only continued to sink. And that was because, the moment the image of Yue Dong’s Junior Sister shattered, that memory became a withered white hair that connected to half of his other memories. It seemed to just spread through countless other memories. It was a very gruish sight and sensation.

It was like looking at a completed painting, only to look closer and find that a bunch of white hairs had been dropped into it. That was when one of the descriptions of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals echoed in his mind.

The inability to abandon things. That is called stinginess... the stingy dog cleaves to a place and loses treasure.

These white hairs were like a door being opened in a sealed secret chamber.

The door was circular. When it opened, white light spilled out. It was like a white eyeball.

The stingy dog... cleaves to a place!

1. The ‘wandering’ being done by the Master isn’t just random wandering. The specific word in Chinese is the word used to describe the type of wandering that monks would do for religious purposes. ☜

2. Erniu originally described the Five Dogs skill in chapter 1033. In that chapter, the wording is slightly different, and there is no mention of the Junior Sister. ☜

Living beings can be viewed as a collective, but can also be viewed as individuals. The same can be said of both mortals and cultivators.

Take, for example, mortals. Mortals had souls in their bodies, as well as physical meridians that formed a self-contained network designed to keep out harmful outside influences. That, in turn, helped to prevent illnesses and other mortal dangers.

Cultivators were similar. They had bodies bolstered by spirit energy, and the cycles and operations of their bodies were governed by various natural rules. Depending on the cultivation base and life level of a cultivator, their cycles and operations would reach increasing levels of perfection. After reaching a certain point, it would be virtually impossible for another person to find weaknesses to exploit, and the cultivator’s defenses would be able to resist all outside forces. The only way to kill a cultivator like that was to be far stronger than them, and wipe them out quickly and decisively. But a cultivator with a similar cultivation base would need some special method to defeat them.

That was one of the reasons why immortal skills had been created to begin with. Generally speaking, immortal skills were designed to be gruish and extraordinary. They were supposed to be used to get past an opponent’s defenses with the goal of killing them decisively.

Meanwhile, human nature was complicated and incorporeal. And that meant that it was one of the main targets that many immortal skills would hone in on as a weakness.

That was the case with Six Thieves Deceive Life. It contained the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures expressed as forms of will. That will would form an attractant that could reverse cyclical patterns, penetrate defenses, and allow for killing blows. As for Five Dogs Cleave Immortals, it actually emphasized the will of temperament.

The word cleave could be used in the sense of ‘cleaving to’ a place. For instance, the soul would cleave to the body that it inhabited. That was why this technique was most commonly thought to be a possession magic.

However, there was another meaning to it. After all, it was also possible to cleave from something. And that meaning was the opposite of possession: letting go.[1]

Unfortunately, most people couldn’t let go of things easily. That was the origin of the saying used to describe the immortal skill.

The concept of cleaving from external things was what made it possible to bypass the defenses of an opponent. When that loophole was present, the immortal skill could be used.

As for the memories of Yue Dong’s Junior Sister, that was the extraordinary aspect of this immortal skill. Using that aspect, it was possible to conceal something that wouldn’t easily be detected. The point was to deceive the subject. And when that thought wasn’t detected, it would have time to grow and mature. It was like opening the door of a room that had previously been locked. It involved five breaths of time, and that was the true meaning of ‘the stingy dog cleaves to a place.’

Overall, the immortal skill relied on that gruishness to unleash the will of the Five Dogs to surpass the traditional extraordinary ability and turn it into something very deadly. Of course, when talking about ‘opening the door’ it referred to maliciously invading the enemy.

As for the white eye, it was a manifestation of the greedy will of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

Having insatiable desire. That is called greed. The greedy dog cleaves to a place and is bound.

A will of greed could restrict the heart and mind. It could bind the body.

The door opened and the white eye appeared. It looked at Xu Qing. At that moment, Xu Qing’s mind reeled, and he became vaguely aware that four breaths of time were about to pass. A gruish sealing symbol appeared, starting on the inside and moving outside. The white eye was sealing Xu Qing in place. During those four breaths of time, the sealing mark formed. And if it could not be broken during that time....

Renouncing the rules of life. That is called foolishness. The foolish dog cleaves to a place and falls into death.

A white vortex appeared in the middle of Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness, without any sound accompanying it. It appeared beneath the white eye, and as it spun, it exerted a force of separation. What was being separated were his fleshly body and soul. After the third breath of time passed, a white mouth appeared in the place of the vortex, which opened wide with boundless evil.

This was....

Arguing without understanding the facts. That is called depravity. The depraved dog cleaves to a place and falls into hell.

The white mouth viciously took a bite. It took a bite of his soul! Finally, something appeared around the eye, the vortex, and the mouth. It was the fifth will of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals. It was a white face.

Because of the contrast it provided, the immortal skill of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals was completed in Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness. It became... a complete face. It had white hair, and a facial expression... that was smiling, yet not smiling. Crying, yet not crying. It was gruish to the extreme. It began to fuse with Xu Qing’s fleshly body.

Renouncing the three paths of hell before attaining lifelessness. That is called austerity. The austere dog cleaves to a place and forever loses the body.

Xu Qing’s view of the world began to dim. Outside, at the bottom of Immortal Cleaving Lake, a new corpse appeared on the huge white magical symbol made of corpses.

It was none other than Xu Qing. His hair was white, as was his skin. His eyes were also opened, and they glowed with white light. He was now one with the other surrounding corpses. His facial expression resembled theirs as well.

But a moment later, something dramatic happened. Outside of Xu Qing there appeared a host of threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures. The threads pulsed with the immortal skill fluctuations of Six Thieves Deceive Life. Xu Qing had prepared them in advance, and they had now been stimulated to congregate around him.

When they arrived, some of them pierced into Xu Qing’s fleshly body, while others went toward the white face. Yet others circled around him, moving round and round until they formed something like a cocoon around him. The cocoon was itself a sealing mark.

As for the white face inside Xu Qing, it was now incapable of emerging into the open.

This was Xu Qing’s plan. He wanted to personally experience Five Dogs Cleave Immortals. And though it was astoundingly gruish, he was now feeling fairly confident. And the reason for that confidence was Six Thieves Deceive Life. After all, Five Dogs Cleave Immortals and Six Thieves Deceive Life were fundamentally part of the same immortal skill.

In that manner, time passed.

***

Everything at the bottom of Immortal Cleaving Lake was still. Then, all of a sudden, the lake water seemed to stop moving. Two hours passed. That was when cracking sounds came out of the cocoon. They started out faint. But soon they became louder and more frequent. At the same time, the cocoon started to split open. The effects continued until the cocoon exploded.

Xu Qing was revealed. His hair was no longer white. It was back to its usual color. It was the same with his eyes, although they did contain traces of lingering fear.

“This is Five Dogs Cleave Immortals,” he murmured.

This skill is far more gruish than Six Thieves Deceive Life.... Wait, no. That’s just because Yue Dong is fundamentally weak, which allowed me to vanquish her version of Six Thieves Deceive Life. The origin of the immortal skill is this sealing mark....

Xu Qing looked down at the white sealing mark beneath his feet. He could sense that the sealing mark was extremely ancient. In fact, if his speculations were correct, it probably came from the time of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity. In fact, there was even the possibility that this seal was the original sealing mark of the immortal skill of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

If I hadn’t gained control of Six Thieves Deceive Life first, and turned it into a dao lineament of authority completely belonging to me, then it would have been difficult to awaken just now.

He looked at all the corpses around him. Now he realized that these were the bodies of people who had failed to gain enlightenment.

This immortal skill....

Xu Qing shifted his attention to his own right hand. The scattered remnants of the cocoon threads were gathering there, where they were forming into a faint symbol. The symbol actually looked exactly like the white symbol at the bottom of Immortal Cleaving Lake. And as he watched, the symbol turned into something that resembled a mask.

By means of Six Thieves Deceive Life, he would later be able to extract the mask and use the ultimate origin of the immortal skill to force it to work for him.

Xu Qing sent his divine will into the mask and experienced the same thing he had just experienced with Five Dogs Cleave Immortals. Ultimately he was able to break through the inner qualities of the immortal skill.

The stingy dog preserves a memory within the memories of the person using it. Because of how deeply it’s hidden, it’s hard to pick up on any clues about what it really is. If five breaths of time pass, and the user hasn’t erased it, the greedy dog will appear.

The greedy dog is a sealing mark that prevents the user from escaping. The sealing mark takes four breaths of time to form. If it isn’t erased before then, the sealing is complete, and the foolish dog appears.

The power of the foolish dog is the vortex. It serves to separate the soul and body of the user, find a weakness, and then magnify it. If it isn’t wiped out within three breaths of time, the depraved dog arrives.

The depraved dog devours the soul, and if it isn’t destroyed within two breaths of time, the austere dog appears.

The austere dog merges with the body, and if it isn’t killed within one breath of time, then... the immortal skill of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals is a success.

If the immortal skill is complete, it unleashes astonishing killing power. To some extent, it uses one’s own body to kill one’s own self! That’s why there is no differentiation between strong and weak. The technique is extremely harmful to the soul. However, there’s still something I don’t understand... freewebnovel.com

Cleaving immortals. Cleaving immortals. Which is the true meaning?

Is it cleaving from the immortal? Casting it aside? Or does it mean cleaving to the immortal?

Xu Qing got the feeling that the two words ‘immortal’ and ‘cleaving’ were key to accessing another, more important level of the immortal skill. Because he hadn’t fully mastered the immortal skill, he had no way to gain full enlightenment.

Xu Qing felt a bit of regret. However, he also knew that the immortal skill was amazing. Although it wasn’t possible to completely master it in a short time, he did have the right foundation. And it was all because of the synergy with the Six Thieves immortal skill.

It’s the foundation that brings the qualifications. As long as I’m qualified, then I have the chance to completely master it.

Xu Qing suppressed his regret, looked up, and shot toward the surface of the lake. After he was gone, the sealing mark at the bottom of the lake faded. It was no longer complete.

***

Outside in the Immortal Skills Hall, there was a secret chamber that was a restricted area. Inside of it was a black stone, upon which was an ancient symbol that looked exactly like the one at the bottom of the lake. That was the true Immortal Cleaving symbol.

Even that symbol was now dimmer, as though part of it had been taken away. Unfortunately, the grand immortal adept of the western Devilbirds was wandering now, and until he returned, it wouldn’t be possible for anyone to discover what had happened.

***

The immortal adepts of Immortal Cleaving Lake were still seated cross-legged seeking enlightenment. It had only been about four hours since Xu Qing sank down into the lake. Because of that, not many of the immortal adepts noticed when Xu Qing emerged from the surface of the lake. Those who did notice were dumbstruck. However, after recovering from their initial shock, their conclusion was that he must not have actually attempted to seek enlightenment. They assumed he had come up to the surface out of fear, and thus, they scorned him.

Xu Qing ignored all of that. Looking at the Immortal Skills Hall, he considered the lessons his Master had taught him. It was important for a person to show gratitude. Therefore, he clasped hands to the Immortal Skills Hall and bowed. That way, he could be free from debt from the subject, and would feel comfortable fighting and killing them later if necessary.[2]

With that, he turned and left.

The young man in the Immortal Skills Hall saw what happened and sneered.

He showed up acting all high and mighty, but when he left, he bowed. Switching from arrogance to deference like that is something I’ve seen a lot of. There’s always somebody who thinks they’re some sort of chosen. Omnipotent. But after experiencing the torment of our immortal skill, they turn chicken. This Sir Blood Dust is a real coward. He was obviously scared away. Well, good riddance!

1. This is the wordplay I mentioned several chapters ago when this immortal skill was introduced. In Chinese, the character I’m rendering as ‘cleave’ has multiple meanings. I’m using ‘cleave’ because I can basically impart the same concept as in Chinese while using an English word that has two opposite meanings depending on the context. For those of you who aren’t very familiar with the word ‘cleave,’ it works as I’ve described it in the translation. To ‘cleave to’ something means to stick close to it, while to ‘cleave from’ or cleave one thing ‘away from’ another means to separate from it. Incidentally, one of the characters used in the technique name is also used in the word commonly used in xianxia for “possession.” Sadly, I could not come up with one word in English that has all three meanings. ☜

2. Xu Qing is referring to what Master Seventh taught him in chapter 304. Search for “clean conscience” on that page, and you’ll get to the exact passage. This lesson was mentioned a few times in subsequent chapters. ☜

As Xu Qing emerged from Immortal Cleaving Lake, powerful fluctuations rolled out from the border of western Devilbird territory, where the wartime teleportation portals had been set up. There were quite a few portals there, and they had been set up in a specific way to lead to various parts of the Revered Ancient mainland. During this wartime period, they were like the front door of the Devilbird holy land. Because of that, this area was normally kept under tight guard by certain organizations from the western Devilbirds.

At the moment, a group of over a hundred cultivators from the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain were respectfully waiting at the seventeenth teleportation portal.

In the lead position was a young boy clad in a daoist robe. Remaining completely silent, he stood there looking at the seventeenth portal and the fluctuations rolling out from it. Rumbling sounds echoed out as the aura of a teleportation grew stronger. Scintillating light shone everywhere as a burly figure took shape. Even as a mere outline, this figure pulsed with a fiendish and bloody aura that caused everyone present to shiver. The faint odor of blood and gore filled the area.

After a moment, the light faded away, and the figure became clear. Astonishingly, a young man stood there, clad in a pitch-black suit of battle armor. His face had two horrendous scars on it that formed the shape of a cross. The way the flesh was bunched up around the scars was appalling.

One might think the scars would make this young man seem simply ugly. But the reality was that there was something unique about his facial features that made him seem somber and desolate. It created quite a contrast with his bright red hair, and it also made it seem like he was the source of the reek of blood that filled the area. His armor bore the evidence of combat, making it clear that he was a veteran of many, many battles.

The moment he appeared, the people from the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, led by the boy, dropped to their knees to kowtow.

“Well met, Your Majesty!”

This new arrival was the third apprentice of the Imperial Sovereign from the seventeenth mountain. Though he was ranked third, that didn’t reflect how strong he was, nor did it indicate his potential. In reality, he wasn’t just the most famous individual from the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. He was actually famous among all the western Devilbirds. In fact, he was even famous in the lands of the eastern Devilbirds.

He was Sir Westdevil!

The reason for his fame was that, based on his natural aptitude, he had once received praise from Grand Emperor Devilbird.

When in Void Returning, he could fight low-level Smoldering Gods. After breaking through to Smoldering God, he seized authority, thus becoming the second Smoldering God in the past thousand years among the western Devilbirds who had authority.

His authority was unique and terrifying. It focused on annihilation!

Now that he was a seven-world Smoldering God, he could dominate anyone up to a nine-world Smoldering God, and if he went all out, he could unleash power similar to that of an Imperial Sovereign. During the war with humankind, the strength and slaughter he unleashed earned him incredible battle credit. In fact, on the official hit list issued by humankind, he was listed with two other chosen Devilbirds as the top targets after the Imperial Sovereigns.

He had been at the front lines this entire time, until he received secret communication from one of his fellow apprentices. He had returned immediately.

As the reek of gore spread, and his somber aura grew stronger, Sir Westdevil strode off the teleportation portal with a cold expression on his face. He stopped in front of the kowtowing disciples.

“Where is he?” Sir Westdevil asked coolly.

The gathered crowd all shivered inwardly. Being from the same mountain, they were all very familiar with his proclivity for slaughter. In fact, one could say it was almost like an addictive hobby for him.

Ruthlessness was second nature to him. He was one of the most famous chosen among all Devilbird chosen. Grand Emperor Devilbird had approved of him. He had an Imperial Sovereign as his Master. People like him could well be said to wield absolute power in their domain.

Everyone kept their heads bowed.

Even the boy in the lead, who was an attendant of the Grand Emperor, didn’t dare to act negligently. Sounding very respectful, he said, “That Sir Blood Dust went to Immortal Cleaving Lake, where he stayed for four hours before heading east. He’s currently resting at Mount Heaven’s East.”

Sir Westdevil nodded. Eyes flashing coldly, he took a step forward. An instant later, he was up in the sky. Locking onto a specific location, he waved his hand, causing masses of black clouds to cover him. Then he flew away at top speed.

Wherever he went, rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth. Wreathed in black clouds as he was, he seemed like a heaven-devil.

He had come back from the front lines for one reason.... Sir Blood Dust. He was aware that Sir Blood Dust had issued a challenge to his own mountain, and that no one had been able to rise to the challenge. Therefore, Sir Westdevil was determined to take Sir Blood Dust’s head off his shoulders and mount it on a stake where he had sat at the bottom of the seventeenth mountain.

Sir Westdevil was completely ambivalent about killing fellow members of his own species, or causing friction between east and west.

***

As Sir Westdevil shot through the dome of heaven toward Mount Heaven’s East, Xu Qing really was resting right there on the mountain.

He had completed all his goals in the lands of the western Devilbirds. The empress had already earned an audience with Grand Emperor Devilbird, therefore, he didn’t need to go around issuing any more challenges. He had also accomplished everything he wanted to accomplish at the Immortal Skills Hall.

What he needed to do now was just wait until the empress finished dealing with the Grand Emperor. Then he would just join the empress on the return trip to the eastern Devilbirds.

By the time we leave the western Devilbirds, it will almost be time to open Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities.

During this entire time, Xu Qing had been thinking a lot about what the empress was really up to. It obviously had something to do with Grand Emperor Netherflame. There were many details and secrets that Xu Qing couldn’t understand. He simply lacked too much information. Therefore, it didn’t make sense to spend too much time analyzing the situation.

However, there was one thing he hadn’t forgotten. Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities contained a destined opportunity that could significantly boost one’s cultivation base.

And there’s Yue Dong’s original plan.... Furthermore, I wonder how Eldest Brother has been making out. I’m sure he’s made significant gains at the eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall.

After thinking about such things for a time, he stowed such thoughts and focused on the items he most needed to learn more about.

First on the list was the Mask of Wishes. In recent days, when he had the chance, he had studied the mask a few times. He was still holding back from making a wish. However, his investigation had revealed a few pertinent details.

This wish item seems to be some sort of godly authority! In terms of personhood, it’s terrifyingly advanced. I can keep it as a trump card, but unless I have absolutely no choice at all, I won’t finish stating a wish. As for the white dust, I have a bit more than before, but it’s still not enough....

Next, Xu Qing moved on to his godly authority of fate.

There’s nothing indicating that this type of godly authority can only be used in one way. Quite the opposite. I can collect it with my soul, use it to bolster divine abilities, and even do other tests. As for its ability to carve fate, there is a backlash contained within it. Carving fate involves replacing the previous trajectory, so any obstacles that pop up are things I have to personally deal with.

Xu Qing lifted his right hand, causing the godly authority of fate to manifest as a carving knife. He studied it for a short time before putting it away and focusing instead on his back. There on his back was a totem tattoo of an extinguished red candle. As he studied the tattoo with his senses, his expression darkened.

Back in the World Origin Pocket Realm, he had not been able to exert any control over it. In fact, he wasn’t even sure what it was. Perhaps everything that happened was all the candle’s doing. After all, the candle was conscious to a certain extent. Or perhaps it had been drawn to Xu Qing because of his special fleshly body. Regardless, Xu Qing did not like the tattoo. And his senses were telling him that it contained potential calamity.

From the very beginning until now, it had remained in an extinguished state. But Xu Qing could sense that the candle was reaching the point of waking up. When he thought about the terrifying power of that candle’s flame, his eyes flashed.

Unless I can control you, I absolutely cannot allow you to awaken and ignite that flame.

Then the authority of erasure appeared in his eyes, spread to his back, and covered the candle wick. The authority of erasure caused the aura of awakening to weaken. However, it didn’t disappear. Therefore, Xu Qing called out to Little Shadow.

“Devour!” he ordered.

Little Shadow wasn’t keen on doing that, but also didn’t dare to defy orders. Bracing itself, it rushed forth with gaping maw to devour the aura of awakening. Because of Little Shadow’s unique properties, it actually succeeded to a certain extent. The aura weakened further.

Time passed. Evening fell.

As the afterglow of the setting sun faded on the horizon, Xu Qing used the authority of erasure several times over. He also had Little Shadow make more attempts to devour the candle. As a result, the aura of awakening was now almost impossible to detect.

It’s still there, but at least I can control it.

Xu Qing went on to place some more sealing marks on it. Considering he was still waiting on the empress, he decided to do further study of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

However, that was when a sudden sensation of dread skyrocketed within him. Eyes hardening, he shot backward at high speed. A rumbling like thunder shattered the evening glow. Everything started to ripple and distort.

Then a pitch-black spear appeared, something that could destroy worlds, and it was shooting down directly toward Xu Qing. The haft of the spear was long enough to fill heaven and earth, while the tip was like a terrifying mountain. It contained almost unstoppable force as it appeared right in front of him.

At that moment of crisis, Xu Qing shot backward at top speed.

Being this close to it, Xu Qing was shaken to find that the mightiness of this spear was almost on the same level as an Imperial Sovereign. Because of how quickly Xu Qing evaded the attack, the spear screamed past him and slammed into Mount Heaven’s East. That one spear shattered the entire mountain! Rubble exploded everywhere.

The spear then passed through the remnants of the mountain and buried itself in the ground. There it remained, stabbed deep into the earth, quivering from the leftover force of the blow.

For 5,000 kilometers in every direction, the land shattered, all while black flames erupted from the tip and up through the resulting cracks and crevices. The entire area became a sea of flames.

Within those flames could be heard howls of anguish coming from countless souls. Those souls belonged to human cultivators. They were obviously victims that had been slaughtered by the spear on the battlefield. Those souls weren’t allowed back into the cycle of reincarnation, but were instead bound to the spear to bolster its might.

It was now possible to see a devilish figure standing atop the haft of the spear, which stuck out diagonally from the ground. Red hair swirled around a pitch-black suit of ferocious-looking armor. Behind him was the illusory projection of a heaven-devil that filled half the sky and glared menacingly at Xu.

“So, you’re Sir Blood Dust?”

For 5,000 kilometers in every direction, the lands looked like a shattered mirror. Black fire rose up from the cracks and crevices, turning the entire area into a sea of flames.

As it burned, countless human souls shrieked in grief. They couldn’t break free, as they were bound in the sea of flames, which surrounded the long spear.

Mount Heaven’s East didn’t exist anymore. In the spot where it had once stood there was now a shocking spear plunged into the earth. Standing on the spear was a figure that resembled a devil looking down on the world, surrounded by swirling red hair. Within that figure were seven brilliant balls of fire.

He was none other than Sir Westdevil.

But what Xu Qing was focused on was the heaven-devil projection behind Sir Westdevil. It filled him with a sense of both vigilance and impending danger.

Though the heaven-devil was illusory, the burly figure in the scintillating pitch-black armor imparted a sense of immense pressure. His eyes were filled with callous coldness, as well as a fiendish light that could penetrate to the core of a person. His long hair swirled like fire in the middle of the night, and emanated a gruish glow. His fingers were long, with sharp nails that seemed like they could rip anything to shreds. His entire body was covered with complex magical symbols, which seemed to serve both as his source of power and as the carrier of some mysterious curse.

His arrival caused darkness to build around him, a wind to kick up, and lightning to crackle. It was a pure manifestation of might and power.

Authority... thought Xu Qing, his eyes glittering as he looked at the devilish projection. He could clearly sense the fluctuations of dao lineament authority. And he could tell that this was not an ordinary type of authority.

“My authority is called devil-spirit rot-crushing,” Sir Westdevil said coolly as he looked down at Xu Qing. “Frankly speaking, it doesn’t matter whether or not you admit to being Sir Blood Dust.

“I’m from the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, and I’m here to fight you. To avoid claims of bullying the weak, I’ll only attack with three divine abilities. If you perish, Lu Lingzi will have no grounds to complain. If you survive my three attacks, then consider it good fortune that I spare your life.”

With that, he pointed directly at Xu Qing. Instantly, the air in front of Xu Qing shattered as a spear appeared that was several feet thick and several dozen meters long. It immediately shot toward Xu Qing. Where it passed, natural and magical laws shattered, which showed how astonishingly powerful it was, and highlighted the authority it contained.

As it locked on to Xu Qing’s mind and heart, it pulsed with a horrifying aura that was very close to the strength of an Imperial Sovereign. It arrived in an instant.

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted. This Sir Westdevil was stronger than any of the other Smoldering Gods he had encountered. In fact, this was probably the strongest Smoldering God he had ever faced. Without any hesitation, he shot backward at top speed, all while keeping his eyes fixed on the spear.

Unfortunately, even as he started moving, a second spear appeared, its tip glittering as it shot toward Xu Qing with just as much power as the first spear.

And yet, the deadly attack wasn’t over yet. There was more to come. In the blink of an eye, a third, fourth, and fifth spear appeared.... Ultimately, a total of nine heaven-shaking, earth-shattering spears appeared, all in different spots, and all of them closing in on Xu Qing with deadly force.

It seemed like the spears were about to pierce through him. However, Sir Westdevil clearly didn’t know much about Xu Qing. Perhaps it would be accurate to say that he did know a lot about Sir Blood Dust. But he was dealing with Xu Qing, not Sir Blood Dust.

The nine spears of this attack contained power similar to that of an Imperial Sovereign, and they were arranged in something like a sealing mark. Unfortunately... they didn’t seal sound.

The nine spears thrummed with destructive power, letting loose deafening rumbling sounds as they smashed together in the same spot.

However, Xu Qing had already disappeared, leaving behind only a fading shadow. His true form had merged into sound and vanished into thin air. When he reappeared, he was behind Sir Westdevil. Without the slightest pause, he thrust his hand out.

Unfortunately, Sir Westdevil had abundant experience in battle, and had lightning-fast reflexes. At almost the exact moment that Xu Qing launched his counter attack, Sir Westdevil also blurred into nothing.

Xu Qing’s palm struck nothing but air. He looked up.

Sir Westdevil appeared high above, looking down at Xu Qing with shining eyes.

“Well, isn’t this interesting,” he said, again lifting his hand and pointing at Xu Qing. The black sea of flames erupted, causing flames to shoot up into the sky. Within them, the souls of the human quivered as they turned into numerous spears.

There were well over 10,000 of them that flew up, like a reverse rain that was focused completely on Xu Qing. Even more terrifying was that as the spears shot through the air, they proliferated, splitting apart. Each individual spear became ten, until there were more than 100,000. They moved with shocking speed, and what was more, they didn’t emit any sound.

Although they weren’t as mighty as the previous attack, the sheer numbers involved made them far more capable of inflicting annihilation. This soundless attack was Sir Westdevil’s second move.

In the blink of an eye they were about to hit Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he considered what to do. In the end, he didn’t evade. Instead, energy and blood surged within him, and he closed his eyes. 100,000 spears shot toward him from all sides and slammed into him. Light flared. Natural laws shattered. Magical laws vanished like smoke in the wind.

Yet Xu Qing didn’t seem affected. In fact, when the spears hit him, they unleashed a force of annihilation that swept back onto themselves. The spears were destroyed by their own power! They simply couldn’t do anything to Xu Qing’s fleshly body defenses.

Sir Westdevil’s eyes narrowed. However, he didn’t seem surprised. After all, he had been told already that this person excelled in defenses. And as it turned out, he had made this attack for another reason. When the spears shattered, they caused more black flames to sweep out. And the gruish fire was now right next to Xu Qing’s fleshly body. Instead of burning him, they formed a host of small-scale flame vortexes that spun rapidly.

Seeing that, Sir Westdevil’s eyes flashed with killing intent.

“Now’s my chance.”

He shot down toward Xu Qing. As he closed in, he extended his right hand. The heaven-devil projection did the same. And then, the heaven-devil’s eyes shone with underworld light as he gave voice to a complicated enchantment. It spoke every word clearly, yet no one who heard those words could possibly understand them.

As the enchantment echoed out, the black flame vortexes spun faster and headed toward Xu Qing’s forehead. At the same time, any spears that hadn’t exploded yet began to do so. More black fire burned, and more flame vortexes formed.

All of them were converging on Xu Qing’s forehead. In the blink of an eye, they merged together to create one incredible vortex.

As the vortex spun over Xu Qing’s forehead, Sir Westdevil reached out with his right hand. Within his palm was a strand of his own soul! He was using a killing move! And this killing move wasn’t about annihilation!

Everything he had said and done up to this point was a smokescreen. They were deceptions to hide his true strategy.

Spirit substitution! Put precisely, he didn’t actually want to defeat Xu Qing. And the reason he had rushed tirelessly from the battlefield had nothing to do with matters of face for the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. He had come for the Netherflame Secret Magic! He wanted to use Xu Qing as a substitute to get that secret magic!

For most people, that would have been a very difficult thing. But when it came to his special devil-spirit rot-crushing authority, the reality was that annihilation was only a secondary manifestation of its power. That authority had another ability hidden deep within it. And it was the ability of spirit substitution.

It was like a forced transfer. The soul strand he had produced was the secret technique that could be used to force the transfer. That soul wouldn’t fall under the control of the target. Rather, it would instantly come back on its own. It was a heaven-devil transfer!

Unfortunately, there are always counterparts to everything. When one person plots against someone else, it’s entirely possible that the other person would be doing the same.

As the vortex spun over Xu Qing’s forehead, and Sir Westdevil reached out with a soul strand in his hand to make the transfer... Xu Qing’s eyes snapped open. They glowed with cold light!

The authority of Six Thieves Deceive Life erupted, filling the area. Instantly, Xu Qing could see threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures surrounding Six Thieves Deceive Life. They connected to him. And thus, the Sixth Thieves became a path. A path that led to the soul.

Within Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness, his soul stepped forward onto the road. It emerged from his forehead and directly faced the incoming right hand of Sir Westdevil!

Floating next to Xu Qing’s soul form was a black carving knife. It didn’t matter what transfer was going to happen, or what technique was being used. The carving knife slashed down. That slash caused the soul strand in Sir Westdevil’s right hand to emit a shriek of anguish as it was cut in half.

Xu Qing wasn’t finished. His soul bore the knife forward, charging toward Sir Westdevil and slashing into his sea of consciousness.

Sir Westdevil’s sea of consciousness was vast and filled with black fire. Seven major worlds orbited above the fire, and seated cross-legged beneath them was a heaven-devil with a long spear in its hands.

Upon spotting the heaven-devil, Xu Qing’s killing intent surged, and he rushed toward it with the knife.

The heaven-devil’s eyes opened and it rose to its feet. Then its spear surged with power as it stabbed it toward Xu Qing.

The knife and the spear clashed. As rumbling sounds echoed out, the knife remained unscathed. In contrast, the spear exploded. The heaven-devil fell back.

Xu Qing was about to pursue it when a sense of impending crisis filled his soul form. Behind the fleeing heaven-devil, he spotted what appeared to be an ancient and rusty bell. As it floated up, it pulsed with terrifying power.

The eyes of Xu Qing’s soul form flickered. Without any hesitation, he fell back. As he left Sir Westdevil’s sea of consciousness, returning to his body, a terrifying power erupted out.

Xu Qing and Sir Westdevil backed away from each other in midair until they were about 300 meters apart.

Sir Westdevil scowled. He still felt lingering fear from the danger he had just been in. Glaring at Xu Qing, he said, “You knew from the beginning what I was planning to do!”

Xu Qing’s face remained calm as he replied, “I didn’t know the exact details. But based on your words and actions, it wasn’t hard to guess that you weren’t actually trying to kill me.”

Sir Westdevil looked at him, his eyes glittering. Then he turned to leave.

Xu Qing lifted his hand, and the air vibrated. A tempest sprang up in front of Sir Westdevil, blocking his path.

Sir Westdevil stopped in place and looked back at Xu Qing with a grim expression. “I made my three moves. And I promised to spare your life if you survived. You’re making a mistake.” freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing shook his head. “I never promised to spare your life.”

And then he took a step forward. Killing intent surged.

As Xu Qing stepped forward, he unleashed every bit of his sound authority. Using that, he entered sound. That single step took him 300 meters so quickly it was like a minor teleportation.

Sir Westdevil had incredibly quick reflexes, and shot backward the moment Xu Qing spoke. Unfortunately, it was like Xu Qing had become part of space-time itself, as he instantly appeared right behind Sir Westdevil. There, his dao lineaments glittered, and the power of his authority erupted.

The might of erasure touched on everything, like an invisible hand preparing to wipe away anything it contacted. Combined with the deadly effects of the sound that he gathered, it created unsurpassably terrifying fluctuations that completely swept over Sir Westdevil. This was Xu Qing’s counterattack.

The attack landed, and rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth.

Sir Westdevil’s expression flickered as a tremor passed through him from head to toe. The first thing he sensed was the surrounding sound vanishing from his ears. It was as if it didn’t even exist. It had all been taken away and turned into an explosive weapon in the hands of Xu Qing.

As sound waves covered Sir Westdevil, blood sprayed out of his mouth, and it looked like his body was already starting to crumble. Even his heartbeat was like a blade slashing into him.

The mightiness of the authority of erasure turned into a blade that began to erase all traces of Sir Westdevil. Bits of his life force, traces of his karma, traces of his existence.... Sir Westdevil began to breathe heavily, and his heart was pounding from the feeling of deadly crisis building within him. Back when Xu Qing’s soul launched a deadly attack into his sea of consciousness, he had felt fear for the first time. This was the second time.

The command medallion the empress had given to Xu Qing was indeed astonishing. Unexpectedly, it was even capable of allowing Xu Qing to attack Sir Westdevil in this manner. The undetectable change to perceptions made it so that Xu Qing was very confident in attacking.

Unfortunately... Sir Westdevil was a top chosen, and he had abundant battle experience. Despite facing this attack from Xu Qing which placed him in immediate danger, he still managed to launch a counterattack.

As the sound authority erupted, and the power of erasure surged, Sir Westdevil unhesitatingly caused a black glow to flicker in his eyes. That black glow started out as a pinprick, but quickly filled his pupils as well as his sea of consciousness. The flames in his seven major worlds instantly went out.

The moment it happened... the heaven-devil behind him seemed to be resurrected. It lifted its head, its mouth twisted in a ferocious grin, and it took a step forward. In the shortest of moments, it fused with Sir Westdevil.

Sir Westdevil threw his head back and let loose a monstrous howl. Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth, all while an astonishing devil energy surged out of him with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. The power of sound authority was crushed. The authority of erasure was suddenly struggling.

Sir Westdevil also changed shape! He became an incarnation of a heaven-devil! He wore vicious pitch-black armor, and was hundreds of meters tall. His fingernails were so sharp they seemed like they could shred space-time itself. His hair was no longer bright red, but pitch black, and spread out so dramatically it could obscure the sky and block the sun. The black fire in the area burned with even greater intensity.

This was a divine ability of authority that Sir Westdevil rarely used. It was the Heaven-Devil Transformation! The reason he rarely used it was that there was a major flaw with this authority. The more Sir Westdevil used it, and the longer he used it, the more quickly he lost his sense of self. And unless he constantly improved his cultivation base, then ultimately he would be absorbed by the authority, and would become a mindless heaven-devil. Unfortunately, this moment of crisis meant that he couldn’t hold back.

After turning into a heaven-devil, he waved his hand, and his seven major worlds appeared in the open to block Xu Qing. Loud rumbling sounds echoed out as the worlds shifted to line up in a row.

A very gruish scene then played out. The seven worlds began to grow larger, causing the space between Xu Qing and Sir Westdevil to ripple and distort. And thus, despite the fact that neither party was backing up, the worlds stretched space so that they were extremely far apart.

The authority lineaments caused Xu Qing’s vigilance to increase dramatically. However, so did his killing intent. And thus, his hands flashed in a double-handed incantation gesture as he sent both godly authority and cultivator authority rushing toward Sir Westdevil.

Sir Westdevil in heaven-devil form looked out with abstruse, pitch-black eyes. Then he extended his massive right hand toward the huge spear stabbed into the earth. The spear thrummed as it flew out of the ground, shrank down, and landed in his hand. Then he stabbed it viciously toward Xu Qing.

A high-pitched piercing sound rang out as Xu Qing dodged. At the same time, he fought back with sound-seizing, once again using sound authority to perform a minor teleportation and gruishly appeared right next to Sir Westdevil.

Sir Westdevil scowled and quickly launched a counterattack. But Xu Qing just disappeared again, to reappear on the other side of Sir Westdevil.

And thus, he repeatedly used sound authority to teleport to different locations around Sir Westdevil. It didn’t matter that Sir Westdevil wasn’t making any sound. His blood was flowing, his heart was beating, and his life force was burning, which created an intangible sound of its own. And Xu Qing could control all of that. As a result, Sir Westdevil’s spear never managed to do anything to Xu Qing.

Sir Westdevil’s heart continued to sink. The longer he used the Heaven-Devil Transformation, the greater danger he was in. And this Sir Blood Dust had astonishing defenses as well as gruish escape magics. He was also very fast.

It took almost no time for Sir Westdevil to be in a very dangerous situation. Finally, determination flashed in his eyes. Lifting his right hand, he shoved it out, causing the spear to shoot up into the sky. At the same time, his hands flashed in a double-handed incantation gesture, and he shoved them out. Then he spoke five words.

“Seven Prisons Heaven-Devil World!”

Five mouthfuls of blood sprayed out, all while his body withered dramatically. This magic produced astounding mightiness. Rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth as all of the devil energy around him erupted, filling an area of 50,000 kilometers.

Xu Qing’s eyes hardened as he found himself surrounded by the devil energy. Simultaneously, Sir Westdevil’s first major world began to descend in illusory form. It slammed into the ground, creating a prison around Xu Qing.

Things weren’t over yet. Instantly, the second, third and fourth worlds followed suit.... All seven worlds fell down, overlapping to create a heaven-devil prison. It crushed down on anything and sealed everything.

Sir Westdevil was seated cross-legged on the very top of the heaven-devil prison. His devil energy was surging out, filling the prison, and causing heavenly lightning and earthly fire to fill the place. He was trying to assimilate Xu Qing.

Inside the heaven-devil world, flames raged, and lightning crashed.

Xu Qing’s expression was grim as he sensed what was happening and looked up toward the canopy of heaven. He could see Sir Westdevil on the outside. He could also sense that his opponent’s divine ability was causing him to wither and weaken. He knew that this was Sir Westdevil’s trump card.

Then, just as he was preparing to do something, his expression flickered as he sensed his candle tattoo stirring. The candle started madly sucking in the surrounding fire, and its aura of awakening rose up dramatically again.

Xu Qing frowned. Though he wasn’t sure what had caused this to happen, he knew that as long as he broke free very soon, he could deal with the situation. His eyes flickered with cold light, all while the carving knife manifestation of the godly authority of fate emerged from his forehead. He was planning to use the power of that carving knife to carve out an unavoidable death for his opponent!

Deathblade's Thoughts

This chapter is about 1,000 characters shorter than average.

Within that 50,000-kilometer area, black flames burned, the heat distorting everything as the fire made something like a sealing mark. The flattened lands also featured Sir Westdevil’s seven major worlds, which were organized atop each other to make a seven-layer prison.

With that blessing, Sir Westdevil was able to unleash the most powerful manifestation of his gruish authority. It was... the Seven Prisons Heaven-Devil World.

That world had a heaven that was the darkest black imaginable, and an earth that was boundlessly crimson. Heaven-devil fire raged, burning with utter madness as if to incinerate all prisoners within that world, destroying them in body and soul.

Sir Westdevil sat cross-legged outside of the heaven-devil world, his motions mirrored exactly by the illusory heaven-devil projection behind him. He was severely withered, and his aura was very weak. His Heaven-Devil Transformation had obviously required him to pay a heavy price, and it was the same with the Seven Prisons Heaven-Devil World.

However, he didn’t seem concerned about that. He was completely focused on assimilating Xu Qing. Xu Qing was so difficult to deal with that their clashes up to this point had been as effective as striking a wad of cotton.

Xu Qing had obviously sustained numerous blows that should have seriously injured him. But his gruish transformation ability and his perverse level of speed made it possible for him to appear at any spot at any time. If that were all there were to it, it might not have been a big deal. It wasn’t as if Sir Westdevil didn’t have defensive techniques. But Xu Qing’s strange melting ability was very pernicious. Every time they made contact with each other, Sir Westdevil found that his energy, lineaments, defenses, and life force were melting. Normally speaking, he wouldn’t have cared about that. But he couldn’t sustain his Heaven-Devil Transformation for very long, and as a result, this fight was becoming extremely frustrating.

The only upside was that his killing intent was constantly growing stronger. Therefore, he was holding nothing back. He was using all trump cards possible to negate his opponent’s advantage, and change the tide of battle to his favor. His devil energy rumbled as he constantly bolstered the heaven-devil world. At the same time, he sent the spear stabbing down into the world. As a result, the assimilating devil fire in the world grew more intense.

Within the heaven-devil world, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with mysterious light. He was currently ignoring how the red candle was devouring the devil fire. He was also ignoring how the candle’s aura of awakening was growing stronger. His current focus was on the carving knife formed from his godly authority of fate. This was his first time to actually use the power of the godly authority of fate. However, he had done a lot of research and also had been given advice by the empress. As a result, he had a good initial understanding of the godly authority.

Therefore, he took a deep breath and extended his right hand. The carving knife shivered, then shot toward Xu Qing and settled onto his hand. It glittered brightly, sending out majestic and astonishing fluctuations that caused all the surroundings to pulsate.

Being on the outside, Sir Westdevil was unable to see anything on the inside. Therefore, he kept his guard up. Gritting his teeth, he burned his own heart-blood to bolster the assimilation process.

As for Xu Qing, his expression was grave. His heart wasn’t beating, and his view of the world had become a monochrome made of black and white. The black was space, the white was time. Between the black and white were innumerable gray strands. They were the fate of all living beings.

When Xu Qing’s heart stopped beating, his emotions became outstandingly calm. There were no fluctuations whatsoever. It was as if all bits of human nature had completely disappeared from within him. The only thing left was godly nature. What was more, this was a godliness that contained no mercy whatsoever. Nor did it contain death. It only contained control over fate.

“Sir Westdevil,” called Xu Qing, his voice thrumming with the might of godly authority.

When his voice echoed out, Sir Westdevil shivered from head to toe. He had suddenly felt a profound sense of fear filling him, something that caused him to struggle merely to breathe.

Within the heaven-devil world, Xu Qing’s breathing caused the countless gray threads to all vanish, with the exception of one that remained behind in front of him. It undulated constantly, all while growing larger. Astonishingly, when it was completely unfurled, it showed Sir Westdevil’s past, present, and future.

The past was already sealed. The present was developing. The future was full of constants.

There were infinite images of Sir Westdevil’s future, all floating in front of Xu Qing. As Xu Qing well knew, they were all possibilities of what could happen.

Zi Qing could select one of those and pick it as the only possible future. But Xu Qing’s control of fate wasn’t about influenced constants. It was about creating variables. Therefore, he took his own will and put it into the carving knife, then sliced out a first stroke.

That stroke didn’t require any sort of innate artistic ability, as it didn’t matter if the final product resembled the original. The only relevant things were the thoughts and desires of the person doing the carving.

Xu Qing’s thought consisted of one concept.

This person must die.

The first carving stroke formed an image of Sir Westdevil dying. It was a miserable death in which he was decapitated and his body shriveled up. This was reaped karma.

Next, Xu Qing’s hand moved as he carved the second concept. This time, in order to lead to the reaped karma, he added the sown karma.

The head of the corpse is lopped off by The Emperor’s Sword!

The carving knife fell, and the image in front of Xu Qing showed The Emperor’s Sword beheading Sir Westdevil from behind. The moment the image took shape, Xu Qing shivered and his mind spun. He coughed up a massive mouthful of blood, and the entire heaven-devil world shook.

Something incredibly terrifying was coming. It was a transformation to fate!

That was because, before this moment, though Sir Westdevil’s countless future constants did contain versions of him dying, they weren’t all instances of him dying, and definitely none in which he was killed by The Emperor’s Sword.

Originally speaking, nothing like that existed. But now those images had appeared, and as they were sealed into Sir Westdevil’s fate threads, he gained an additional future. What was more, it was the only future that had anything to do with The Emperor’s Sword. That indicated that, as long as The Emperor’s Sword appeared in his presence, then Sir Westdevil’s future could not end with any other possibility.

This was the power of a god. This was godly authority!

Unfortunately, the price to pay was enormous. As the image was carved, Xu Qing’s five yin organs writhed, his soul filled with stinging pain, and blood sprayed out of his mouth. It wasn’t just one mouthful of blood. It was seven or eight successive mouthfuls.

His powerful fleshly body suddenly showed signs of withering. A sense of weakness filled the depths of his soul, and quickly spread into his sea of consciousness.

Then his Emperor’s Sword secret trove... suddenly erupted. The trove gate, which had already been opened, emitted raging sword energy. Within that secret trove, the emperor’s soul was fused with The Emperor’s Sword. And that sword had been powering up this entire time. As the sword energy rumbled, the actual sword trembled... and then shot forth.

It flew out of the trove gate, flew out of the sea of consciousness, pierced out of the inside of Xu Qing’s body and emerged into the open. In the blink of an eye, the heaven-devil world began to shake violently as The Emperor’s Sword shot upward, its power crushing everything. It was bolstered by the emperor’s soul, blessed by fate, and was able to conquer every obstacle!

This one sword... could pierce worlds! And it stabbed directly toward Sir Westdevil, who was still in his astonishing state of transformation.

Sir Westdevil’s mind reeled, and his flesh seemed to be screaming out because of the danger. Lunging backward, he held nothing back to defend himself.

The heaven-devil spear shot toward The Emperor’s Sword. When the two weapons clashed, the spear shattered!

The Emperor’s Sword pierced onward toward the terrified Sir Westdevil. With only one burst of momentum, it stabbed right toward his neck!

When Sir Westdevil realized the sword was about to plunge into his neck and kill him, he let loose a roar of defiance. All of a sudden, an ancient bell appeared, surrounding him and providing an obstacle to the sword.

RUMBLE!

Cracks spread out over the bell, but it didn’t explode! It actually blocked The Emperor’s Sword!

Xu Qing sat cross-legged in the heaven-devil world, blood constantly spraying out of his mouth. This was the price for dealing with fate! He had to bear the consequences of the fate he carved. What was more, once the path of fate was set, he had to suffer the backlash of any attempts by the target to fight against that fate.

If he could deal with that, then the fate would be completed. But if he couldn’t, that carved image of fate would fail. The carver had to pay an extremely heavy price.

At the moment, Xu Qing’s soul was weak, and cracks were already spreading out across his fleshly body. When it came to dealing with a chosen like Sir Westdevil, there was still a big disparity in battle prowess. Killing a person like this was going to be extremely difficult.

Up in midair, Sir Westdevil was breathing heavily as he stared at The Emperor’s Sword on the other side of the bell. However, after sensing that his ancient treasure had managed to resist the attack, the fear in his heart finally began to subside. And thus, his eyes turned cold.

“You’re not Sir Blood Dust!” he said. “That sword is not something that comes from my species. And this power... you’re stirring my fate! That’s the power of a god! Who are you really...?”

Sir Westdevil’s eyes glittered with understanding. And then a sense of wild joy rose within him as he realized that, if this person had a secret identity, it was highly likely that Lu Lingzi would also have another identity. This was something big. Furthermore, if he was wrong about that speculation, it wouldn’t really matter. But if he was right, then he would earn an incredible amount of battle credit!

Shivering slightly, he began to contemplate methods of getting away from this fight. At the same time he pulled out a jade slip to send a message to his Master. However, as he backed up and took out the jade slip... he suddenly saw something playing out that hadn’t previously existed in his fate.

From the moment he had gained enlightenment of his authority, the heaven-devil behind him had always moved in harmony with him, no matter what type of battle he had fought. But not now. It was the first time it had ever happened.

Instead, it looked down at Sir Westdevil, and there was greed in its eyes. Then it lunged toward him!

Sir Westdevil’s mind and heart were instantly thrown into chaos as he looked over his shoulder in incredulity. There wasn’t time for him to shout out, much less take evasive action. The suddenly traitorous heaven-devil slammed into him.

A howl of anguish erupted from Sir Westdevil’s mouth. He wanted to struggle free. He wanted to fight back. But he was powerless. This heaven-devil was almost the same as him, but stronger, and thus, none of his efforts amounted to anything. He could do nothing as the heaven-devil entered him and began attacking him wildly.

Down in the heaven-devil world, Xu Qing’s face was pale and he was getting very weak. His soul was listless. However, his eyes shone with merciless coldness. He was not surprised by any of this.

If Sir Westdevil’s gray fate threads could be magnified exponentially, it would be possible to see that the fate image Xu Qing had carved included the rebellion of the heaven-devil! That was because Xu Qing’s carving didn’t contain only two concepts. It contained a third! And in that third concept, the heaven-devil turned traitor!

Xu Qing was fully aware of the extent of his battle prowess, and knew that directly fighting a chosen like Sir Westdevil would be extremely difficult. However, just because he couldn’t kill someone didn’t mean that person couldn’t die.

Therefore, he had carved out that the true death fate of Sir Westdevil wasn’t because of The Emperor’s Sword, but rather, because his own heaven-devil revolted against him! It was a case of using four ounces to move a thousand catties.

That was why the first concept that he had carved wasn’t just a simple beheading. It was also a withering of his body, something akin to life force being sucked out. That reaping of karma was the result of two things. First was the beheading by The Emperor’s Sword, while the withering came from the heaven-devil rebellion.

That was why the second concept Xu Qing carved was: The head of the corpse is lopped off by The Emperor’s Sword!

What was beheaded was the corpse! That was because Xu Qing couldn’t sustain the fate of the Emperor’s Sword executing this opponent. However, he could sustain the instigation of the heaven-devil rebellion.

More blood sprayed out of Xu Qing’s mouth as, outside of the heaven-devil world, Sir Westdevil screamed, and his body rapidly withered. The heaven-devil was absorbing his life force.

That included the bell blocking The Emperor’s Sword. And then, since the sword had nothing opposing it, it slashed forth and beheaded the corpse of Sir Westdevil. It was... exactly the same as the first concept from Xu Qing’s carving!

“Sir Westdevil was not killed by me. He was killed by the heaven-devil.” Xu Qing rose to his feet as the heaven-devil world collapsed around him.

The 50,000 kilometers of black fire went out. The heaven-devil prison formed by the seven major worlds collapsed. The dome of heaven returned, the lands went back to normal. The mountains and rivers were there just as before.

Xu Qing stood on the level ground, his face pale and his soul weak. The ground before him, and the front of his garment, were both soaked in the blood that he had been coughing up constantly. In fact, the act of standing had caused a bit more blood to ooze out of his mouth and drip down to the ground.

He took a breath. This was the first time he had officially used the godly authority of fate. Considering that, it was also his first time getting a deeper understanding of the paramount godly authority. The more he understood it, the more he feared it. This godly authority was terrifying to the extreme. The price to use it... was similarly extreme.

It was clear that if he hadn’t come up with a third concept, then it wouldn’t have been possible for him to sustain the effort of carving Sir Westdevil’s fate. And in all likelihood, he would have ended up dead.

And even though he had used that third concept, and thus had been able to move a thousand catties with four ounces, he had still been forced to pay a huge price to transform Sir Westdevil’s fate and put him to death.

His soul was now very weak. His fleshly body was cracked and crumbling. His cultivation base power was running on fumes, and both his cultivator authority and godly authority were extremely dim.

This godly authority is not something I can use casually....

Taking a deep breath, he wiped away the blood from the ground, then turned to leave.

Sir Westdevil’s death was definitely going to cause some big waves, and sticking around would be dangerous. However, he had only taken a single step before he stopped and frowned grimly.

A flame wisp had appeared on the red candle on his back! It was already so intensely hot that everything in the area was rippling and distorting. The candle’s aura of awakening had surged, and it seemed to be taking advantage of the moment to ignite itself. If it fully ignited, Xu Qing wasn’t sure how much danger he would be in, but the sense of crisis in his heart was already significant.

That sense of crisis was like a sea of flames threatening to overwhelm him. As a result, Xu Qing couldn’t leave the area. The most important thing right now was to handle the red candle.

Therefore, he didn’t hesitate for an instant to temporarily ignore his injuries and tap into his authority of erasure, all while reaching out to Little Shadow as well. The authority shot toward the red candle, and Little Shadow trembled and followed.

In the middle of the candle, the flame wisp glittered.... It was just on the verge of igniting!

When Little Shadow and the authority arrived, they worked together to suppress the candle and extinguish it. Because the candle had absorbed the devil fire, it was now showing signs of waking up.

Thankfully, Xu Qing had worked quickly and efficiently to smash the heaven-devil world, and therefore, the candle had only been able to absorb a limited amount of the devil fire. And the combined effort of Little Shadow and the authority of erasure immediately proved effective.

It didn’t take long before the flame wisp vanished along with a defiant howl. The fluctuations of awakening had been thoroughly crushed.

Unfortunately, the sense of crisis didn’t disappear. It came partly from the dome of heaven, and partly from Sir Westdevil’s withered carcass. The former was outright terrifying, while the other brought lingering traces of fear. The carcass was so withered it was starting to smoke.

Then the smoke converged into the image of a heaven-devil. When it formed, it didn’t look at Xu Qing, but rather, at the horizon. Then it vanished, leaving behind only a few words.

“The fruit of Sir Westdevil had not ripened. But since you stirred his fate, I had no choice but to devour that fruit early. You need to make up for any karma going forward.... I hope that you can avoid the coming deadly trial. If you don’t die... then I’ll find you in the future.”

Normally, Xu Qing would have found such words to be very thought-provoking. But at the moment, he was far more focused on that sense of crisis coming from the dome of heaven. That crisis surpassed anything from this heaven-devil, and it also surpassed Sir Westdevil himself. In fact, it surpassed any enemy cultivator Xu Qing had ever faced.

To him, it felt like a god! And that was because this was the power of an Imperial Sovereign who could indeed fight against gods. This wasn’t an Imperial Sovereign who had just broken through, like Floating Fiend. Instead, this was someone who could truly be considered almighty within the Imperial Sovereign level.

Xu Qing’s soul was trembling, his mind was spinning, and his authority was in chaos. The sensation of crisis rose explosively within him, and the shadow of death seemed to overwhelm everything. He wanted to flee, but he couldn’t.

The sky pulsated as a massive mirror came into view. It was fully 500,000 kilometers in size, such that it was like heaven itself! It was circular and pitch black. And of course, everything it covered was cast into darkness.

Then... snowflakes started drifting out of the mirror, filling the darkness with snow. The snow was also black. There was no wind, but the snowflakes drifted about as if guided by natural and magical laws. It was as if the entire area had become a world of its own.

And Xu Qing was inside it. The heaven of that world was the black mirror, and it now seemed as if it was falling. Collapsing. It dropped an inch, and all of the mountains in that 500,000 kilometers blurred and vanished.

Then, the outline of all those mountains appeared within the mirror. They had been sucked into the nonexistent reality of the mirror.

Xu Qing shivered as cracks spread out across him, and a sensation of imminent death filled him. His eyes were already bloodshot, and he wanted to struggle, but couldn’t. All he could do was cough up mouthful after mouthful of blood. In fact, blood was seeping out of him all over, until it ran down like a river. In the end, he simply couldn’t stand up to this Imperial Sovereign.

When this Imperial Sovereign took action, Xu Qing’s godly authority and cultivator authority became meaningless.

The black mirror that was now the canopy of heaven dropped down by another inch. Within the 500,000-kilometer area, all of the rivers blurred and disappeared. Their outlines appeared in the mirror.

Next came the lands. All the lands in the 500,000-kilometer area rippled and disappeared.

And then, within the black mirror, something else appeared. It was... an outline of Xu Qing himself, slowly starting to form. Death had come. All it would take would be for the mirror to drop down another inch.

Xu Qing was shivering from head to toe, and he was soaked in blood. And yet, there was no despair in his eyes. Instead, there was a crazy look. He knew that he wasn’t a match for an Imperial Sovereign. Whether it was Floating Fiend or whatever cultivator he was dealing with now, it didn’t matter if he had some destined opportunity and a boost to his battle prowess. Imperial Sovereigns were not people he could harm. However... that didn’t mean he was out of options here.

Looking very crazy, he threw his head back and roared. And then, just as he was about to burst into motion, the black mirror... dropped down another inch. It seemed that something very dramatic was about to happen.

But then, a burly figure appeared out of thin air. He entered the world created by the black mirror, approached Xu Qing, and stood in front of him. He looked like a mountain himself, towering over the chaotic battlefield.

He was Lu Lingzi!

Of course, it was more accurate to say that it was Empress Summer Departure in the form of Lu Lingzi. The moment shē appeared in front of Xu Qing, shē blocked the tempest winds, blocked death, and dispelled all the pressure weighing down on him.

Xu Qing relaxed slightly. Now he didn’t have to put everything on the line. Clasping hands, he bowed. The empress looked up at the black mirror above. The passage of that gaze was like a grand army that could send fires raging and mountains crumbling into ruin. And that gaze... focused on the middle of the mirror.

It was a gaze full of power, and it caused the black mirror to tremble. It was a gaze of abstrusity, and it caused a pinpoint of light to appear within the black mirror.

That pinpoint of light was a sun in the night. The moment it appeared, boundless white light spread out everywhere, shattering the darkness with unstoppable momentum. It spread through the mirror. Where it went, the outlines of the mountains in the mirror vanished. The rivers and lakes and lands and even the blurry outline of Xu Qing were all wiped away.

The black mirror was turning white!
