When the outlines disappeared, everything in the 500,000-kilometer area reversed. Everything was returning. This was a confrontation between ‘Lu Lingzi’ and this unknown Imperial Sovereign. And the confrontation wasn’t over.

At about the same time as the mirror turned white, a cold harrumph echoed through the sky. The mirror shattered, and every bit of white turned back into black. And then a middle-aged man appeared. The shattered bits of the mirror converged in the dome of heaven.

It was... the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign of the western Devilbirds. He was none other than Sir Westdevil’s Master.

He hovered in the sky looking at the empress for a moment, then flicked his sleeve, causing endless amounts of black snow to appear.

The empress’ facial expression didn’t change as hēr forehead split open and a blood-red eye appeared. Instantly, the sky rippled as a large red sun rose behind the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign.

The empress coolly said, “Sir Blood Dust, as you know, my authority relates to wind. Do you know how the authority of wind manifests at a higher level?”

Xu Qing inhaled and shook his head.

The empress’ expression remained placid. “Air has weight. And so does wind. Watch.”

The empress reached a hand out and pushed it down.

Instantly, the red sun behind the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign blurred. Then, all of the air in the 500,000-kilometer area started converging there. In the blink of an eye, the effects spread beyond 500,000 kilometers to 5,000,000... and the movement created wind.

In the briefest of moments, a rumbling tempest formed. But the real deadly attack didn’t come from the wind, but rather... the weight of the air.

That weight all bore down on the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign, causing his expression to flicker. He was unable to resist and unable to flee. Under the consummate force of this authority, he immediately fell down toward the ground below. The ground quaked as he slammed into it, and there was suppressed, unable to free himself no matter how he struggled.

And then an even more shocking scene played out. The air converged on him, weighing down with such intensity that it broke open his defenses and entered his body, causing him to scream shrilly. Numerous wounds opened up, yet no blood flowed out. Instead, it went inward.

The pain was incredible.

Lu Lingzi was just that horrifyingly mighty. It was the first time that mightiness was being made manifest among the western Devilbirds!

The ground trembled with lingering aftershocks.

The seventeenth Imperial Sovereign’s struggles were so ineffective that he couldn’t even launch a counterattack. It was clear that this Imperial Sovereign’s understanding of his personal authority was far inferior to Lu Lingzi’s understanding.

That was especially true of the wounds. They were innumerable. All the air from the 5,000,000-kilometer area poured into him, seeping into every crevice of his fleshly body and soul, as if to completely fill them. When the process was complete, the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign would be destroyed in body and soul.

The dramatic scene was so shocking that, almost instantly, people started showing up to see what was going on. Some came as their true selves, others sent divine will. Some had grave expressions, others were shocked, and there were some who seemed thoughtful. And yet all of them were equally taken aback!

“It’s hard to believe this Lu Lingzi has achieved such a deep level of understanding about this authority!”

“No wonder Grand Emperor Devilbird is taking him seriously. And it’s also no surprise that the Lan Clan’s plot against him failed so spectacularly!”

“And then there’s that Sir Blood Dust.... He’s definitely not somebody to take lightly. And he clearly has more secrets besides having the Netherflame Secret Magic. It’s just too bad that Lu Lingzi covered for him during his fight with Sir Westdevil.”

“Yeah, but it’s very telling that the heaven-devil formed from Sir Westdevil’s authority just up and fled. It was probably some unknown method that caused the heaven-devil to turn traitor.”

“That heaven-devil authority might be shockingly deadly, and can give the enlightened astonishingly quick progress. But the side effects can be very difficult to deal with. You’re constantly dealing with the danger of the heaven-devil rebelling and turning on you.”

As various parties reeled in shock, Xu Qing came to his own conclusions about what was going on.

The empress’ arrival didn’t just lead to him sighing with relief. It also confirmed his previous speculation; the empress wanted to have the initiative here in the lands of the western Devilbirds. And the empress had seized that initiative just now, by taking all the air in a 5,000,000-kilometer area and directing it at the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign.

This was how to establish prestige. And it was also a way to send a message.

Xu Qing suddenly realized he’d come to a better understanding of how to handle important matters. It was very much in line with what he had learned from Master Seventh.

He looked over at the struggling seventeenth Imperial Sovereign. From the way the Imperial Sovereign’s face was distorted, Xu Qing could well imagine how terrifying it was to deal with that immense weight.

The empress’ face remained calm the entire time. And then, instead of outright killing him, shē waited until the very last moment before closing the blood-red eye on hēr forehead. Shē retracted the authority.

The moment that eye closed, the sun shē had summoned vanished. The air that was weighing down on the Imperial Sovereign was scattered by the wind.

Without that immense weight on him, the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign’s injuries quickly healed up. Then he blurred, vanished from the spot he occupied, and reappeared up in midair. There he looked at the empress, his expression complicated. He said nothing. He wasn’t the only one to react in such a way. The others who had come to watch the fight were equally silent. This demonstration of superiority, followed by clear humility, was what a truly powerful expert was like.

“Can you move?” the empress asked Xu Qing.

He quickly nodded.

“Then let’s go. We’re returning to the eastern Devilbirds.” The empress strode toward the horizon.

Xu Qing didn’t hesitate to fly up into the air and follow hēr.

And thus, the Imperial Sovereigns of the western Devilbirds looked on as the empress led Xu Qing away through the dome of heaven. Eventually, they disappeared over the horizon. No one attempted to block their path.

Sir Westdevil had apparently been forgotten. Dead was dead.

It was only the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign who looked over at Sir Westdevil’s corpse, which was a withered husk after having been attacked by the heaven-devil. Eventually, he sighed, cleared his thoughts, and left.

The trip to the west was over. The wind returned, blowing through the 5,000,000-kilometer area, and clearing the area of the gazes of all onlookers.

***

On the wing-like dao altar of the western Devilbirds, Grand Emperor Devilbird sat cross-legged looking at the scene play out. When it was all over, he retracted his gaze.

“How amusing,” he murmured. “Is shē really so confident I’ll let hēr do what shē wants?”

Cruel laughter rang out in response to his words. At the same time, a black figure wreathed in flames and chains appeared in midair. “Of course shē’s confident!”

Grand Emperor Devilbird looked up at the black-cloaked figure. A long moment passed, and then he laughed.

***

By now, the empress was nearing the border between the west and east. Xu Qing was following close behind. The empress hadn’t said anything during the journey, nor had Xu Qing. Thinking back to everything that happened in the west, he tried to come up with a more accurate theory about what was really going on.

After the empress arrived in the western Devilbird lands, Grand Emperor Devilbird issued orders that set the tone for what was to come. After that, most of the Imperial Sovereigns issued challenges.

Given the balance of power between the eastern and western Devilbirds, it’s not hard to figure out what’s going on. The Devilbirds from the two areas are at odds with each other.

That’s especially true considering the sensitive nature of Lu Lingzi’s status. He’s an apprentice of Grand Emperor Netherflame, and is also a consummate chosen among the eastern Devilbirds. He thwarted the Lan Clan’s plot, then accumulated enough bloodline power to become an Imperial Sovereign.

Then he did something really outstanding. He revealed the secret of Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities to everyone. Without shedding any blood, he united the Imperial Sovereigns of the eastern Devilbirds, and smoothly took over the power structures and resources of the Lan Clan.

During that time, he handed out numerous invitations to enter the secluded meditation facilities of Grand Emperor Netherflame, which secretly implied that he was actually plotting to kill certain people. That, in turn, broke down the barrier between the east and west, and ensured that the western Devilbirds could also get involved.

After analyzing all of this, Xu Qing was starting to realize why the western Devilbirds were acting in the way they were.

Lu Lingzi’s background, status, methods, and the fact that he was rising to prominence ensured that many in the Devilbird holy land were watching him now. However, there were some things that obviously weren’t so simple. That was why, after Grand Emperor Devilbird set the tone for things, the western Devilbirds had obviously been given an unstated mission to crush Lu Lingzi.

But the empress didn’t face that challenge head-on. Instead, I was sent to deliver challenges, which meant that shē kept the initiative.

Xu Qing could thus come to the conclusion that he had successfully accomplished his mission. That was why the empress had taken such forceful action when the seventeenth Imperial Sovereign showed up.

I guess the big question is whether or not Grand Emperor Devilbird saw through all of this. And if he did, does it mean that he had some reason for letting it all happen?

Xu Qing looked at the empress in front of him as he considered the matter. He had already come up with a possible answer to the question....

In that manner, time passed.

The empress was neither in a hurry nor moving slowly. As the afterglow of sunset shone onto the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain, the rogue cultivators there looked up at the two returning figures. As they bowed their heads in excitement and reverence, Xu Qing and the empress landed on the mountain.

Upon entering the grand hall, Xu Qing bowed, then hesitated briefly before telling the empress about the red candle tattoo.

The empress listened, then calmly said, “And here I thought you were going to keep hiding it. Turn around and remove your outer robe.”[1]

Xu Qing immediately removed his outer robe and turned his back to show the candle tattoo. After studying it in detail, the empress’ eyes glittered in surprise.

“That candle doesn’t come from Revered Ancient,” shē said in a cool voice. “It’s from an ancient organization in the Ninth Star Ring. I’ve never heard of it transferring onto the body of a cultivator. But I do know that, when ignited, it can incinerate souls. I could help you seal it. However, to you, this thing can be both a detriment and a blessing. It just depends on how you use it. Therefore, I’ll leave it up to you whether or not to seal it.”

With that, shē walked to the end of the hall and sat down cross-legged.

Xu Qing considered the matter as he put his clothes back on. For the time being, he wasn’t going to ask the empress to seal it. He would study it further before making a final decision. Clasping hands, he bowed, then turned to leave.

That was when the empress’ voice once again echoed out. “Don’t leave the Imperial Sovereign mountain. In five days, you’ll take a command medallion from me to the Immortal Skills Hall of the eastern Devilbirds.”

Xu Qing blinked a few times and suddenly found himself thinking about his Eldest Brother. He turned to look at the empress. “Your Majesty, the eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall is where—”

The empress snorted coldly. “They sent out a notice yesterday inviting all eastern Devilbird Imperial Sovereigns to send emissaries to witness their grand immortal adept ceremony.

“They also notified everyone that the apprentice of the former grand immortal adept, Yue Dong, was competing with the current grand elder to earn the title of grand immortal adept. However, Yue Dong was defeated and taken captive by the grand elder.

“In five days, the Immortal Skills Hall will hold their succession ceremony, and will take Yue Dong’s Six Thieves Deceive Life away. The ceremony has to be approved by all of the Imperial Sovereigns, which is why everyone was invited to bear witness.”

An odd expression appeared on Xu Qing’s face. Obviously... the empress knew who Yue Dong really was. However, when he heard that his Eldest Brother had been defeated and taken captive by the grand elder of the Immortal Skills Hall, it seemed to him... that it was probably all part of his Eldest Brother’s plan. He was all too familiar with his unreliable and crazy Eldest Brother.

“I want you to head over there and see how they plan to take away Yue Dong’s immortal skill,” the empress said.

“Yes, Your Majesty,” Xu Qing said loudly.

Upon seeing Xu Qing react in this way, the empress reached up and kneaded the bridge of hēr nose. Shē had been worried all along that unforeseen variables would pop up. That was why shē had tried to send Xu Qing and Erniu away, only for them to show up anyway. The only question now was which of them would cause more trouble.

“Generally speaking, the Imperial Sovereigns don’t interfere in the internal affairs of the Immortal Skills Hall. They’ll support whoever wins. Once you’re over there, do not cause a big scene. And tell your Elder Brother that High God Sunfire previously requested that he be sent to fight for the Firemoons in the war. I tactfully refused.”

Xu Qing could hear the veiled threat in hēr words. Quickly bowing, he bid farewell.

The empress shook hēr head as shē watched him leave. No wonder their Master sends them out instead of keeping them around....

Five days passed in a flash.

At dawn, Xu Qing flew off of the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain and headed at top speed toward the eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall.

He wasn’t feeling worried at all. In contrast, he was looking forward to what was coming.

1. If directly translated from Chinese, what the empress literally says is “take off your clothes.” However, she’s not asking him to strip naked, so I’m adding a bit of clarity here. Traditional types of ancient Chinese clothing for men would usually involve multiple layers of garments, including pants and one or two layers of robes. Of course there could be additional elements. If you’ve watched your fair share of kung fu and wuxia movies, you’ll know what I’m talking about. In movies, especially the older kung fu ones, the male characters will inevitably end up topless during fight scenes as their robe is either taken off or ripped off. Anyway, in this passage, the empress is obviously asking Xu Qing to take off the clothing covering his back. ☜

Xu Qing didn’t feel any reason to be worried about his Eldest Brother’s safety. In all the time he had known his Eldest Brother, he had never seen an instance in which Erniu suffered. It was always other people who did the suffering. Among his victims was a godly entity from the Forbidden Sea, the three soul fragments of the Ghost Emperor, and most impressive of all... Crimson Mother and even the broken face of Eminent Desolation. Erniu had bitten chunks out of all of them.

From Xu Qing’s perspective, it seemed completely impossible that his crazy Eldest Brother would somehow meet misfortune in one of the Immortal Skills Halls in the Devilbird holy land. After all, his Eldest Brother had gone to the Immortal Skills Hall on purpose, and before leaving, he had seemed solemnly confident.

What was more, Xu Qing was going as an emissary of the tenth Imperial Sovereign, to bear witness to the event and see what the fuss was all about. In the past, he was always going on big jobs with his Eldest Brother. This was his first chance to go watch things play out as a spectator.

That said, I should do my best to keep things from getting out of hand. Given what the empress had asked of him, he felt like it was his responsibility to make sure his Eldest Brother didn’t cause too much of a scene. But when he thought about how much his Eldest Brother tended to stir up trouble, he felt a bit less confident. I can at least try to convince him to keep a low profile.

Feeling a bit better, he sped on his way. About four hours later, as he flew over the horizon, he saw the city where he and his Eldest Brother had parted ways some time ago. The eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall was located about 500 kilometers north of that very city.

Xu Qing didn’t pause for a moment. He flew over the city, crossed those 500 kilometers, and arrived at a white lake! Very much like the western Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall, this hall was built on a lake. The difference was that one lake was black and the other was white. freewebnovel.com

This one was called Deceive Life Lake. In the middle of the lake was a palace that looked like a temple. It was pitch black and made of jade, making the contrast between it and the lake very striking.

The lake in western Devilbird lands had been full of immortal adepts seeking enlightenment. This one was different. Perhaps the place was emptier, or perhaps it was because of the ceremony that was about to take place. Either way, there were no immortal adepts seated in meditation. The place looked empty. The black Immortal Skills Hall itself looked to be in bad shape, and the damage didn’t look old. In fact, it looked like it had been inflicted recently.

Taking it all in, Xu Qing crossed the lake and stopped in midair above the Immortal Skills Hall. Keeping his hands clasped behind his back, he said, “Would the immortal adept in charge here please come out to see me immediately?”

His voice boomed like thunder, causing the air to ripple and distort, and sending waves rolling out over the lake.

Eight figures flew out from the Immortal Skills Hall and toward Xu Qing. The person in the lead was a middle-aged immortal adept. When he looked at Xu Qing, his pupils constricted, and he suddenly assumed a much more respectful posture. Stopping a few dozen meters away, he bowed deeply.

“Well met, Fellow Daoist Blood Dust. We offer respectful greetings. We were busy with other guests that had just arrived, and thus neglected to receive you promptly. Please don’t take offense, Fellow Daoist.”

The immortal adept seemed very sincere. As for the others gathered behind him, they had very serious looks on their faces as they ducked their heads and bowed.

The reason for their attitude was that Sir Blood Dust’s reputation had skyrocketed recently in the Devilbird holy land. News about his challenges to the western Devilbirds, and especially his fight with Sir Westdevil, had already spread far and wide. When you added in the fact that he was backed by the tenth Imperial Sovereign, it ensured that the struggling Immortal Skills Hall wouldn’t dare to be negligent when dealing with him.

Xu Qing kept his expression neutral as he nodded his head. When the middle-aged immortal adept saw that Xu Qing didn’t seem offended, he breathed an inner sigh of relief. He had heard about how ruthless Sir Blood Dust usually was, and how deadly his divine abilities were.

Keeping his guard up, he gestured and said, “Please, follow me inside, Fellow Daoist Blood Dust!”

However, that was when Xu Qing turned to look at the horizon.

Looking stunned, the middle-aged immortal adept looked in the same direction. Laughter rang out from that spot.

“Is that Fellow Daoist Blood Dust over there?” A burly man was approaching. He wore a long blue robe and had eyes that flashed like lightning. As he neared, he pulsed with the cultivation base fluctuations of a nine-world Smoldering God, which created massive pressure in the area.

The middle-aged immortal adept quickly bowed. “Greetings, Revered One!”

Xu Qing’s facial expression was the same as ever. Based on Sir Blood Dust’s memories, he knew that this person was the eldest son of the fifth Imperial Sovereign. His name was Lin Kun.[1]

However, Sir Blood Dust and Lin Kun never had much dealings, and Lin Kun had obviously not given him much thought. But things were clearly different now.

Xu Qing clasped hands and bowed slightly.

Lin Kun neared, laughing heartily. “There’s no need for such formality, Fellow Daoist Blood Dust. I heard all about your heroic actions among the western Devilbirds, and I was cheering you on the entire time!” It was hard to say how sincere Lin Kun was being. Both his facial expression and his wording seemed very cordial. “Now that I can lay eyes on you in person, I can tell you really are a hero!”

It was only natural that a person’s true intentions couldn’t be determined by just looking at their facial expression. As such, Xu Qing wouldn’t form a good opinion based on only a few words. He shook his head.

“It was all due to the protection of an Imperial Sovereign,” he said. “Your humble servant is a mere follower of an Imperial Sovereign. Granted, I earned some prestige. But if you had been in my shoes, Fellow Daoist Lin, you would probably have become even more famous.”

Lin Kun smiled even more broadly in response to Xu Qing’s sincerity. He then went on to say a few more things, hidden within which were some probing words.

Xu Qing had plenty of experience in this kind of thing. He engaged in conversation naturally, not making any mistakes, and even managing to cleverly praise Lin Kun. On the surface, at least, it seemed that the two of them were getting along very well. And thus, the middle-aged immortal adept led them into the Immortal Skills Hall.

On the way, Lin Kun looked at the damage that had been done to the Immortal Skills Hall. Smiling, he looked at Xu Qing.

“Brother Blood Dust, while you were over in western Devilbird lands, some big things happened here at the Immortal Skills Hall. The apprentice of the former grand immortal adept returned. Her name is Yue Dong. She wanted to take over as the new grand immortal adept. However, several of the famous elders opposed her, and the friction got really intense.

“Yue Dong has some serious skills, and is also very charismatic. Not only did she win over quite a few of the other immortal adepts, but also, she got outside help. She somehow managed to convince the young lord of the Yun Clan to help her kill some of the elders!

“Given how things were playing out, Yue Dong was on the track to victory. And if she won, she would have become the grand immortal adept. But at the most critical point of the fight, the grand elder came out of several years of secluded meditation. He immediately stepped in, stopped the fighting, arrested Yue Dong, and calmed everything down.”

As they walked along, Lin Kun made his explanation and also kept an eye on Xu Qing to gauge his reaction.

Upon hearing Yue Dong’s name, Xu Qing’s eyes turned cold.

Lin Kun smiled faintly. “Brother Blood Dust, I heard that you and Yue Dong hate each other. Maybe you won’t be able to strike the killing blow yourself, but at least you’ll be able to witness the end of her life. Hopefully that will ease some of your frustration.”

Xu Qing shook his head. “No. I hope she comes out on top. If she does, then I’ll have the chance to personally kill her. It doesn’t sit well with me to let others do things in my stead.”

Lin Kun nodded. He could sympathize with such sentiment, and in fact, if he were in Sir Blood Dust’s shoes, he would feel exactly the same. If he had an enemy he simply wasn’t strong enough to get revenge on, it wouldn’t be worth worrying about. But if he did have the means to get revenge, then doing it personally would be the best.

They continued to chat as the middle-aged immortal adept led them down a long corridor in the Immortal Skills Hall. Eventually, they reached a circular arena. It was magnificently constructed, being filled with carvings of ancient mutant beasts. It also had portraits of outstanding heroes who wielded immortal skills in the time of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity.

And in the middle of it all was a woman suspended in midair by means of six iron chains, arms and legs splayed so that she resembled the character 大. She was none other than Yue Dong. Her hair was disheveled, she was soaked with blood, and she wasn’t moving. She had so much blood on her it seemed like she probably didn’t have any left inside to bleed out. She looked like she hardly had any breath in her.

Arrayed around her were ten huge thrones. Each one was made from immortal jade, making them look like scintillating treasures, or like ten beautiful suns.

Six of the thrones were already occupied by cultivators. Some were men and some were women. Most shocking was that all of them were nine-world Smoldering Gods. They were all emissaries of Imperial Sovereign mountains.

When Xu Qing and Lin Kun entered, the six of them looked over. And they focused... on Xu Qing. Each individual knew what they were thinking, but no one else did. None would reveal any facial expression unless it was on purpose. Most looked calm, although some nodded at him.

Xu Qing reacted in kind. Then he and Lin Kun flew over to sit, each one of them on one of the thrones.

Xu Qing sat on the tenth throne. As he did, he looked at Yue Dong. The moment he did, he could tell that Erniu was fine. After all, he was well aware that Erniu had an endless supply of blood. How could he possibly bleed out?[2]

Is Eldest Brother deliberately trying to make the enemy think he’s weak? Or is he trying to gain leverage somehow? I guess it doesn’t matter. Presumably, he’ll wait until just the right moment to turn things around. The reason for all of this is definitely to make sure this grand elder is convinced that Eldest Brother can’t do anything to turn the situation around. I just wish I knew the details of the plan. I wonder what Eldest Brother is going to do next?

As Xu Qing was wrapped up in such thoughts, Yue Dong shivered slightly. It was as if she realized something was going on, and was trying to wake up. Unfortunately, her wounds were so severe that it wasn’t even possible for her to open her eyes.

Time ticked by. Eventually, the emissaries from the other two Imperial Sovereigns arrived and took their places.

Then the officiator emerged. He was an old man wearing a black robe, with long white hair. What was more, he was so withered he almost looked like a skeleton. Strangely, he was backed by projections that resembled himself as a middle-aged man, a young man, and a boy. His true form carried a huge magic staff, and he pulsed with terrifying fluctuations that reminded Xu Qing of the majesty of the sea. This old man was different from any other Smoldering God he had ever encountered. What was more, he also pulsed with fluctuations of immortal skills.

His arrival caused the entire arena to quiet down. Everyone, including Xu Qing, looked at him with serious expressions.

“In compliance with the ancient decrees,” he said in a hoarse voice, “when a new grand immortal adept appears, all the Imperial Sovereigns will come to bear witness. That is why you have been invited here today.”

With that, he raised his magic staff and pointed it at Yue Dong. “Yue Dong betrayed the dao of the immortal skills. Thus, I invited everyone here, not just to bear witness to the rise of a new grand immortal adept, but also, to watch as she is stripped of her Six Thieves immortal seal. I hereby request that the emissaries of the Imperial Sovereign mountains take out their command medallions. The immortal assimilation ceremony is about to begin!”

1. Lin Kun: Lin is #18 on the list of 100 common Chinese surnames. It also means “woods, forest.” Kun is one of the Eight Trigrams that symbolizes earth, and is generally associated with yin and feminine things. Madam Deathblade says that this is a “handsome and ordinary-sounding name.” ☜

2. I was initially inclined to render Yue Dong like this: ‘Yue Dong,’ considering that ‘she’ really isn’t Yue Dong at all. However, that quickly got too complicated. So going forward in this scene, I’ll just render the name as Yue Dong even though we all know she’s really Erniu. This is the same way I’ve been handling Lu Lingzi who is really the empress. ☜

In the eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall, the black-robed grand elder had a voice that sounded like metal scraping against rock. His voice seemed to overlap with itself, probably because as the old version of himself spoke, so did the middle-aged version behind him, as well as the young man and boy versions. It was a very gruish sight.

Clearly, though the grand elder didn’t carry the legacy of the immortal skill Six Thieves Deceive Life, whatever immortal skill he did possess was spectacular.

When his words finished echoing out into the arena, he swung his magic staff out into the air. Though it didn’t seem to strike anything, the sound of a tolling bell rang out. It was like a crack of thunder, and at the same time, seemed like the cry of countless living beings. It created a mountain-toppling, sea-draining momentum that distorted the air and blurred everything in the area.

In fact, it caused an enormous vortex to spring up. The vortex rotated, becoming like a black hole that led to parts unknown.

The emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains looked on intently. As for Xu Qing, his expression was the same as ever, but he was clearly intrigued. The other nine emissaries all seemed thoughtful in various ways, and were clearly seeing the grand elder in a new light.

“Emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains,” the old man said, “in compliance with the ancient agreement, please produce your command medallions and permit the Immortal Skills Hall to activate the Immortal-Refining Pill Cauldron!”

The emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains exchanged glances. Then the representative from the fifth Imperial Sovereign mountain waved his hand, sending a command medallion flying out to hover over his head, where it cast out dazzling light. The other emissaries followed suit.

The agreement between the Immortal Skills Hall and the Imperial Sovereign mountains was designed in such a way that the former was kept in check by the latter. And every time a new grand immortal adept was named, that person was required to gain the approval of all the mountains.

There were even more restrictions in place when it came to using the Immortal-Refining Pill Cauldron. It could only be activated by means of command medallions. After all, it was an extremely rare treasure that was one-of-a-kind in the Devilbird holy land. In the past, it represented the epitome of orthodox governance among the eastern Devilbirds. And even nowadays, when the east was in decline, it served as a deterrent to ensure the western Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall could never successfully make any moves.

Although there were technically limitations placed on the Immortal Skills Hall in the east, the reality was that the Imperial Sovereign mountains had never interfered in the hall’s internal affairs.

After the other Imperial Sovereign mountain emissaries took out their command medallions, Xu Qing considered the situation briefly before doing the same.

Ten command medallions appeared, casting out a dazzling sea of light that poured into the vortex below. As a result, the vortex began to shine with many colors and rumble loudly. Then, astonishing, something emerged from the vortex.

It started with a skull! There was no flesh on it. It was pure bone, and it pulsed with astonishing malevolence. Next came a lid that was some 300 meters wide. After that came the enormous body of a cauldron.

Ultimately, what came out of the vortex was a massive pill cauldron that was several hundred meters in size! Unexpectedly, it was pure white, as it was crafted from bone. It was covered with innumerable magical symbols, and it pulsed with a sensation of malice and ancient time.

When it was out in the open, it seemed to bring with it a wind from antiquity, along with a begrudging, maddened roar. Everyone looked at it in shock.

There were only a few people present who had seen the Immortal-Refining Pill Cauldron in years past. Everyone else had only heard the stories about it, and were only seeing it in person for the first time.

Xu Qing was looking very closely at it. And there was one part that he was most interested in. The skull. There was something about it that seemed... familiar! All of a sudden, a very preposterous thought occurred to Xu Qing. However, before he could explore it, one of the other Imperial Sovereign mountain emissaries spoke.

“Grand Elder, is this one of the six bone cauldrons crafted by Grand Emperor Immortal Skill, the original creator of the immortal skills?”

The grand elder nodded, his eyes shining. “Grand Emperor Immortal Skill was human, and chose to be forgotten by history, which is why no one knows his actual name. Not even we practitioners of immortal skills know much about him.

“However, we immortal adepts have not forgotten his accomplishments. This pill cauldron was crafted during the early years of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity’s conquest of Revered Ancient. At that time, Grand Emperor Immortal Skill slaughtered six megavillains and used their skulls to create six cauldrons!

“The skull you see here is the refined skull of one of those megavillains. As for the bones that make this cauldron, it’s impossible to say which species they came from. The megavillain does look human, but at the same time, doesn’t seem human.

“Based on the traditions of the Immortal Skills Hall, the megavillain had a towering cultivation base comparable to that of a Grand Emperor. What was more, this person was well-known for being incredibly crazy, and possessed a level of greed that made peoples’ hair stand up in anger.

“By taking advantage of the wartime situation in Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity’s time, this megavillain was able to infiltrate countless species and steal treasures from them. In his final heist, he attempted to steal Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity’s imperial crown, but failed. The enraged Dark Serenity sent Grand Emperor Immortal Skill after him.

“Eventually, Grand Emperor Immortal Skill set up an incredible spell formation designed to trap and kill the megavillain. Because his greed was imbued into the cauldron, it’s possible to instill that greed into an immortal skill by use of the cauldron.”

All of the emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains reacted with varying levels of surprise to the grand elder’s story. Although all of them had heard of or seen the cauldron before, this was their first time hearing about its background.

And then there was Xu Qing.... He already had a very strange feeling, and his previous speculation was now getting increasingly intense. And then his gaze shifted from the skull on the cauldron over to Yue Dong suspended in midair.

Don’t tell me that Eldest Brother... wants this cauldron?

As Xu Qing pondered that concept, the grand elder finished with his introduction of the cauldron and then threw his hands into the air.

“Having assumed the title of grand immortal adept, and with the command medallions of ten Imperial Sovereign mountains, I hereby activate this bone cauldron to refine the traitor Yue Dong into... a six thieves immortal pill!

“Cauldron: ignite!”

The huge bone cauldron immediately started vibrating. The white lake surrounding the Immortal Skills Hall started seething, and the water transformed into white fire. The fire then poured into the Immortal Skills Hall, filling the arena, and ultimately entering the bone cauldron. It hissed and popped as it burned. The grand elder’s eyes shone brightly as he pointed out with his magic staff.

“Cauldron: activate!” he shouted.

The lid of the cauldron rumbled loudly as it tipped to one side. Boundless fire then shot out of the cauldron and surrounded Yue Dong. The chains binding her couldn’t sustain the heat and began to melt. As a result, Yue Dong fell down into the flaming interior of the cauldron!

Xu Qing hesitated, but suppressed his impulse to take action. Instead, he would trust his Eldest Brother.

The grand elder strode forward to the cauldron, his black robe billowing around him. As everyone looked on, he took a deep breath, lifted his left hand, and then made a grasping gesture in the direction of the middle-aged version of himself behind him. The middle-aged figure collapsed into a mass of gore that swept into the grand elder’s hand.

“Fetch the Star-Shredding Wind from the starry sky and use it to catalyze the body!”

The wind he had just mentioned appeared, filled with a terrifying power that caused the gazes of all onlookers to harden. freewebnovel.com

The grand elder flicked his left hand, and the Star-Shredding Wind entered the cauldron. The cauldron rumbled loudly. Because the cauldron was open, everyone could see clearly that Yue Dong was inside. And when the Star-Shredding Wind hit her, it started shredding her flesh off of her. Next, the grand elder made a grasping gesture toward the younger version of himself, whose flesh crumbled into a black liquid.

“Fetch the Un-Withering Water from the darkness of hell to melt the soul!”

The black water rushed into the cauldron. When it hit Yue Dong, her expression distorted as if she were experiencing unimaginable pain. In fact, it was the pain of the soul melting.

Xu Qing’s expression flickered, but after looking closely at what was happening, he suppressed any urge to take action.

The grand elder’s ceremony continued. He had obviously prepared very thoroughly for this day. By using flesh from various stages of his immortal skill, he was creating his ‘immortal-refining’ materials. Next, the boy behind him shattered. It turned into a piercing howl.

“Fetch the Howl of Defiance from ancient antiquity to call to the immortal!”

The howl entered the cauldron.

Yue Dong shivered as threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures transformed from intangible to tangible.

The grand elder hefted his magic staff, and it crackled with lightning and thunder. In a flash, the staff shattered and turned into flesh and blood. That magic staff was actually formed from the flesh and blood of the grand elder’s immortal skill. Now that flesh and blood quivered as it shot into the cauldron.

“Fetch the Lightning of Eternity from primal-chaos to form the seal!”

Things weren’t over yet. There was one final step in the ceremony.

It was fire!

The ground quaked as eight scales flew out from the vortex in the cauldron. Each scale had glittering striations on it, and each one was a different color. When combined, they created an eight-colored glow. They included all of the seven ordinary colors, plus black! And those eight colors combined with the white fire from the lake made... a total of nine colors!

The nine-colored flame entered the cauldron and instantly began raging! It was Immortal-Seizing Flame, and stretching back to ancient times, it was the method the Immortal Skills Hall used to punish traitors. The grand elder’s ceremony consisted of wind, rain, thunder, lightning, and fire! Now that they were complete, he raised his right hand.

“Cauldron: combine!”

He was preparing to close the cauldron and begin the refining process.

Xu Qing watched all of this play out. And though at first he was fairly certain everything was going according to his Eldest Brother’s plan, he was now starting to waver. Everything seemed to be so real.

I can’t let the grand elder do anything more!

With that, Xu Qing prepared to act. Except... that was when something extremely dramatic happened!

Inside the nearly-closed cauldron, the only thing left of Yue Dong was the head. The eyes on that head, which had been closed the entire time so far, suddenly opened! And they shone with an incredibly crazy look.

“I’ve been waiting for this exact moment, you old codger!”

Yue Dong suddenly spat out a mouthful of blood. It wasn’t ‘her’ blood. Instead, it came from the grand elder. ‘She’ had acquired it secretly during their fight earlier.

As of now, the cauldron contained the middle-aged version of the grand elder, the young version, the boy version, as well as the flesh and blood from his staff. Now, with this mouthful of blood.... The cauldron contained five things connected closely to the grand elder.

And that conformed perfectly to Erniu’s secret magic!

The Grand Five Ox Essence-Tracing Grand Merciless Dao!

That secret magic was able to lock onto the target and drag them into Erniu’s presence.

A vortex appeared inside the cauldron, and it immediately exerted a massive gravitational force. At the same time, the skull that was part of the cauldron started glowing with a mysterious light. It was as if there was some sort of resonance bolstering it.

Outside of the cauldron, the grand elder’s face fell as the secret magic locked onto him and... he vanished! When he reappeared... he was inside the cauldron! And then the cauldron’s lid slammed shut.

All of the onlookers were shocked, and the nine emissaries from the other Imperial Sovereign mountains shot to their feet.
